
-----title
天门（竟陵） (出生地)

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=852')">835-852年</a>　居乡。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='826c241fc78346f485e62fdd2ab43000_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=861&endYear=861')">861年</a>　离别襄阳，回复州竟陵。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c115dcaa46c14eeba4c3d041a5573b42_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c115dcaa46c14eeba4c3d041a5573b42");'><span id='c115dcaa46c14eeba4c3d041a5573b42_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=863')">863年</a>，30岁</div><div id='c115dcaa46c14eeba4c3d041a5573b42' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=863')">863年5月</a>　在竟陵短暂停留，继又南下洞庭，吊屈悼贾，有文。<div id='poem_1376035' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376035' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376035?labeling=true' target='_blank'>悼贾</a><span class='authorDate'>（863年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1376035")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376035_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1376035'>余尝读贾谊新书。见其经济之学。大矣哉。真命世王佐之才也。自汉氏革嬴。高祖得于矢石。不暇延儒生。及为天子。制缺度弛。处华而夷。是时独有叔孙生能定朝仪。其制未悉。唯生草其书。欲以制屈诸侯。推定正朔。调革舆服。通流货币。天不佑汉。绛灌兴谤。竟枉其道。出傅湘沅。生自以不得志。哀屈平之放逐。及渡沅湘。沈文以吊之。故其辞曰。𣉽九州而相君兮。何必怀此故都。噫。余释生之意矣。当战国时。屈平不用于荆。则有齐赵秦魏矣。何不舍荆而相他国乎。余谓平虽遭靳尚子兰之谗。不忍舍同姓之邦。为他国之相。宜矣。然则生之见弃。又甚于平。当汉时。舍乎帝则为诸侯矣。如适诸侯。则新书之文。抑诸侯而尊天子。舍诸侯则胡越矣。则新书之文。灭胡越而崇中夏也。是以其心切。其愤深。其词隐而丽。其藻伤而雅。余悲生哀平之见弃。又生不能自用其道。呜乎。圣贤之文与道也。求知与用。苟不在一时。而在百世之后者乎。其生之哀平欤。余之悲生欤。吾之道也。废与用幸未可知。但不知百世之后。得其文而存之者。复何人也。咸通癸未中。南浮至沅湘。复沈文以悼之。其辞曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1376035_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376035'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376035'>粤<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1376035", 1376035, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>炎绪</span>之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1376035", 1376035, "Clauses/0/Comments/1")'>嫣绵</span>兮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1376035'>其国度之未彰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1376035'>天锡生以命理兮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1376035'>冀其道之益光。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1376035'>伟吴公之知贤兮。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1376035'>道其名于文皇。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1376035'>既敐以召之兮。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1376035'>遂位之于上庠。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1376035'>悯耋儒之惷愚兮。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1376035'>对天问之不臧。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1376035'>既群愚之让俊兮。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1376035'>驰其誉之煌煌。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1376035'>嗟大汉之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1376035", 1376035, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>丕绪</span>兮。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1376035'>虬其贤于污潢。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1376035'>上下溷而不分兮。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1376035'>议制削于骄王。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1376035'>杀僇棼而不制兮。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1376035'>曾不能以抑强。<div id='poem_sentence_19_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1376035'>念五德之更承兮。<div id='poem_sentence_22_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1376035'>论尵结而不纲。<div id='poem_sentence_23_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1376035'>乃秉臆以兴说兮。<div id='poem_sentence_24_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1376035'>数用五而色尚黄。<div id='poem_sentence_25_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1376035'>又诸侯以开国兮。<div id='poem_sentence_26_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1376035'>输其租于咸阳。<div id='poem_sentence_27_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1376035'>曾不得以抚民兮。<div id='poem_sentence_28_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1376035'>各驰化于所疆。<div id='poem_sentence_31_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1376035'>上既悦而欲大用兮。<div id='poem_sentence_32_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1376035'>遭绛灌于<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_34_1376035'>道既摈兮何明。<div id='poem_sentence_34_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1376035'>乃出傅于沅湘。<div id='poem_sentence_35_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1376035'>侼沅波之滃洫兮。<div id='poem_sentence_36_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1376035'>想怀沙之幽忧。<div id='poem_sentence_41_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_1376035'>䗤毒乎芳洲。<div id='poem_sentence_45_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1376035'>景黯沮以不明兮。<div id='poem_sentence_46_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_1376035'>若夫悼乎离骚。<div id='poem_sentence_47_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_1376035'>香依依兮杜若。<div id='poem_sentence_48_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1376035'>韵凄凄兮篻簩。<div id='poem_sentence_49_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_1376035'>山隐隐以扫空兮。<div id='poem_sentence_50_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1376035'>烟微微而淡秋。<div id='poem_sentence_51_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_1376035'>嗟吾不知所惑兮。<div id='poem_sentence_52_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_1376035'>泪懭恨以横流。<div id='poem_sentence_53_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_1376035'>当<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1376035", 1376035, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>抱愤</span>于渺藩兮。<div id='poem_sentence_54_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_1376035'>曾无足以少休。<div id='poem_sentence_55_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_1376035'>呜呼哀哉。<div id='poem_sentence_58_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_1376035'>世既不平领吾道以为非兮。<div id='poem_sentence_59_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_1376035'>吾复何依。<div id='poem_sentence_60_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_61_1376035'>蘋兰憔悴兮稂莠繁滋。<div id='poem_sentence_61_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_62_1376035'>麟凤匿迹兮枭獍腾威。<div id='poem_sentence_62_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1376035'>哲匠罢斧兮拙者搆之。<div id='poem_sentence_63_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_64_1376035'>离娄闭目兮瞽者扬眉。<div id='poem_sentence_64_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_1376035'>子都蒙袂兮敦洽骋姿。<div id='poem_sentence_65_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_66_1376035'>呜呼哀哉。<div id='poem_sentence_66_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_67_1376035'>亦先生之尤也。<div id='poem_sentence_67_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1376035'>眙其世之不可兮。<div id='poem_sentence_68_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_1376035'>何不解而去位。<div id='poem_sentence_69_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_70_1376035'>又垂万世之名兮。<div id='poem_sentence_70_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_71_1376035'>取舍在此。<div id='poem_sentence_71_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_1376035'>奚自谤于童羖兮。<div id='poem_sentence_72_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_73_1376035'>乃憪然而为累。<div id='poem_sentence_73_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_74_1376035'>盖伊尹三就五就之心兮。<div id='poem_sentence_74_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1376035'>冀其民之可治。<div id='poem_sentence_75_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_76_1376035'>奈悯悯以不悟兮。<div id='poem_sentence_76_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_77_1376035'>又被之以非议。<div id='poem_sentence_77_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_78_1376035'>幸一人之再觉兮。<div id='poem_sentence_78_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_79_1376035'>答受之奥义。<div id='poem_sentence_79_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_80_1376035'>既孱王以堕驾兮。<div id='poem_sentence_80_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1376035'>乃冤恸而已矣。<div id='poem_sentence_81_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_82_1376035'>讯曰。<div id='poem_sentence_82_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_83_1376035'>君不明矣莫我知。<div id='poem_sentence_83_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_84_1376035'>幽都寂兮和涕归。<div id='poem_sentence_84_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_85_1376035'>文悬日月兮俟后圣用之。<div id='poem_sentence_85_1376035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_86_1376035'>大故忽兮其何足悲。</div><div id='poem_sentence_86_1376035_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
襄阳

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=858&endYear=858')">858年</a>　入徐商襄州幕，皮日休或因“试艺精专”而为徐商所赏，招其入幕。<br /><a href="javascript: href='/Writing/1375962?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酒箴</a><span class='authorDate'>（859年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375962")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1375962_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1375962'>皮子性嗜酒。虽行止穷泰。非酒不能适。居襄阳之鹿门山。以山税之馀。继日而酿。终年荒醉。自戏曰醉士。居襄阳之洞湖。以舶䑿载醇酎一甔。往来湖上。遇兴将酌。因自谐曰醉民。于戏。吾性至荒。而嗜于此。其亦为圣哲之罪人也。又自戏曰醉士。自谐曰醉民。将天地至广。不能容醉士醉民哉。又何必厕丝竹之筵。粉黛之坐也。襄阳元侯。闻醉士醉民之称。订皮子曰。子耽饮之性。于喧静岂异耶。皮子曰。酒之道。岂止于充口腹乐悲欢而已哉。甚则化上为淫溺。化下为酗祸。是以圣人节之以酬酢。谕之以诰训。然尚有上为淫溺所化。化为亡国。下为酗祸所化。化为杀身。且不见前世之饮祸耶。路酆舒有五罪。其一嗜酒。为晋所杀。庆封易内而耽饮。则国朝迁。郑伯有窟室而耽饮。终奔于驷氏之甲。栾高嗜酒而信内。卒败于陈鲍氏。卫侯饮于籍圃。卒为大夫所恶。呜乎。吾不贤者。性实嗜酒。尚惧为酆舒之僇。过此吾不为也。又焉能俾喧为静乎。俾静为喧乎。不为静中淫溺乎。不为酗祸之波乎。既淫溺酗祸作于心。得不为庆封乎。郑伯有乎。栾高乎。卫侯乎。盖中性不能自节。因箴以自符。箴曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1375962_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375962'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375962'>酒之所乐，乐其全真。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1375962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1375962'>宁能我醉，不醉于人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1375962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1375962'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1375962_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=859&endYear=859')">859年</a>　入徐商襄州幕，三月中下旬，皮日休有《襄州春游》诗。<div id='poem_15567' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15567' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15567?labeling=true' target='_blank'>襄州春游</a><span class='authorDate'>（859年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15567")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_15567_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_15567'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1262, "poem_allusion_15567")'>猖狂似祢衡</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_15567_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15567'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15567'>信马腾腾触处行，春风相引与诗情。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15567'>等闲遇事成<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_15567", 15567, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>歌咏</span>，取次冲筵隐姓名。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15567'>映柳<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作竹）</span>认人多错误，透花窥鸟最分明。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15567'>岑牟单绞何曾著，莫道<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1262, "poem_sentence_3_15567")'>猖狂似祢衡</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15567'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15567_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=859&endYear=859')">859年</a>　入徐商襄州幕，应邑人刘永之邀，作《刘枣强碑》<div id='poem_1376078' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376078' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376078?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刘枣强碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（859年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1376078")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376078_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376078'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376078'>歌诗之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376078_comment'></div>荡来久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376078_comment'></div>大抵丧于南朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376078_comment'></div>坏于陈叔宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376078_comment'></div>然今之业是者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376078_comment'></div>苟不能求古于建安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376078_comment'></div>即江左矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376078_comment'></div>苟不能求丽于江左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376078_comment'></div>即南朝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376078_comment'></div>或过为艳伤丽病者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376078_comment'></div>即南朝之罪人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376078_comment'></div>吾唐来有是业者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376078_comment'></div>言出天地外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376078_comment'></div>思出鬼神表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376078_comment'></div>读之则神驰八极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376078_comment'></div>测之则心怀四溟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376078_comment'></div>磊磊落落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376078_comment'></div>直非世间语者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376078_comment'></div>有李太白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376078_comment'></div>百岁有是业者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376078_comment'></div>彫金篆玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376078_comment'></div>牢奇笼怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376078_comment'></div>百锻为字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376078_comment'></div>千练成句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376078_comment'></div>虽不追躅太白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376078_comment'></div>亦后来之佳作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376078_comment'></div>有与李贺同时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376078_comment'></div>有刘枣强焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376078_comment'></div>先生姓刘氏名言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376078_comment'></div>史不详其乡里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376078_comment'></div>所有歌诗千首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376078_comment'></div>其美丽恢赡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376078_comment'></div>自贺外世莫得比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376078_comment'></div>王武俊之节制镇冀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376078_comment'></div>先生造之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376078_comment'></div>武俊性<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1376078", 1376078, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>雄健</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376078_comment'></div>颇好词艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376078_comment'></div>一见先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376078_comment'></div>遂见异敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376078_comment'></div>将署之宾位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376078_comment'></div>先生辞免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376078_comment'></div>武俊善骑射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376078_comment'></div>载先生以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1376078", 1376078, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>贰乘</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376078_comment'></div>逞其艺如野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376078_comment'></div>武俊先骑惊双鸭起于蒲稗间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376078_comment'></div>武俊控弦不再发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376078_comment'></div>双鸭联毙于地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376078_comment'></div>武俊欢甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376078_comment'></div>命先生曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376078_comment'></div>某之伎如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376078_comment'></div>先生之词如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376078_comment'></div>可谓文武之会矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376078_comment'></div>何不出一言以赞邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376078_comment'></div>先生由是马上草射鸭歌以示武俊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376078_comment'></div>议者以为祢正平鹦鹉赋之类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376078_comment'></div>武俊益重先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376078_comment'></div>由是奏请官先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376078_comment'></div>诏授枣强县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376078_comment'></div>先生辞疾不就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376078_comment'></div>世重之曰刘枣强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376078_comment'></div>亦如范莱芜之类焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376078_comment'></div>故相国陇西公夷简之节度汉南也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376078_comment'></div>少与先生游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376078_comment'></div>且思相见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376078_comment'></div>命列将以襄之髹器千事赂武俊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376078_comment'></div>以请先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376078_comment'></div>武俊许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376078_comment'></div>先生由是为汉南相府宾冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376078_comment'></div>陇西公日与之为笔宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376078_comment'></div>其献酬之歌诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376078_comment'></div>大播于当时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376078_comment'></div>陇西公从事或曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376078_comment'></div>以某下走之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376078_comment'></div>诚不足污辱<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_73_1376078", 1376078, "Clauses/73/Comments/0")'>重地</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376078_comment'></div>刘枣强至重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376078_comment'></div>必以公宾刘于幕吏之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376078_comment'></div>何抑之如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376078_comment'></div>公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376078_comment'></div>愚非惜幕间一足地不容刘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376078_comment'></div>然视其状有不足称者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376078_comment'></div>诸公视某与刘分岂有间然哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376078_comment'></div>反为之惜其寿尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376078_comment'></div>后不得已问先生所欲为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376078_comment'></div>先生曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376078_comment'></div>司功椽甚閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376078_comment'></div>或可承阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376078_comment'></div>相国由是椽之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376078_comment'></div>虽居官曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376078_comment'></div>宴见与从事仪埒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376078_comment'></div>后从事又曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376078_comment'></div>刘枣强纵不容在宾署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376078_comment'></div>承乏于掾曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376078_comment'></div>诎矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376078_comment'></div>奚不疏整其秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376078_comment'></div>相国不得已而表奏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376078_comment'></div>诏下之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376078_comment'></div>先生不恙而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1376078_comment'></div>相国哀之恸曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1376078_comment'></div>果然止椽曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1376078_comment'></div>然吾爱客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1376078_comment'></div>葬之有加等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376078_comment'></div>坟去襄阳郭五里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376078_comment'></div>曰柳子关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1376078_comment'></div>后先生数十岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1376078_comment'></div>日休始以鄙文称于襄阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1376078_comment'></div>襄阳邑人刘永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1376078_comment'></div>高士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1376078_comment'></div>尝述先生之道业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1376078_comment'></div>常咏先生之歌诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1376078_comment'></div>且叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1376078_comment'></div>襄之人只知有孟浩然墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1376078_comment'></div>不知有先生墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1376078_comment'></div>恐百岁之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1376078_comment'></div>埋灭而不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1376078_comment'></div>与荆棘凡骨溷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1376078_comment'></div>吾子之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1376078_comment'></div>吾当刊焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1376078_comment'></div>日休曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1376078_comment'></div>存既摭实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1376078_comment'></div>录之何愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1376078_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1376078_comment'></div>先生之官卑不称其德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1376078_comment'></div>宜加私谥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1376078_comment'></div>然枣强之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1376078_comment'></div>世已美矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1376078_comment'></div>故不加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1376078_comment'></div>是为刘枣强碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1376078_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1376078_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_128_1376078'>巳夫先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1376078_comment'></div>禄不厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1376078_comment'></div>彼苍不诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1376078_comment'></div>位既过于赵壹兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1376078_comment'></div>才又逾于祢衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1376078_comment'></div>既当时之有道兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1376078_comment'></div>非殁世而无名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1376078_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1376078_comment'></div>襄阳之西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1376078_comment'></div>坟高三尺而不树者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1376078_comment'></div>其先生之故茔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_138_1376078_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=860&endYear=860')">860年</a>　襄阳隐读，与史拱山人游。作品：史处士。<div id='poem_15334' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15334' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15334?labeling=true' target='_blank'>史处士</a><span class='authorDate'>（860年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15334")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_15334_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15334'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15334'>山期须早赴，世累莫迟留。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15334'>忽遇狂风起，闲心不自由。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15334'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_15334_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=860&endYear=860')">860年</a>　襄阳隐读，与从弟皮崇相聚，皮日休有诗相送。作品：送从弟归复州。<div id='poem_15497' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15497' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15497?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送从弟皮<span class='inlineComment2'>（一本无此字）</span>崇归复州</a><span class='authorDate'>（860年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15497")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_15497_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15497'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15497'>羡尔优游正少年，竟陵烟<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作风）</span>月似吴天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15497'>车螯近岸无妨<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作劳）</span>取，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_15497", 15497, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>舴艋</span>随风不费牵。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15497'>处处路傍千顷稻，家家门外一渠莲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15497'>慇勤莫笑襄阳住，为爱南溪<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作塘）</span>缩项鳊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15497'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15497_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=860&endYear=860')">860年</a>　襄阳隐读，邓州刺史某闻皮日休之名，礼聘之，不应，并作《食箴》<div id='poem_1375963' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375963' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375963?labeling=true' target='_blank'>食箴</a><span class='authorDate'>（860年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375963")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375963_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1375963'>皮子少且贱。至于食。自甘粢粝而已。未尝食于乡里。食于亲戚。食于州鄙。有邓邑大夫。向皮子之名。曾未相贽。具厚羞以宾之。皮子辞。大夫订之曰。子自甘粢粝则可矣。于乡里亲戚州鄙何有。皮子曰。一杯之食至鲜矣。苟专其味。必不能自抑。既不能自抑。日须丰其羞。既日须丰其羞。则贫也不能无不足。因是妄求苟欲之心生。穷贪极嗜之名生。且大夫不见前世之味祸乎。故羊斟不及。华元受其谋。鼋羹不均。子家肆其祸。熊蹯不熟。杀宰夫而赵盾弑。双鸡易鹜。馈子雅而庆舍死。呜乎。吾不仁者乎。诚赖其用。所欲不可求。所嗜不可得。方自甘粢粝而已。使我生于钟鼎之家。</div><div id='poem_preface_1375963_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375963'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375963'>膏梁之门。日纵异嗜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375963_comment'></div>年成奇欲。未必不为御者之奔华元也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375963_comment'></div>子家之伐灵公也。晋灵之杀宰夫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375963_comment'></div>卢蒲癸之杀庆舍也。此犹之禽兽欲争食而死者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375963_comment'></div>故食于天子者则死其天下。食于诸侯者则死其国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375963_comment'></div>食于大夫者则死其邑。食于士者则死其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375963_comment'></div>又焉能以乡里亲戚州鄙为让乎。大夫曰善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375963_comment'></div>自惟食之性不能自节。亦犹酒之性也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375963_comment'></div>复箴以自符。箴曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375963_comment'></div>宁能我食。不食于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375963_comment'></div>复食于人。是食其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375963_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1375963_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=860&endYear=860')">860年</a>　襄阳隐读，《六箴》或作于此时。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=860&endYear=860')">860年</a>　襄阳隐读，《七爱》或作于此时。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=860&endYear=860')">860年</a>　襄阳隐读，《鹿门隐书》或作于此时。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=861&endYear=861')">861年</a>　秋初，江西观察使裴寅任满回京，路出襄阳，皮日休干谒之，并陪襄州延庆寺，献诗。作品：陪江西裴公游襄州延庆寺。<div id='poem_15522' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15522' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15522?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陪江西裴公游襄州延庆寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（861年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15522")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_15522_comment'></div><div onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_15522", 15522, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>后乘</span>载诗人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15522_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_15522", 15522, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>不妨</span>犹有草茅臣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15522_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15494_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15494'>儿童不许惊幽鸟，药草须教上假山。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15494_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
洛阳
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=857&endYear=857')">857年</a>　冬十月，或赴洛阳集试。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7b88718e1884404cb93113b8c83f5867_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7b88718e1884404cb93113b8c83f5867");'><span id='7b88718e1884404cb93113b8c83f5867_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=863')">863年</a>，30岁</div><div id='7b88718e1884404cb93113b8c83f5867' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=863')">863年</a>　科举落第，献书有司，请以《孟子》为学科，视同明经。作品：请孟子为学科书。<div id='poem_1375934' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375934' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375934?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请孟子为学科书</a><span class='authorDate'>（863年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375934")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375934_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375934'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375934'>臣闻圣人之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375934_comment'></div>不过乎经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375934_comment'></div>经之降者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375934_comment'></div>不过乎史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375934_comment'></div>史之降者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375934_comment'></div>不过乎子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375934_comment'></div>子不异乎道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375934_comment'></div>孟子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375934_comment'></div>舍是子者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375934_comment'></div>必戾乎经史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375934_comment'></div>又率于子者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375934_comment'></div>则圣人之盗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375934_comment'></div>夫孟子之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375934_comment'></div>粲若经传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375934_comment'></div>天惜其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375934_comment'></div>不烬于秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375934_comment'></div>自汉氏得其书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375934_comment'></div>常置博士以专其学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375934_comment'></div>故其文继乎六艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375934_comment'></div>光乎百氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375934_comment'></div>真圣人之微旨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375934_comment'></div>若然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375934_comment'></div>何其道奕奕于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375934_comment'></div>而其书没没于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375934_comment'></div>得非道拘乎正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375934_comment'></div>文极乎奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375934_comment'></div>有好邪者惮正而不举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375934_comment'></div>嗜浅者鄙奥而无称耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375934_comment'></div>盖仲尼爱文王嗜昌歜以取味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375934_comment'></div>后之人将爱仲尼者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375934_comment'></div>其嗜在孟子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375934_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375934_comment'></div>古之士以汤武为逆取者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375934_comment'></div>其不读孟子乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375934_comment'></div>以杨墨为达智者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375934_comment'></div>其不读孟子乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375934_comment'></div>由是观之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1375934_comment'></div>孟子之功利于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1375934_comment'></div>亦不轻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1375934_comment'></div>今有司除茂才明经外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1375934_comment'></div>其次有熟庄周列子书者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1375934_comment'></div>亦登于科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1375934_comment'></div>其诱善也虽深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1375934_comment'></div>而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1375934", 1375934, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>悬科</span>也未正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1375934_comment'></div>夫庄列之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1375934_comment'></div>荒唐之文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1375934_comment'></div>读之可以为方外之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1375934_comment'></div>习之可以为鸿荒之民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1375934_comment'></div>安有能汲汲以救时补教为志哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1375934_comment'></div>伏请命有司去庄列之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1375934_comment'></div>以孟子为主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1375934_comment'></div>有能精通其义者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1375934_comment'></div>其科选视明经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1375934_comment'></div>苟若是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1375934_comment'></div>不谢汉之博士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1375934_comment'></div>既遂之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1375934_comment'></div>如儒道不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1375934_comment'></div>圣化无补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1375934_comment'></div>则可刑其言者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1375934_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=863')">863年3月</a>　三月寒食日，作《洛中寒食二首》<div id='poem_15490' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15490' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15490?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洛中寒食二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（863年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15490")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_15490_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15490'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15490'>千门万户掩斜晖，绣幰金衔晚未归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15490'>击鞠王孙如锦地，斗鸡公子似花衣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15490'>嵩云静对行台起，洛鸟闲穿上苑飞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15490'>唯有路傍无意者，献书未纳问淮肥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15490'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15490_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15491' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15491' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15491?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（863年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_15491_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15491'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15491'>远近垂杨映钿车，天津桥影压神霞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15491_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15491'>弄春公子正回首，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_15491", 15491, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>趁节</span>行人不到家。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15491_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15491'>洛水万年<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_15491", 15491, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>云母竹</span>，汉陵千载野棠花。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15491_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15491'>欲知豪贵堪愁处，请看邙山晚照斜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15491_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15491'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15491_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=863')">863年3月</a>　三月寒食日，又作《河桥赋》<div id='poem_1375928' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375928' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375928?labeling=true' target='_blank'>河桥赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（863年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375928")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375928_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1375928'>咸通癸巳岁。日休游河桥。观桥之利。不楫而济。美其事。著河桥赋。其辞曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1375928_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375928'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375928'>西荒之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375928_comment'></div>有昆崙山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375928_comment'></div>帝都之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375928_comment'></div>丰隆在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375928_comment'></div>其表无际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375928_comment'></div>其高破天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375928_comment'></div>河汉极北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375928_comment'></div>昭回相连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375928_comment'></div>分其坎德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375928_comment'></div>遂有河源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375928_comment'></div>其出绵绵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375928_comment'></div>其流涓涓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375928_comment'></div>如带是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375928_comment'></div>滥觞信然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375928_comment'></div>始礐石以作注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375928_comment'></div>终裂地以成川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375928_comment'></div>迨乎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1375928", 1375928, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>放勋</span>之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375928_comment'></div>重华之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375928_comment'></div>其水怀山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375928_comment'></div>其波浸天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375928_comment'></div>鳌怒则蹴翻五岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375928_comment'></div>鲸激则掉破百川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375928_comment'></div>迅澓欻而似曝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375928_comment'></div>涌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1375928", 1375928, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>湍濆</span>而若煎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375928_comment'></div>渍地轴以摧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375928_comment'></div>烂天轮而缺然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375928_comment'></div>草木则尾闾之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375928_comment'></div>日月则沃焦之巅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375928_comment'></div>人民死而为介。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375928_comment'></div>裸虫化而为蠙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375928_comment'></div>有桑不绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375928_comment'></div>有麻不田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375928_comment'></div>此则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1375928", 1375928, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>乘垲</span>望万里之渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375928_comment'></div>且夫天地之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375928_comment'></div>有河生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375928_comment'></div>则盘石之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375928_comment'></div>不能导而使归海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1375928_comment'></div>朴父之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1375928_comment'></div>不能疏而使为川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1375928_comment'></div>岂非元命未降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1375928_comment'></div>抑自上元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1375928_comment'></div>大圣未出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1375928_comment'></div>大功未宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1375928_comment'></div>天之作矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1375928_comment'></div>抑有由焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1375928_comment'></div>于是尧之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1375928_comment'></div>恻然惘然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1375928_comment'></div>咨其四岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1375928_comment'></div>举尔所贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1375928_comment'></div>天之元命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1375928_comment'></div>不自于鲧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1375928_comment'></div>鲧虽作矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1375928_comment'></div>其功不全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1375928_comment'></div>果殛于山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1375928_comment'></div>其罪昭然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1375928_comment'></div>天之元命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1375928_comment'></div>降而自禹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1375928_comment'></div>禹既作矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1375928_comment'></div>其功如天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1375928_comment'></div>于是禹之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1375928_comment'></div>忧然劳然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1375928_comment'></div>股既无胈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1375928_comment'></div>过不入门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1375928_comment'></div>以已为下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1375928_comment'></div>以物为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1375928_comment'></div>既乘橇以即檋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1375928_comment'></div>又随山而浚川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1375928_comment'></div>导自积石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1375928_comment'></div>至于龙门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1375928_comment'></div>裂岝𡺀以风响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1375928_comment'></div>斩崭岩而昼昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1375928_comment'></div>破灵怪窟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1375928_comment'></div>断天地根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1375928_comment'></div>分其注使不可溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1375928_comment'></div>修其流使不可吞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1375928_comment'></div>然后千岩万壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1375928_comment'></div>雷吼电奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1375928_comment'></div>抉逆流而并泻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1375928_comment'></div>入渤海以犹浑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1375928_comment'></div>天下安流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1375928_comment'></div>昏垫无忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1375928_comment'></div>禹功既大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1375928_comment'></div>舜禅克修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1375928_comment'></div>其功也与天优优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1375928_comment'></div>其绩也与河悠悠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1375928_comment'></div>兆庶其安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1375928_comment'></div>九河如箭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1375928_comment'></div>浊不可鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1375928_comment'></div>崄不可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1375928_comment'></div>涡若惊风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1375928_comment'></div>浪如狂电。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1375928_comment'></div>若此帝妫之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1375928_comment'></div>则其流也如丝如线。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1375928_comment'></div>在昔典午之世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1375928_comment'></div>其君实良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1375928_comment'></div>其臣孔臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1375928_comment'></div>念济者之太劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1375928_comment'></div>乃致功而去航。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1375928_comment'></div>子产之济也不足比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1375928_comment'></div>充国之奏也胡可方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1375928_comment'></div>于是督斤斧于梓匠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1375928_comment'></div>下材干于豫章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1375928_comment'></div>造其舟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1375928_comment'></div>乃絙乃杠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1375928_comment'></div>乃舆乃梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1375928_comment'></div>功既夺于利涉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1375928_comment'></div>力可侔于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_106_1375928", 1375928, "Clauses/106/Comments/0")'>巨防</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1375928_comment'></div>如御鼋鼍者以妖为德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1375928_comment'></div>聚鱼鳖者以怪为祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1375928_comment'></div>观其步高于空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1375928_comment'></div>履险于深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1375928_comment'></div>其形也若剑倚天外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1375928_comment'></div>其状也若龙横水心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1375928_comment'></div>其高也若大虹之贯天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1375928_comment'></div>风吹不动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1375928_comment'></div>其壮也若巨鳌之压海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1375928_comment'></div>浪泛不沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1375928_comment'></div>曙色霍开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1375928_comment'></div>济者相排。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1375928_comment'></div>如川失水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1375928_comment'></div>一物时来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1375928_comment'></div>蹄响如雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1375928_comment'></div>车音若雷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1375928_comment'></div>有贤有俊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1375928_comment'></div>有隶有台有贫有窭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1375928_comment'></div>有货有财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1375928_comment'></div>噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1375928_comment'></div>前王之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1375928_comment'></div>深有旨哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1375928_comment'></div>在水则河桥晓济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1375928_comment'></div>在陆则四关尽开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1375928_comment'></div>水之与陆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1375928_comment'></div>一贯而来所以大同其轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1375928_comment'></div>广纳其材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1375928_comment'></div>岂梁之防乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1375928_comment'></div>抑闻三代之桥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1375928_comment'></div>不斤不斧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1375928_comment'></div>不徒不杠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1375928_comment'></div>以道为水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1375928_comment'></div>以贤为梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1375928_comment'></div>济民者民不病溺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1375928_comment'></div>济世者世不颓纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1375928_comment'></div>开之也通仁流义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1375928_comment'></div>闭之也关淫限荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1375928_comment'></div>夏之梁也曰汤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1375928_comment'></div>殷之梁也曰昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1375928_comment'></div>周之梁也曰旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1375928_comment'></div>汉之梁也曰光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1375928_comment'></div>自汉之季。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1375928_comment'></div>国窃主折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1375928_comment'></div>为水者以洚以强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1375928_comment'></div>及隋之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1375928_comment'></div>为梁者唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1375928_comment'></div>故能济民于万方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1375928_comment'></div>同轨于八荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1375928_comment'></div>是知河桥之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1375928_comment'></div>可以献于天王。</div><div id='poem_sentence_156_1375928_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=863')">863年3月</a>　三月寒食日，又作《首阳山碑》<div id='poem_1376076' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376076' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376076?labeling=true' target='_blank'>首阳山碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（863年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1376076")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376076_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376076'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376076'>天必从道。道不由天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376076_comment'></div>其曰人乎哉。大圣应千百年之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376076_comment'></div>仁发于祥。义发于瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376076_comment'></div>上圣帝也。次素王也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376076_comment'></div>莫不应乎天地。亘乎日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376076_comment'></div>动乎鬼神。或有守道以介死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376076_comment'></div>秉志以穷生。确然金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376076_comment'></div>不足为贞。澹然冰玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376076_comment'></div>不足为洁。非其上古圣人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376076_comment'></div>不以动其心。况当世富贵之士哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376076_comment'></div>斯其自信乎道。则天地不可得而应者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376076_comment'></div>呜呼。夷齐之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376076_comment'></div>当以神农虞夏形于言。由是观之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376076_comment'></div>岂有意于文武者哉。然迹其归周不从谏而死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376076_comment'></div>彼当求西伯也。而得武王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376076_comment'></div>不曰得仁乎。既得其仁而不取其谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376076_comment'></div>则夷齐之死宜矣。太史公以其饿死责乎天道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376076_comment'></div>呜呼。若夷齐之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376076_comment'></div>可谓道不由天者乎。如不得仁而饿死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376076_comment'></div>天可责也。苟夷齐以殷乱可去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376076_comment'></div>而臣于周。则周召之列矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376076_comment'></div>奚有首阳之阨乎。若夷齐者自信其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376076_comment'></div>天不可得而应者也。天尚不可应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376076_comment'></div>况于人乎。况于鬼神乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376076_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1376076_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=863')">863年3月</a>　三月寒食日，又作《文中子碑》<div id='poem_1376074' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376074' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376074?labeling=true' target='_blank'>文中子碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（863年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1376074")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376074_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376074'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376074'>天不能言。阴骘乎民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376074_comment'></div>民不可纵。是生圣人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376074_comment'></div>圣人之道德与命符。是为尧舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376074_comment'></div>性与命乖。是为孔颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376074_comment'></div>噫。仲尼之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376074_comment'></div>不及于一国。而被于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376074_comment'></div>不治于一时。而霈于万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376074_comment'></div>非删诗书定礼乐赞周易修春秋者乎。故孟子<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1376074", 1376074, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>叠踵</span>孔圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376074_comment'></div>而赞其道。夐出千世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376074_comment'></div>而可继孟氏者。复何人哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376074_comment'></div>文中子王氏。讳通字仲淹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376074_comment'></div>生于陈隋之间。以乱世不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376074_comment'></div>退于汾晋。序述六经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376074_comment'></div>敷为中说。以行教于门人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376074_comment'></div>夫仲尼删诗书定礼乐赞周易修春秋。先生则有礼论二十五篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376074_comment'></div>续诗三百六十篇。元经三十一篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376074_comment'></div>易赞七十篇。孟子之门人有高第弟子公孙丑万章焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376074_comment'></div>先生则有薛收李靖魏徵李绩杜如晦房玄龄。孟子之门人郁郁于乱世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376074_comment'></div>先生之门人赫赫于盛时。较其道与孔孟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376074_comment'></div>岂徒然哉。设先生生于孔圣之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376074_comment'></div>余恐不在游夏之亚也。况七十子欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376074_comment'></div>惜乎德与命乖。不及䖟吾唐受命而殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376074_comment'></div>苟唐得而用之。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1376074", 1376074, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>贞观之治</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376074_comment'></div>不在于房杜褚魏矣。后先生二百五十馀岁生日休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376074_comment'></div>嗜先生道。业先生文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376074_comment'></div>因读先生后序。尚阙于赞述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376074_comment'></div>想先生<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1376074", 1376074, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>封隧</span>所在。因为铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376074_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1376074'>大道不明。天地沦精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376074_comment'></div>俟圣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1376074", 1376074, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>畅教</span>。乃出先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376074_comment'></div>百氏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1376074", 1376074, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>黜迹</span>。六艺<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1376074", 1376074, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>腾英</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376074_comment'></div>道符真宰。用失阿衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376074_comment'></div>先生门人。为唐之桢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376074_comment'></div>差肩明哲。接武名卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376074_comment'></div>未逾一纪。致我太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376074_comment'></div>先生之功。莫之与京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376074_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1376074_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
永修（建昌）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='482f49d736834eeab6e1101d3c13ddcf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("482f49d736834eeab6e1101d3c13ddcf");'><span id='482f49d736834eeab6e1101d3c13ddcf_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=861&endYear=861')">861年</a>，28岁</div><div id='482f49d736834eeab6e1101d3c13ddcf' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=861&endYear=861')">861年</a>　经永修县北上时，游云居院，访玄福上人，有诗记之。作品：过云居院玄福上人旧居。<div id='poem_15429' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15429' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15429?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作题）</span>云居院玄福上人旧居</a><span class='authorDate'>（861年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15429")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_15429_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15429'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15429'>重到云居独悄然，隔窗窥影尚疑禅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15429'>不逢野老来听法，犹见邻僧为引泉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15429'>龛上已生新<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_15429", 15429, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>石耳</span>，壁间空带旧茶烟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15429'>南宗弟子时时到，泣把山花奠几筵。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15429'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15429_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

南昌

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=861&endYear=861')">861年</a>　冬，入江西观察使幕。作品：秋叶有怀秋江晓望。旅舍除夜。<div id='poem_15514' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15514' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a -----title
彭泽
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0cd1ddf8e79641a9bab723e00404f6d2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0cd1ddf8e79641a9bab723e00404f6d2");'><span id='0cd1ddf8e79641a9bab723e00404f6d2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=862&endYear=862')">862年</a>，29岁</div><div id='0cd1ddf8e79641a9bab723e00404f6d2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=862&endYear=862')">862年5月</a>　在江西观察使幕，五月，游庐山，至江州彭泽。受裴坦之荐，干谒李正范。作品：咏鬼诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=862&endYear=862')">862年</a>　在江西观察使幕，尝与友人李中白相处。八月或入冬之后，皮日休获九江之荐。作品：喜鹊。<div id='poem_15725' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15725' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15725?labeling=true' target='_blank'>喜鹊</a><span class='authorDate'>（862年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15725")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15725_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15725'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15725'>弃膻在庭际，双鹊来摇尾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15725'>欲啄怕人惊，喜语晴光里。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15725'>何况佞倖人，微禽解如此。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15725'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_15725_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1'
