href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=864&endYear=864')">864年</a>，31岁</div><div id='5245dbdaa2d847e3892f6b2da1ae8cf0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=864&endYear=864')">864年3月</a>　与故友李中白相游处和，有词。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=864&endYear=864')">864年</a>　拜谒裴坦、李正范，作《狄梁公祠碑》<div id='poem_1376079' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376079' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376079?labeling=true' target='_blank'>狄梁公祠碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（864年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1376079")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376079_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376079'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376079'>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376079_comment'></div>天后革大命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376079_comment'></div>垂二十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376079_comment'></div>天下晏如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376079_comment'></div>不让贞观之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376079_comment'></div>是遵何道哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376079_comment'></div>非以敬任公乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376079_comment'></div>不然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376079_comment'></div>来俊臣之酷不能诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376079_comment'></div>诸武之猜不能害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376079_comment'></div>房龄之谏不能逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376079_comment'></div>□进士皮日休游江左至彭泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376079_comment'></div>当河东公观察之四年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376079_comment'></div>赞皇公刺史之二年<span class='inlineComment2'>（下阙）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376079_comment'></div>其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376079_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1376079'>惟唐中否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376079_comment'></div>帝室如燬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376079_comment'></div>□后持权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376079_comment'></div>式人端委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376079_comment'></div>书诫牝鸡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376079_comment'></div>易称羸豕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376079_comment'></div>大树得蘬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376079_comment'></div>崇台欲坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376079_comment'></div>便藩诸武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376079_comment'></div>作我蜴虺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376079_comment'></div>泉深兮东宫已矣□北极绾我神玺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376079_comment'></div>娲皇肇命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376079_comment'></div>吕君函纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376079_comment'></div>周德方木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376079_comment'></div>秦运为水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376079_comment'></div>杜□与化宫阙致治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376079_comment'></div>天将启唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376079_comment'></div>载诞忠良□为道如勃木强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376079_comment'></div>乃写大辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376079_comment'></div>对彼明飏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376079_comment'></div>一言苟悖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376079_comment'></div>视死如乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376079_comment'></div>少海既阔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376079_comment'></div>少阳既光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376079_comment'></div>五公始昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376079_comment'></div>共交玉堂<span class='inlineComment2'>（下阙）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1376079_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=864&endYear=864')">864年</a>　重游云居院。作品：十原。惑雷刑。<div id='poem_1376062' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376062' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376062?labeling=true' target='_blank'>惑雷刑</a><span class='authorDate'>（864年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1376062")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376062_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376062'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376062'>彭泽县乡曰黄花。有农户曰逢氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376062_comment'></div>田甚广。巳牛不能备耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376062_comment'></div>尝僦他牛以兼其力。逢氏之猾恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376062_comment'></div>为一乡之师焉。得他牛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376062_comment'></div>则昼役夕归。箠耕于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1376062", 1376062, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>烈景</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376062_comment'></div>笞耨于晦冥。未尝一息容其殆忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376062_comment'></div>一日。猝雷发山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376062_comment'></div>逢氏震死。日休曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376062_comment'></div>逢氏之猾恶。天假雷刑绝其命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376062_comment'></div>信矣。夫生民之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376062_comment'></div>不过乎稼穑之功。皆不为是畜之力哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376062_comment'></div>则天之保牛。齐民命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376062_comment'></div>宜矣。今逢氏苦其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376062_comment'></div>天则震死。如燕赵无赖少年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376062_comment'></div>椎之以私享。烹之以市货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376062_comment'></div>法不可戢。刑不可威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376062_comment'></div>则天之保牛。皆不降于雷刑哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376062_comment'></div>则逢氏之死。吾不知是天地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376062_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1376062_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
西安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7bab68c64fee42bb885acb95554576b2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7bab68c64fee42bb885acb95554576b2");'><span id='7bab68c64fee42bb885acb95554576b2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=862&endYear=863')">862-863年</a>，29-30岁</div><div id='7bab68c64fee42bb885acb95554576b2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=862&endYear=862')">862年</a>　冬，皮日休离江右而至长安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=862&endYear=862')">862年</a>　皮日休入长安后，或干谒前江西观察使、户部侍郎裴寅。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=862&endYear=862')">862年</a>　入长安，即招谗致谤，乃愤然自辨。作品：内辨。<div id='poem_1376024' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376024' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376024?labeling=true' target='_blank'>内辨</a><span class='authorDate'>（862年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1376024")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376024_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376024'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376024'>日休自布衣受九江之荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376024_comment'></div>与计偕寓止永崇里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376024_comment'></div>居浃旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376024_comment'></div>有来候者曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376024_comment'></div>子几退于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376024_comment'></div>几孰于执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376024_comment'></div>其誉与名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376024_comment'></div>煜煜于京师矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376024_comment'></div>致是也者孰自。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376024_comment'></div>曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376024_comment'></div>偶与计偕者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376024_comment'></div>曾未识咸阳城阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376024_comment'></div>所贽者未及卿相之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376024_comment'></div>所趋者未入势利之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376024_comment'></div>其誉与名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376024_comment'></div>反不知其自矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376024_comment'></div>曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376024_comment'></div>闻子受今小司徒河东公知素矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376024_comment'></div>公当时之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376024_comment'></div>溟渤于文场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376024_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1376024", 1376024, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>嵩华</span>于朝右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376024_comment'></div>子之上第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376024_comment'></div>不足凭他门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376024_comment'></div>曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376024_comment'></div>公之为前达接后进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376024_comment'></div>今之中古人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376024_comment'></div>愚欲自知其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376024_comment'></div>干之以其文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376024_comment'></div>以名臣之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376024_comment'></div>绌贱士之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376024_comment'></div>其为知大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376024_comment'></div>所谓干之以其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376024_comment'></div>知之亦以其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376024_comment'></div>遇其人则宣之于口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376024_comment'></div>不遇其人则贮之于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376024_comment'></div>非佞传媚说者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376024_comment'></div>或者不怿而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376024_comment'></div>居一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376024_comment'></div>又有来者曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376024_comment'></div>喋喋之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376024_comment'></div>谓子赖其知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376024_comment'></div>欲一举于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376024_comment'></div>信哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376024_comment'></div>曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376024_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376024_comment'></div>圣天子之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376024_comment'></div>文教如膏雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376024_comment'></div>儒风如扶摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376024_comment'></div>草茅之士得以达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376024_comment'></div>市井之子可以进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376024_comment'></div>名场大辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376024_comment'></div>豁若广路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376024_comment'></div>千百人各负累能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376024_comment'></div>时执事各立用誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376024_comment'></div>如日休之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376024_comment'></div>处于场中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376024_comment'></div>若放鲲鲕于东溟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376024_comment'></div>逐獐麛于五岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376024_comment'></div>以小入大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376024_comment'></div>以微混众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376024_comment'></div>其汨汨没没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376024_comment'></div>昭然可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376024_comment'></div>岂能一举于有司哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376024_comment'></div>或练穷物态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376024_comment'></div>晓尽时机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376024_comment'></div>一二十举于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376024_comment'></div>倘处之下列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376024_comment'></div>行其道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376024_comment'></div>上可以布大知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376024_comment'></div>下可以存禄利而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376024_comment'></div>曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376024_comment'></div>若能者谤欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376024_comment'></div>子宜默处梁上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376024_comment'></div>第防其萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376024_comment'></div>曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376024_comment'></div>大圣者不过周孔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376024_comment'></div>然犹管蔡谤然前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376024_comment'></div>叔孙毁于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376024_comment'></div>何由处世而然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376024_comment'></div>亦犹登高者必望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376024_comment'></div>临深者必窥矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376024_comment'></div>诗曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376024_comment'></div>谗言罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376024_comment'></div>交乱四国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376024_comment'></div>夫四国且乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376024_comment'></div>况一士哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376024_comment'></div>虽然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376024_comment'></div>敢不防其萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376024_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376024_comment'></div>防而免者人欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376024_comment'></div>防而不免者天欤。</div><div id='poem_sentence_90_1376024_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=862&endYear=862')">862年</a>　皮日休谒成均博士某，与归氏子相侮，或在此时。作品：移成均博士书。<div id='poem_1375935' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375935' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375935?labeling=true' target='_blank'>移成均博士书</a><span class='authorDate'>（862年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375935")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375935_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375935'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375935'>夫居位而愧道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375935_comment'></div>上则荒其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375935_comment'></div>下则偷其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375935_comment'></div>业而可荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375935_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1375935", 1375935, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>文弊</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375935_comment'></div>言而可偷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375935_comment'></div>训薄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375935_comment'></div>故圣人惧是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375935_comment'></div>寖移其化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375935_comment'></div>上自天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375935_comment'></div>下至子男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375935_comment'></div>必立庠以化之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375935_comment'></div>设序以教之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375935_comment'></div>犹歉然不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375935_comment'></div>士有业高训深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375935_comment'></div>必诎礼以延之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375935_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1375935", 1375935, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>越爵</span>以贵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375935_comment'></div>俾庠声序音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375935_comment'></div>玲珑以珩佩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375935_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1375935", 1375935, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>锵訇</span>于金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375935_comment'></div>此圣人之至治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375935_comment'></div>今国家立成均之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375935_comment'></div>其礼盛于周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375935_comment'></div>其品广于汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375935_comment'></div>其诎礼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1375935", 1375935, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>越爵</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375935_comment'></div>又甚于前世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375935_comment'></div>而未免乎愧道者何哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375935_comment'></div>夫圣人之为文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375935_comment'></div>为经约乎史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375935_comment'></div>赞易近乎象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375935_comment'></div>诗书止乎删。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375935_comment'></div>礼乐止乎定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375935_comment'></div>春秋止乎修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375935_comment'></div>然六籍仪刑乎千万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375935_comment'></div>百王更命迭号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375935_comment'></div>莫不由是大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375935_comment'></div>其幽幽于鬼神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1375935_comment'></div>其妙妙于元造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1375935_comment'></div>后之人苟不能行决句释者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1375935_comment'></div>犹万物但被元造之化者耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1375935_comment'></div>故万物但化而巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1375935_comment'></div>不知元造之源也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1375935_comment'></div>六艺于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1375935_comment'></div>又何异于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1375935_comment'></div>故诗得毛公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1375935_comment'></div>书得伏生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1375935_comment'></div>易得杨何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1375935_comment'></div>礼得二戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1375935_comment'></div>周官得郑康成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1375935_comment'></div>摫其微言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1375935_comment'></div>釽其大义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1375935_comment'></div>幽者明于日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1375935_comment'></div>奥者廓于天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1375935_comment'></div>然则今之讲习之功与决释之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1375935_comment'></div>不啻半矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1375935_comment'></div>其文得不弊乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1375935_comment'></div>其训得不薄乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1375935_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1375935_comment'></div>西域氏之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1375935_comment'></div>其徒日以讲习决释其法为事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1375935_comment'></div>视吾之太学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1375935_comment'></div>又足为西域氏之羞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1375935_comment'></div>足下出<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1375935", 1375935, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>文阃</span>生<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1375935", 1375935, "Clauses/62/Comments/1")'>学世</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1375935_comment'></div>业精前古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1375935_comment'></div>言高当今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1375935_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1375935", 1375935, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>洸洸</span>乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1375935_comment'></div>洋洋乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1375935_comment'></div>为诸生之蓍龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1375935_comment'></div>作后来之绵蕝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1375935_comment'></div>得不思居其位者不愧其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1375935_comment'></div>处于职者不堕其业乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1375935_comment'></div>否则市大易负乘之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1375935_comment'></div>招诗人伐檀之刺矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1375935_comment'></div>奚不日诫其属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1375935_comment'></div>月励其徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1375935_comment'></div>年持六籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1375935_comment'></div>日决百氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1375935_comment'></div>俾诸生于盛典也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1375935_comment'></div>洞知大晓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1375935_comment'></div>犹驾车者必知康庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1375935_comment'></div>操舟者必知河海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1375935_comment'></div>既若是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1375935_comment'></div>执其业者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1375935_comment'></div>精者进而堕者退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1375935_comment'></div>公者得而私者失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1375935_comment'></div>非惟大发于儒风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1375935_comment'></div>抑亦不苟于禄位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1375935_comment'></div>足下之道被于太学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1375935_comment'></div>其利可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1375935_comment'></div>果行是说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1375935_comment'></div>则太华之石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1375935_comment'></div>峨峨于成均之门者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1375935_comment'></div>吾不颂于他人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1375935_comment'></div>足下听之无忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1375935_comment'></div>日休再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_94_1375935_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=863')">863年</a>　科举落第。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='6e5dd4f0c8e64bad923e372de9ab2c36_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6e5dd4f0c8e64bad923e372de9ab2c36");'><span id='6e5dd4f0c8e64bad923e372de9ab2c36_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=865&endYear=866')">865-866年</a>，32-33岁</div><div id='6e5dd4f0c8e64bad923e372de9ab2c36' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=865&endYear=865')">865年</a>　入冬后自寿州经樊、邓、商颜、蓝关入京。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=866&endYear=866')">866年</a>　科举不第。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1b1b0b35fa4445188d465184b9402528_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1b1b0b35fa4445188d465184b9402528");'><span id='1b1b0b35fa4445188d465184b9402528_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=866&endYear=868')">866-868年</a>，33-35岁</div><div id='1b1b0b35fa4445188d465184b9402528' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=866&endYear=866')">866年9月</a>　皮日休盖负令狐绹、杨知至之苈往长安。作品：桃花赋。请韩文公配响太学书。<div id='poem_1375929' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375929' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375929?labeling=true' target='_blank'>桃花赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（866年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375929")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375929_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1375929'>余尝慕宋广平之为相。贞姿劲质。刚态毅状。疑其铁肠石心。不解吐婉媚辞。然睹其文而有梅花赋。清便富艳。得南朝徐庾体。殊不类其为人也。后苏相公味道得而称之。广平之名遂振。呜呼。夫广平之才。未为是赋。则苏公果暇知其人哉。将广平困于穷。厄于踬。然强为是文邪。日休于文尚矣。状花卉。体风物。非有所讽。辄抑而不发。因感广平之所作。复为桃花赋。其辞曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1375929_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375929'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375929'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1375929", 1375929, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>伊祁氏</span>之作春也。有艳外之艳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375929_comment'></div>华中之华。众木不得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375929_comment'></div>融为桃花。厥花伊何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375929_comment'></div>其美实多。儓隶众芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375929_comment'></div>缘饰阳和。开破嫩𦹛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375929_comment'></div>压低柔柯。其色则不淡不深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375929_comment'></div>若素练轻茜。玉颜半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375929_comment'></div>若夫美景妍时。春含晓滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375929_comment'></div>密如不干。繁若无枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375929_comment'></div>妦妦婉婉。夭夭怡怡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375929_comment'></div>或俛者若想。或閒者如痴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375929_comment'></div>或向者若步。或倚者如疲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375929_comment'></div>或温黁而可薰。或婑媠而莫持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375929_comment'></div>或<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1375929", 1375929, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>幽柔</span>而旁午。或<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1375929", 1375929, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>扯冶</span>而倒披。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375929_comment'></div>或翘矣如望。或凝然若思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375929_comment'></div>或<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1375929", 1375929, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>奕偞</span>而作态。或窈窕而骋姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375929_comment'></div>日将明兮似喜。天将惨兮若悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375929_comment'></div>近榆钱兮妆翠靥。映杨柳兮颦愁眉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375929_comment'></div>轻红拖裳。动则袅香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375929_comment'></div>宛若郑袖。初见吴王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375929_comment'></div>夜景皎洁。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1375929", 1375929, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>鬨然</span>秀发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375929_comment'></div>又若常娥。欲奔明月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375929_comment'></div>蝶散蜂寂。当闺脉脉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375929_comment'></div>又若妲巳。未闻裂帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375929_comment'></div>或开故楚。艳艳春曙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375929_comment'></div>又若息妫。含情不语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375929_comment'></div>或临金塘。或交绮井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375929_comment'></div>又若西子。浣纱见影。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375929_comment'></div>玉露<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1375929", 1375929, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>厌浥</span>。妖红坠湿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375929_comment'></div>又若骊姬。将谮而泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375929_comment'></div>或在水滨。或临江浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375929_comment'></div>又若神女。见郑交甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375929_comment'></div>或临广筵。或当高会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375929_comment'></div>又若韩娥。将歌敛态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375929_comment'></div>微动轻风。婆娑暖红。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375929_comment'></div>又若飞燕。舞于掌中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375929_comment'></div>半沾斜吹。或动或止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1375929_comment'></div>又若文姬。将赋而思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1375929_comment'></div>丰茸旖旎。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1375929", 1375929, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>互交</span>递倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1375929_comment'></div>又若丽华。侍宴初醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1375929_comment'></div>狂风猛雨。一阵红去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1375929_comment'></div>又若褒姒。初随戎虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1375929_comment'></div>满地春色。阶前砌侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1375929_comment'></div>又若戚姬。死于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1375929", 1375929, "Clauses/87/Comments/0")'>鞠域</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1375929_comment'></div>花品之中。此花最异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1375929_comment'></div>以众为繁。以多见鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1375929_comment'></div>自是物情。非关春意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1375929_comment'></div>若氏族之斥<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1375929", 1375929, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>素流</span>。品秩之卑寒士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1375929_comment'></div>他目则目。他耳则耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1375929_comment'></div>或以昵而称珍。或以疏而见贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1375929_comment'></div>或有实而华乖。或有花而实悴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1375929_comment'></div>其花可以畅君之心目。其实可以充君之口腹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1375929_comment'></div>匪乎兹花。他则碌碌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1375929_comment'></div>我将修花品以此花为第一。惧俗情之横议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1375929_comment'></div>我曰不然。为之则巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1375929_comment'></div>我目吾目。我耳吾耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1375929_comment'></div>妍蚩决于心。取舍断于志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1375929_comment'></div>岂于草木之品独然。信为国兮如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1375929_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1375929_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1375933' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375933' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375933?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请韩文公配飨太学书</a><span class='authorDate'>（866年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375933")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375933_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375933'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375933'>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375933_comment'></div>圣人之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375933_comment'></div>不过乎求用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375933_comment'></div>用于生前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375933_comment'></div>则一时可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375933_comment'></div>用于死后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375933_comment'></div>则百世可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375933_comment'></div>故孔子之封赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375933_comment'></div>自汉至隋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375933_comment'></div>其爵不过乎公侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375933_comment'></div>至于吾唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375933_comment'></div>乃策王号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375933_comment'></div>七十子之爵命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375933_comment'></div>自汉至隋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375933_comment'></div>或卿大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375933_comment'></div>至于吾唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375933_comment'></div>乃封公侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375933_comment'></div>曾参之孝道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375933_comment'></div>动天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375933_comment'></div>感鬼神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375933_comment'></div>自汉至隋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375933_comment'></div>不过乎诸子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375933_comment'></div>至于吾唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375933_comment'></div>乃旌入十哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375933_comment'></div>噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375933_comment'></div>天地久否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375933_comment'></div>忽泰则平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375933_comment'></div>日月久昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375933_comment'></div>忽开则明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375933_comment'></div>雷霆久息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375933_comment'></div>忽震则惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375933_comment'></div>云雾久郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375933_comment'></div>忽廓则清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375933_comment'></div>仲尼之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375933_comment'></div>否于周秦而昏于汉魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375933_comment'></div>息于晋宋而郁于陈隋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375933_comment'></div>遇于吾唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1375933_comment'></div>万世之愤一朝而释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1375933_comment'></div>倘死者可作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1375933_comment'></div>其志可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1375933_comment'></div>今有人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1375933_comment'></div>身行圣人之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1375933_comment'></div>口吐圣人之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1375933_comment'></div>行如颜闵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1375933_comment'></div>文若游夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1375933_comment'></div>死不得配食于夫子之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1375933_comment'></div>愚又不知尊先圣之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1375933_comment'></div>夫孟子荀卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1375933_comment'></div>翼传孔道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1375933_comment'></div>以至于文中子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1375933_comment'></div>文中子之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1375933_comment'></div>降及贞观开元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1375933_comment'></div>其传者醨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1375933_comment'></div>其继者浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1375933_comment'></div>或引刑名以为文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1375933_comment'></div>或援纵横以为理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1375933_comment'></div>或作词赋以为雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1375933_comment'></div>文中之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1375933_comment'></div>旷百世而得室授者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1375933_comment'></div>惟昌黎文公焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1375933_comment'></div>公之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1375933_comment'></div>蹴杨墨于不毛之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1375933_comment'></div>蹂释老于无人之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1375933_comment'></div>故得孔道巍然而自正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1375933_comment'></div>夫今之文人千百世之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1375933_comment'></div>释其卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1375933_comment'></div>观其词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1375933_comment'></div>无不裨造化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1375933_comment'></div>补时政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1375933_comment'></div>繄公之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1375933_comment'></div>公之文曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1375933_comment'></div>仆自度若世无孔子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1375933_comment'></div>仆不当在弟子之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1375933_comment'></div>设使公生孔子之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1375933_comment'></div>公未必不在四科焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1375933_comment'></div>国家以二十二贤者代用其书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1375933_comment'></div>垂于国胄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1375933_comment'></div>并配享于孔圣庙堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1375933_comment'></div>其为典礼也大矣美矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1375933_comment'></div>苟以代用其书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1375933_comment'></div>不能以释圣人之辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1375933_comment'></div>笺圣人之义哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1375933_comment'></div>况有身行其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1375933_comment'></div>口传其文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1375933_comment'></div>吾唐以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1375933_comment'></div>一人而巳死反不得在二十二贤之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1375933_comment'></div>则未闻乎典礼为备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1375933_comment'></div>伏请命有司定其配享之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1375933_comment'></div>则自兹以后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1375933_comment'></div>天下以文化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1375933_comment'></div>未必不由夫是也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_90_1375933_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=867&endYear=867')">867年</a>　科举及第，旋遭座主郑愚之嘲戏。作品：登第后寒食杏园有宴，因寄录事宋垂文同年。<div id='poem_15543' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15543' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=868&endYear=868')">868年</a>　旋自京东游，往淮南扬州；道出华山，有诗；出函关，有诗；又乐荆山，赏女几，度轩辕，穷嵩高，入京索，又浮汴渠。作品：古函关。<div id='poem_15330' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15330' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=872&endYear=872')">872年2月</a>　春二月，皮日休在长安秘书省教书郎任，又撮岭南东道节度使郑愚巡官，应邀为常熟县令周邦弼作《破山龙堂记》<div id='poem_1375942' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375942' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375942?labeling=true' target='_blank'>破山龙堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（872年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375942")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375942_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375942'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375942'>礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375942_comment'></div>山林川谷邱陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375942_comment'></div>能出云为风雨见怪物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375942_comment'></div>皆曰神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375942_comment'></div>若然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375942_comment'></div>龙亦能为风雨见怪物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375942_comment'></div>则其泽之在民厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375942_comment'></div>神而祀之又宜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375942_comment'></div>常熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375942_comment'></div>泽国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375942_comment'></div>风雨怪物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375942_comment'></div>日作于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375942_comment'></div>在有其地者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375942_comment'></div>苟祀之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375942_comment'></div>民被其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375942_comment'></div>祀之不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375942_comment'></div>民受其祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375942_comment'></div>汝南周君为令之初年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375942_comment'></div>夏且旱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375942_comment'></div>禜其神于破山之潭上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375942_comment'></div>果雨以应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375942_comment'></div>君曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375942_comment'></div>受其赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375942_comment'></div>徒禜以报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375942_comment'></div>不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375942_comment'></div>于是命工以土木介其象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375942_comment'></div>为宝宫以荫之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375942_comment'></div>著之于典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375942_comment'></div>以洁其祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375942_comment'></div>于是风雨时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375942_comment'></div>怪物止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375942_comment'></div>水旱不为厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375942_comment'></div>民经大荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375942_comment'></div>连岁以穰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375942_comment'></div>其神之泽乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375942_comment'></div>君之祀乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375942_comment'></div>凡雩者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1375942_comment'></div>春秋之道皆书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1375942_comment'></div>勤民之祀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1375942_comment'></div>君为其祠已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1375942_comment'></div>乞文其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1375942_comment'></div>日休佳君之为志在民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1375942_comment'></div>故从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1375942_comment'></div>咸通十三年二月十九日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1375942_comment'></div>襄阳皮日休记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1375942_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=873&endYear=874')">873-874年</a><br /></div><div class='label1' id='9d011bc45ac34c25bfc6b02aa5e0e5ed_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9d011bc45ac34c25bfc6b02aa5e0e5ed");'><span id='9d011bc45ac34c25bfc6b02aa5e0e5ed_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=880&endYear=880')">880年</a>，47岁</div><div id='9d011bc45ac34c25bfc6b02aa5e0e5ed' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=880&endYear=880')">880年12月13日</a>　冬，十二月五日凌晨，唐僖宗仓皇出逃。巢军入长安。十二月三日，黄巢建大齐，皮日休为翰林学士，之后，皮日休行履未详。传闻不一出。或云：巢令皮日休作谶词，词曰：“预知圣人姓，田八二十一。欲知圣人名，果头三曲律。”巢以其谶己，大怒而杀皮日休。有云巢败后，皮日休被唐廷诛杀。有云终老南粤者，不足以信。有云病死宿州者，更不足信。甚有以为皮日休借巡查新定州县之机，在同官县题壁后自裁者，然所据文献误。亦有云巢败后，皮日休逃归江南。晚依钱镠，终老会稽，并尝与罗隐等在钱镠幕府幕府共座谈笑者。此似有可信之处。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
许昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='692408dd67214cbd82b956afbf7a82a7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("692408dd67214cbd82b956afbf7a82a7");'><span id='692408dd67214cbd82b956afbf7a82a7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=863')">863年</a>，30岁</div><div id='692408dd67214cbd82b956afbf7a82a7' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>皮日休至许昌，作《三羞诗》之“南蛮不择吏”；又作《忧赋》之“南蛮不择吏”忧赋。<div id='poem_1375927' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375927' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375927?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忧赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（863年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375927")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375927_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1375927'>草茅臣日休见南蛮不宾。天下徵发。民力将毙。乃为赋以见其志。词曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1375927_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375927'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375927'>上有太古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375927_comment'></div>粤有民族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375927_comment'></div>颛若混命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375927_comment'></div>愚如视肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375927_comment'></div>当斯时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375927_comment'></div>虽三王之道不能化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375927_comment'></div>五帝之泽不能沐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375927_comment'></div>迨乎混沌欻起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375927_comment'></div>觇视騞分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375927_comment'></div>其形也有精有神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375927_comment'></div>其心也有伪有真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375927_comment'></div>既凋其质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375927_comment'></div>又秀其纯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375927_comment'></div>有智有机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375927_comment'></div>有义有仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375927_comment'></div>有怨有怼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375927_comment'></div>有悲有辛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375927_comment'></div>居人灵府者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375927_comment'></div>总属于神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375927_comment'></div>神之生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375927_comment'></div>摄爽孕精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375927_comment'></div>胎意婴情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375927_comment'></div>不迹不眹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375927_comment'></div>无臭无声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375927_comment'></div>不居于愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375927_comment'></div>不侵于婴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375927_comment'></div>先物而动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375927_comment'></div>先人而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375927_comment'></div>不注而溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375927_comment'></div>不丝而萦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375927_comment'></div>神之居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375927_comment'></div>填胸塞臆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375927_comment'></div>冥冥默默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375927_comment'></div>静如寐魔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375927_comment'></div>将语不得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375927_comment'></div>其遇如噎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375927_comment'></div>其饮如食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1375927_comment'></div>其轻者瘠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1375927_comment'></div>其重者殛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1375927_comment'></div>神之行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1375927_comment'></div>其居幽幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1375927_comment'></div>其行悠悠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1375927_comment'></div>来不可抑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1375927_comment'></div>去不可留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1375927_comment'></div>其情如剸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1375927_comment'></div>其绪如抽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1375927_comment'></div>其刚为愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1375927_comment'></div>其弱为羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1375927_comment'></div>其子为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1375927_comment'></div>其孙为愁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1375927_comment'></div>入人之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1375927_comment'></div>如毒如螫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1375927_comment'></div>如虔如刘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1375927_comment'></div>不纶而渔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1375927_comment'></div>不兵而蒐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1375927_comment'></div>其坚也龙泉不能割。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1375927_comment'></div>其痛也蓖荔不能瘳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1375927_comment'></div>入人之怀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1375927_comment'></div>倘倘佯佯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1375927_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1375927", 1375927, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>隐隐遑遑</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1375927_comment'></div>牢然不胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1375927_comment'></div>悒若有亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1375927_comment'></div>威能制佚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1375927_comment'></div>力可摧刚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1375927_comment'></div>乖人之性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1375927_comment'></div>反天之常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1375927_comment'></div>不丧而戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1375927_comment'></div>不役而忙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1375927_comment'></div>不触而醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1375927_comment'></div>不驰而狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1375927_comment'></div>是知食鯈鱼者不能巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1375927_comment'></div>树萱草者不可忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1375927_comment'></div>倘怀如嚄唶者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1375927_comment'></div>其人立伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1375927_comment'></div>入人之神也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1375927_comment'></div>昧人之精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1375927_comment'></div>烁人之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1375927_comment'></div>痴然而作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1375927_comment'></div>如病宿酲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1375927_comment'></div>虽有王澄之色必俛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1375927_comment'></div>乐广之神不清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1375927_comment'></div>入人之首也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1375927_comment'></div>欻从内热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1375927_comment'></div>郁而上结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1375927_comment'></div>不劳膏沐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1375927_comment'></div>自清其发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1375927_comment'></div>有久而释者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1375927_comment'></div>则其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1375927_comment'></div>冠丝簪雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1375927_comment'></div>入人之眉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1375927_comment'></div>于悒摧颓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1375927_comment'></div>思不自裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1375927_comment'></div>动如葭灰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1375927_comment'></div>飞上眉来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1375927_comment'></div>颦然无力。<div id='poem_sentence_96_1375927_comment'></div>双眉之翠如一月不开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1375927_comment'></div>入人之目也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1375927_comment'></div>端坐日晏。<div id='poem_sentence_101_1375927_comment'></div>外象不遍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1375927_comment'></div>虽有斧藻之绣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1375927_comment'></div>毛嫱骊姬到于前。<div id='poem_sentence_106_1375927_comment'></div>希希夷夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1375927_comment'></div>俯而不思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1375927_comment'></div>殷然满耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1375927_comment'></div>其身如尸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1375927_comment'></div>虽师旷之善听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1375927_comment'></div>苟入之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1375927_comment'></div>迅雷烈风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1375927_comment'></div>亦不闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1375927_comment'></div>入人之齿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1375927_comment'></div>噤其齿牙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1375927_comment'></div>淡其含咀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1375927_comment'></div>悲嗟既巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1375927_comment'></div>哆如饿虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1375927_comment'></div>虽有膹炙餫𩝧堆其前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1375927_comment'></div>粝不可茹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1375927_comment'></div>入人四枝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1375927_comment'></div>如絷如维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1375927_comment'></div>如劳如疲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1375927_comment'></div>其力如柳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1375927_comment'></div>弱不可支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1375927_comment'></div>苟甚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1375927_comment'></div>消骨枯髓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1375927_comment'></div>夺色削肌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1375927_comment'></div>其人也立不胜衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1375927_comment'></div>噫嘻呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1375927_comment'></div>忧之甚也如斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1375927_comment'></div>向其入之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1375927_comment'></div>臣皆有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1375927_comment'></div>然犹未忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1375927_comment'></div>何实为师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1375927_comment'></div>既忧其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1375927_comment'></div>须忧其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1375927_comment'></div>苟肉食者谋失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1375927_comment'></div>而藿食者殃罹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1375927_comment'></div>可不忧欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1375927_comment'></div>可不忧欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1375927_comment'></div>夫于政而疲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1375927_comment'></div>于禄而尸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1375927_comment'></div>王道不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1375927_comment'></div>皇纲不维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1375927_comment'></div>元恶作矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1375927_comment'></div>大盗乘之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1375927_comment'></div>是臣忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1375927_comment'></div>后之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1375927_comment'></div>阴教规矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1375927_comment'></div>夏德涂山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1375927_comment'></div>周赞文母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1375927_comment'></div>牝鸡无晨。<div id='poem_sentence_156_1375927_comment'></div>乃神器之可取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1375927_comment'></div>宫掖紊乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1375927_comment'></div>奸邪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_159_1375927", 1375927, "Clauses/159/Comments/0")'>麀聚</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1375927_comment'></div>文信为相而私后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1375927_comment'></div>董偃作庸而尚主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1375927_comment'></div>其甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1375927_comment'></div>汉成母以国循姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1375927_comment'></div>周宣后将权授父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1375927_comment'></div>是臣忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1375927_comment'></div>储后之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1375927_comment'></div>实贤与良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1375927_comment'></div>少海增润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1375927_comment'></div>重离益光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1375927_comment'></div>辅导不至。<div id='poem_sentence_172_1375927_comment'></div>嗟临江之悯王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1375927_comment'></div>斯爱是即。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1375927_comment'></div>恶乃易彰。<div
