id='poem_sentence_182_1375927_comment'></div>印绶足以饰其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1375927_comment'></div>至乃割域中之土宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1375927_comment'></div>半天下之黎民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1375927_comment'></div>王犹未足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1375927_comment'></div>乱以遄臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1375927_comment'></div>其甚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1375927_comment'></div>篡则王伦孙秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1375927_comment'></div>杀则清河万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1375927_comment'></div>是臣忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1375927_comment'></div>辅之而王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1375927_comment'></div>在忠与良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1375927_comment'></div>致叔父于折木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1375927_comment'></div>取太公于钓璜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1375927_comment'></div>宠之极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1375927_comment'></div>其化为权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1375927_comment'></div>权之极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1375927_comment'></div>其化为强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1375927_comment'></div>其甚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1375927_comment'></div>曹操以兵而上殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1375927_comment'></div>高澄抑帝而劝觞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1375927_comment'></div>是臣忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1375927_comment'></div>内竖之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1375927_comment'></div>乃宠而绥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1375927_comment'></div>竖刁乱齐之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1375927_comment'></div>伊戾祸宋之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1375927_comment'></div>西汉则中令扇迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1375927_comment'></div>东京则鄛卿构基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1375927_comment'></div>举手天转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1375927_comment'></div>切齿国危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1375927_comment'></div>其甚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1375927_comment'></div>陈蕃以贤而陷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1375927_comment'></div>何进用忠而僇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1375927_comment'></div>是臣忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1375927_comment'></div>贾谊爱时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1375927_comment'></div>仕止于国傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1375927_comment'></div>桓谭非谶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1375927_comment'></div>官止于郡丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1375927_comment'></div>是臣忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1375927_comment'></div>将在于军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1375927_comment'></div>君命不复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1375927_comment'></div>知魏绛之法行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1375927_comment'></div>见条侯之令肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1375927_comment'></div>郭开受谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1375927_comment'></div>李牧就诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1375927_comment'></div>范睢一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1375927_comment'></div>武安被僇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1375927_comment'></div>是臣忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1375927_comment'></div>王臣蹇蹇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1375927_comment'></div>言须逆耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1375927_comment'></div>治乱终书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1375927_comment'></div>善恶必纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1375927_comment'></div>赵盾终屈于董狐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1375927_comment'></div>崔杼竟书于太史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1375927_comment'></div>至有陈象极言以族灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1375927_comment'></div>李云上书而身死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1375927_comment'></div>是臣忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1375927_comment'></div>悬官待贿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1375927_comment'></div>命相取资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1375927_comment'></div>崔烈作司徒之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1375927_comment'></div>曹嵩为太尉之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1375927_comment'></div>未搜岩穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1375927_comment'></div>莫访茅茨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1375927_comment'></div>秦缪既诛于五羖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1375927_comment'></div>桓魋将退于仲尼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1375927_comment'></div>是臣忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1375927_comment'></div>法令如网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1375927_comment'></div>随而补之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1375927_comment'></div>肺石之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1375927_comment'></div>落人涕洟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1375927_comment'></div>公孙鞅恢令之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1375927_comment'></div>严延年扫墓之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1375927_comment'></div>是臣忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1375927_comment'></div>命将兴师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1375927_comment'></div>夸力四夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1375927_comment'></div>既侵岭徼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1375927_comment'></div>又定边陲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1375927_comment'></div>以无用之沙漠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1375927_comment'></div>竭有限之民资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1375927_comment'></div>是以先王谓之荒服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1375927_comment'></div>后嗣谓之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_262_1375927", 1375927, "Clauses/262/Comments/0")'>羁縻</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1375927_comment'></div>岂可使亲帅武旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1375927_comment'></div>躬挥战阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1375927_comment'></div>故汉高有白登之辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1375927_comment'></div>隋炀有雁门之围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1375927_comment'></div>是臣忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1375927_comment'></div>出警入跸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1375927_comment'></div>以示严肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1375927_comment'></div>非有事于名山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1375927_comment'></div>即展义于群牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1375927_comment'></div>故昭王游汉水以无归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1375927_comment'></div>宣帝幸中山而不复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1375927_comment'></div>是臣忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1375927_comment'></div>功作非宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1375927_comment'></div>夺民农时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1375927_comment'></div>我簠不粢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1375927_comment'></div>我黍阻饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1375927_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_279_1375927", 1375927, "Clauses/279/Comments/0")'>倾宫</span>既作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1375927_comment'></div>阿房又施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1375927_comment'></div>人既怨矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1375927_comment'></div>鬼其泣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1375927_comment'></div>是臣忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1375927_comment'></div>头会箕敛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1375927_comment'></div>关征市赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1375927_comment'></div>民之胥怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1375927_comment'></div>无所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_287_1375927", 1375927, "Clauses/287/Comments/0")'>赴愬</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_287_1375927_comment'></div>人厌进修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1375927_comment'></div>家为积聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1375927_comment'></div>卜式出于富人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1375927_comment'></div>宏羊拔于贾竖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1375927_comment'></div>是臣忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1375927_comment'></div>外戚之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1375927_comment'></div>上公是列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1375927_comment'></div>西汉则王根为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_295_1375927", 1375927, "Clauses/295/Comments/0")'>玉山</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1375927_comment'></div>东京则郭况制金穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1375927_comment'></div>国步将移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_297_1375927_comment'></div>天泽未歇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_298_1375927_comment'></div>不师殷鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_299_1375927_comment'></div>尚遵覆辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1375927_comment'></div>是臣忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1375927_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_302_1375927", 1375927, "Clauses/302/Comments/0")'>大乐</span>既没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1375927_comment'></div>淫声是起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1375927_comment'></div>宋都已改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1375927_comment'></div>行人贪贿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1375927_comment'></div>如斯陈国一时雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1375927_comment'></div>玉树后庭花至死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1375927_comment'></div>是臣忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1375927_comment'></div>先之而昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1375927_comment'></div>后之而亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1375927_comment'></div>先之者尧兴唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1375927_comment'></div>舜兴虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1375927_comment'></div>后之者癸丧夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1375927_comment'></div>辛丧商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1375927_comment'></div>故王之忧国者而日旰不食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1375927_comment'></div>士之忧位者而载贽出疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_316_1375927_comment'></div>鹑居●8766食者何汲汲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1375927_comment'></div>孔席墨突者何遑遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_318_1375927_comment'></div>故臣之忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_319_1375927_comment'></div>尽此而巳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_320_1375927_comment'></div>愿陛下忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_321_1375927_comment'></div>治可致乐康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_322_1375927_comment'></div>道可跻羲皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_323_1375927_comment'></div>则天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_324_1375927_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
钟祥
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c70dd324891a41909ff8aa7141fcb8fa_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c70dd324891a41909ff8aa7141fcb8fa");'><span id='c70dd324891a41909ff8aa7141fcb8fa_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=863')">863年</a>，30岁</div><div id='c70dd324891a41909ff8aa7141fcb8fa' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=863')">863年4月</a>　刺史郑诚建孟亭以纪念孟浩然，皮日休为作《郢州孟亭记》<div id='poem_1375943' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375943' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375943?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郢州孟亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（863年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375943")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375943_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375943'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375943'>明皇世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375943_comment'></div>章句之风大得建安体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375943_comment'></div>论者推李翰林杜工部为尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375943_comment'></div>介其间能不愧者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375943_comment'></div>惟吾乡之孟先生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375943_comment'></div>先生之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375943_comment'></div>遇景入咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375943_comment'></div>不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1375943", 1375943, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>拘奇抉异</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375943_comment'></div>令龌龊束人口者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375943_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1375943", 1375943, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>涵涵</span>然有干霄之兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375943_comment'></div>若公输氏当巧而不巧者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375943_comment'></div>北齐美萧悫芙蓉露下落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375943_comment'></div>杨柳月中疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375943_comment'></div>先生则有微云澹河汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375943_comment'></div>疏雨滴梧桐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375943_comment'></div>乐府美王融日霁沙屿明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375943_comment'></div>风动甘泉浊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375943_comment'></div>先生则有气蒸云梦泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375943_comment'></div>波撼岳阳城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375943_comment'></div>谢朓之诗句精者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375943_comment'></div>有露湿寒塘草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375943_comment'></div>月映清淮流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375943_comment'></div>先生则有荷风送香气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375943_comment'></div>竹露滴清响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375943_comment'></div>此与古人争胜于釐毫间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375943_comment'></div>他称是者众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375943_comment'></div>不可悉数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375943_comment'></div>呜乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375943_comment'></div>先生之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375943_comment'></div>复何言耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375943_comment'></div>谓乎贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375943_comment'></div>则天爵于身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375943_comment'></div>谓乎死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375943_comment'></div>则不朽于文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375943_comment'></div>为士之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375943_comment'></div>亦以至乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375943_comment'></div>先生襄阳人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1375943_comment'></div>日休襄阳人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1375943_comment'></div>既慕其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1375943_comment'></div>亦睹其貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1375943_comment'></div>盖仲尼思文王则嗜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1375943", 1375943, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>昌歜</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1375943_comment'></div>七十子思仲尼则师有若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1375943_comment'></div>吾于先生见之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1375943_comment'></div>说者曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1375943_comment'></div>王右丞笔先生貌于郢之亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1375943_comment'></div>每有观型之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1375943_comment'></div>四年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1375943_comment'></div>荣阳郑公诚刺是州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1375943_comment'></div>余将抵江南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1375943_comment'></div>𫇢舟而诣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1375943_comment'></div>果以文见贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1375943_comment'></div>则先生之貌纵视矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1375943_comment'></div>先是亭之名取先生之讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1375943_comment'></div>公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1375943_comment'></div>焉有贤者名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1375943_comment'></div>为趋厮走养朝夕言于刺史前耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1375943_comment'></div>命易之以先生姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1375943_comment'></div>日休时在宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1375943_comment'></div>因曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1375943_comment'></div>春秋书纪季公子友仲孙湫字者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1375943_comment'></div>贵之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1375943_comment'></div>故书名曰贬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1375943_comment'></div>书字曰贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1375943_comment'></div>况以贤者名署于亭乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1375943_comment'></div>君子是以知公乐善之深也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1375943_comment'></div>百祀之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1375943_comment'></div>一朝而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1375943_comment'></div>则民之弊也去之可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1375943_comment'></div>见善不书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1375943_comment'></div>非圣人之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1375943_comment'></div>宴豆既彻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1375943_comment'></div>立而为文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1375943_comment'></div>咸通四年四月三日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_72_1375943_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
岳阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='027ed63df9374cee8ecb28293ef70a99_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("027ed63df9374cee8ecb28293ef70a99");'><span id='027ed63df9374cee8ecb28293ef70a99_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=863')">863年</a>，30岁</div><div id='027ed63df9374cee8ecb28293ef70a99' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在竟陵短暂停留，继又南下洞庭，吊屈悼贾，有文。作品：九讽系述。反招魂。<div id='poem_1376036' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376036' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376036?labeling=true' target='_blank'>反招魂</a><span class='authorDate'>（863年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1376036")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376036_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1376036'>屈原作大招魂。(或曰景差作疑不能明)宋玉作招魂。皮子以为忠放不如守介而死。奚招魂为。故作反招魂一篇以辨之。词曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1376036_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376036'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376036'>承<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1376036", 1376036, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>溟涬</span>之命兮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1376036'>付余才而辅君。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1376036'>君既不得乎志兮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1376036'>余飘飘而播迁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1376036'>余将荡大空而就灭兮。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1376036'>君又招余俾复身。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1376036'>余诣帝以请诀兮。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1376036'>帝俾巫阳以筮云。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1376036'>巫阳语余以不可归兮。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1376036'>故作词以招君。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1376036'>乃下招曰。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1376036'>君兮归来。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1376036'>故都慎不可留些。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1376036'>其君雄虺兮。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1376036'>其民封狐些。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1376036'>食民之肝鬲以为其肉兮。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1376036'>摘民之发肤以为其衣些。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1376036'>朝刀锯而暮鼎镬兮。<div id='poem_sentence_17_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1376036'>上暧昧而下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1376036", 1376036, "Clauses/18/Comments/2")'>墨<span class='inlineComment2'>（眉）</span>杘</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（痴）</span>些。<div id='poem_sentence_18_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1376036'>君兮归来。<div id='poem_sentence_19_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1376036'>故都慎不可留些。<div id='poem_sentence_20_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1376036'>余昔为比干之魂兮。<div id='poem_sentence_21_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1376036'>干僇而余去些。<div id='poem_sentence_22_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1376036'>未闻干贪生以自招兮。<div id='poem_sentence_23_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1376036'>余竟洁其所处些。<div id='poem_sentence_24_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1376036'>君兮归来。<div id='poem_sentence_25_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1376036'>故都慎不可留些。<div id='poem_sentence_26_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1376036'>余昔为伍胥之魂兮。<div id='poem_sentence_27_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1376036'>胥僇而余逝些。<div id='poem_sentence_28_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1376036'>未闻胥贪位以惜生兮。<div id='poem_sentence_29_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1376036'>执属镂而不滞些。<div id='poem_sentence_30_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1376036'>君兮归来。<div id='poem_sentence_31_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1376036'>故都慎不可留些。<div id='poem_sentence_32_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1376036'>余昔为宏演之魂兮。<div id='poem_sentence_33_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1376036'>演自残而余行些。<div id='poem_sentence_34_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1376036'>未闻演惜命以不死兮。<div id='poem_sentence_35_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1376036'>俾其义而益明些。<div id='poem_sentence_36_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1376036'>君兮归来。<div id='poem_sentence_37_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1376036'>故都慎不可留些。<div id='poem_sentence_38_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1376036'>帝命余以辅君兮。<div id='poem_sentence_39_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_1376036'>亦以君之忠介自。<div id='poem_sentence_40_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1376036'>今以忠而见闻兮。<div id='poem_sentence_41_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_1376036'>尚盘桓而有待些。<div id='poem_sentence_42_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1376036'>将自富贵而入羁旅兮。<div id='poem_sentence_43_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1376036'>其志乃悔些。<div id='poem_sentence_44_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_1376036'>将恋骨肉而惜家族兮。<div id='poem_sentence_45_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1376036'>何不自裁些。<div id='poem_sentence_46_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_1376036'>枭食母而獍食父兮。<div id='poem_sentence_47_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_1376036'>见禽兽之为生些。<div id='poem_sentence_48_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1376036'>苟残者眉寿兮。<div id='poem_sentence_49_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_1376036'>实枭獍而同名些。<div id='poem_sentence_50_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1376036'>君乎慎勿怀故都之恋归来乎。<div id='poem_sentence_51_1376036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_1376036'>余为君存千古忠烈之荣名些。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1376036_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南京
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='dcdefbc1dbbb412d839ebba70303c090_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dcdefbc1dbbb412d839ebba70303c090");'><span id='dcdefbc1dbbb412d839ebba70303c090_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=863')">863年</a>，30岁</div><div id='dcdefbc1dbbb412d839ebba70303c090' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，至白门，游栖霞山寺，有诗。作品：白门表。游栖霞寺。<div id='poem_1375931' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375931' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375931?labeling=true' target='_blank'>白门表</a><span class='authorDate'>（863年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375931")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375931_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375931'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375931'>三年秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375931_comment'></div>徐卒无状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375931_comment'></div>叛兵逐其帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375931_comment'></div>不再日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375931_comment'></div>剽公私财析尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375931_comment'></div>异时卒有不平者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375931_comment'></div>至是皆门抗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375931_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1375931", 1375931, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>监戎</span>者以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375931_comment'></div>上赫然大怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375931_comment'></div>命大将职正其罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375931_comment'></div>卒有首叛者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375931_comment'></div>前后累劫其将曰银刀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375931_comment'></div>至是命皆僇之无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375931_comment'></div>赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375931_comment'></div>将至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375931_comment'></div>先令徐裨将曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375931_comment'></div>银刀族无老幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375931_comment'></div>强者斩之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375931_comment'></div>弱者幽之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375931_comment'></div>及徐之枝邑派聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375931_comment'></div>捕银刀族且尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375931_comment'></div>或僇而枭者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375931_comment'></div>或拲而送者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375931_comment'></div>不浃日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375931_comment'></div>其族无馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375931_comment'></div>或有诈弱惧僇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375931_comment'></div>皆论幽于牢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375931_comment'></div>迨六七百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375931_comment'></div>且俟大将命业兵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375931_comment'></div>居无何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375931_comment'></div>上悯徐卒尽死中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375931_comment'></div>或有不干其谋者偕僇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375931_comment'></div>降内贵人于徐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375931_comment'></div>诏曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375931_comment'></div>银刀族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375931_comment'></div>诏至未死者贳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375931_comment'></div>六七百人分属数郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1375931_comment'></div>未至属所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1375931_comment'></div>途亡为盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1375931_comment'></div>四年夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1375931_comment'></div>盗推其率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1375931_comment'></div>鼓而徐入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1375931_comment'></div>火里舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1375931_comment'></div>将县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1375931_comment'></div>诛制使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1375931_comment'></div>系虏民辎而掠货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1375931_comment'></div>徐守闭中城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1375931_comment'></div>竟不命偏将御之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1375931_comment'></div>盗得志徐去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1375931_comment'></div>四年秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1375931_comment'></div>进士皮日休之白门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1375931_comment'></div>道逢徐民之耄者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1375931_comment'></div>泣曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1375931_comment'></div>翁世富于徐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1375931_comment'></div>子孙嗣其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1375931_comment'></div>祈二百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1375931_comment'></div>前日以徐卒乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1375931_comment'></div>翁之资已竭劫于兵矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1375931_comment'></div>独存者居第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1375931_comment'></div>而已为残烬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1375931_comment'></div>翁以为天子命将尽杀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1375931_comment'></div>且银刀族无三千人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1375931_comment'></div>遇圣天子在上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1375931_comment'></div>四境无征伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1375931_comment'></div>重粮其属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1375931_comment'></div>厚衣其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1375931_comment'></div>有餔儿啜孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1375931_comment'></div>至死手不执干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1375931_comment'></div>体不被铠甲者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1375931_comment'></div>上于徐卒厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1375931_comment'></div>今乃忘上恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1375931_comment'></div>叛主帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1375931_comment'></div>逐天子命将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1375931_comment'></div>残天子兆民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1375931_comment'></div>如此逆之甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1375931_comment'></div>上又活其半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1375931_comment'></div>今反盗而寇徐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1375931_comment'></div>前日翁之亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1375931_comment'></div>独贿与产耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1375931_comment'></div>今子孙为贼隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1375931_comment'></div>妻女为贼室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1375931_comment'></div>馀骸残齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1375931_comment'></div>溘然无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1375931_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1375931_comment'></div>皇天仁于数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1375931_comment'></div>反不仁于一郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1375931_comment'></div>岂得言者过耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1375931_comment'></div>且兵者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1375931_comment'></div>圣王不能免其征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1375931_comment'></div>仁帝不能无其伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1375931_comment'></div>是以逆者必杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1375931_comment'></div>顺者必生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1375931_comment'></div>所以示天下不私也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1375931_comment'></div>往年数万之卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1375931_comment'></div>逐天子命将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1375931_comment'></div>自树其便者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1375931_comment'></div>国家以不忍尽杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1375931_comment'></div>因听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1375931_comment'></div>皆贼而不贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1375931_comment'></div>兵而不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1375931_comment'></div>死而辄代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1375931_comment'></div>名为列藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1375931_comment'></div>实一州之主也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1375931_comment'></div>故春秋讥世卿得专公禄者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1375931_comment'></div>以春秋小国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1375931_comment'></div>尚贬而不空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1375931_comment'></div>况今圣天子在上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1375931_comment'></div>百执事称职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1375931_comment'></div>万方雀息以无虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1375931_comment'></div>四夷骏奔而入贡哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1375931_comment'></div>前日徐卒幸活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1375931_comment'></div>而为盗于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1375931_comment'></div>特苦国家无辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1375931_comment'></div>或不尽僇而赦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1375931_comment'></div>则自树其便者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1375931_comment'></div>日休曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1375931_comment'></div>翁其力之贤者耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1375931_comment'></div>吾知夫今之食其食者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1375931_comment'></div>未必有翁之是心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1375931_comment'></div>幸以文贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1375931_comment'></div>而未得入上言列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1375931_comment'></div>固不合陈便宜事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1375931_comment'></div>因采翁之说为表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1375931_comment'></div>庶天子召直言极谏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1375931_comment'></div>得以遗之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_124_1375931_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15541' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15541' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15541?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游栖霞寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（863年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15541")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_15541_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15541'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15541'>不见明居士，空山但寂寥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15541'>白莲吟次缺，青霭坐来销。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15541'>泉冷无三伏，松枯有六朝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15541'>何时石上月，相对论逍遥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15541'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_15541'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(15541)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
寿县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ae306ef0278b4fdbb8b65bb4a75faa31_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ae306ef0278b4fdbb8b65bb4a75faa31");'><span id='ae306ef0278b4fdbb8b65bb4a75faa31_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=864')">863-864年</a>，30-31岁</div><div id='ae306ef0278b4fdbb8b65bb4a75faa31' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=863')">863年</a>　冬，至寿州；岁末，再自寿州之江右。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=864&endYear=864')">864年</a>　春，皮日休自寿州之江右而道出英六城下，访咎繇庙，作《咎繇碑》<div id='poem_1376075' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376075' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376075?labeling=true' target='_blank'>咎繇碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（864年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1376075")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376075_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376075'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376075'>噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376075_comment'></div>谆谆之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376075_comment'></div>必归于德盛者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376075_comment'></div>出不徒然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376075_comment'></div>上应运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376075_comment'></div>次命代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376075_comment'></div>苟非相者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376075_comment'></div>数十祀翼出于一时者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376075_comment'></div>其运与命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376075_comment'></div>彼失此得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376075_comment'></div>彼得此失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376075_comment'></div>咸在乎谆谆之命焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376075_comment'></div>奚在归乎德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376075_comment'></div>夫帝挚之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376075_comment'></div>不盛于尧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376075_comment'></div>尧而得焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376075_comment'></div>十六族之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376075_comment'></div>不盛于舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376075_comment'></div>舜而得焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376075_comment'></div>至于咎繇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376075_comment'></div>德齐于舜禹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376075_comment'></div>道超乎稷启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376075_comment'></div>禹荐于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376075_comment'></div>不命而殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376075_comment'></div>则谆谆之命奚归乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376075_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376075_comment'></div>天何为哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376075_comment'></div>不付咎繇之命者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376075_comment'></div>将欲空授天下哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376075_comment'></div>未必独死咎繇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376075_comment'></div>设咎繇得天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376075_comment'></div>其暮必荐益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376075_comment'></div>益得天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376075_comment'></div>其暮之荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376075_comment'></div>必有其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376075_comment'></div>自咎繇之降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376075_comment'></div>空授之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376075_comment'></div>其暴民黩天者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376075_comment'></div>可忍言也哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376075_comment'></div>太史公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376075_comment'></div>禹封咎繇之后于英六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376075_comment'></div>五年春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376075_comment'></div>日休自淝陵之江左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376075_comment'></div>道出英六城下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376075_comment'></div>因求遗实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376075_comment'></div>厥祀存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376075_comment'></div>乃絓马于古木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376075_comment'></div>再拜于庙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376075_comment'></div>退而碑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376075_comment'></div>请枞阳小尹刊于壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376075_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376075_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1376075'>惟天降圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376075_comment'></div>不锡厥命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376075_comment'></div>一篇帝谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376075_comment'></div>百王之镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376075_comment'></div>禹有奚遏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376075_comment'></div>荐之不定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376075_comment'></div>启有令德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376075_comment'></div>受之而正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376075_comment'></div>已矣何伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376075_comment'></div>明德逾盛。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1376075_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='0ca7521657024e288c69e2a078c0e173_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0ca7521657024e288c69e2a078c0e173");'><span id='0ca7521657024e288c69e2a078c0e173_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=865&endYear=865')">865年</a>，32岁</div><div id='0ca7521657024e288c69e2a078c0e173' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=865&endYear=865')">865年8月</a>　皮日休得寿州刺史杨某之助，并寓寿州州东别墅；并取乡贡资格。作品：何武传。<div id='poem_1376081' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376081' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376081?labeling=true' target='_blank'>何武传</a><span class='authorDate'>（865年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1376081")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376081_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376081'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376081'>何武者。寿之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1376081", 1376081, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>骁卒</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376081_comment'></div>故为步卒将。戍邻霍岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376081_comment'></div>岳生名荈。有负其贩者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376081_comment'></div>多强暴民。民不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376081_comment'></div>必愬于将。武之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376081_comment'></div>责其强暴者。尽擒而械之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376081_comment'></div>俟簿圆。将申寿守请杀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376081_comment'></div>强暴之党惧且死。乃诬愬武于寿守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376081_comment'></div>且曰。不顺守命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376081_comment'></div>擅生杀于外。寿之守<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1376081", 1376081, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>严悍</span>不可犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376081_comment'></div>苟闻不便于民。虽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1376081", 1376081, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>剧寮</span>贵吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376081_comment'></div>皆得辱杀之。至是闻武罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376081_comment'></div>如乳虎遇触。怒蝮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1376081", 1376081, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>遭伤</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376081_comment'></div>其将害也可知。乃命功卒将命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376081_comment'></div>拲武至府。武巳知理可申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376081_comment'></div>不柰守<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1376081", 1376081, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>严悍</span>。必当受枉刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376081_comment'></div>乃乐而俟死矣。至则守怒而责武以其过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376081_comment'></div>武善媚对。又肢体魁然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376081_comment'></div>乃投石状枉之事。守雅爱是类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376081_comment'></div>翻然释之。黜其职一级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376081_comment'></div>武曰。吾今日不归地下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376081_comment'></div>真守之赐也。请得以命报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376081_comment'></div>居未久。寿之指邑曰枞阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376081_comment'></div>野寇四起。其邑将危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376081_comment'></div>武请于守曰。此真某毕命之秋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376081_comment'></div>守壮之。复其故职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376081_comment'></div>奉命为贰将。领偏师自间道入枞阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376081_comment'></div>不意伏盗发于丛翳间。兵尽骇逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376081_comment'></div>武独斗死。日休曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376081_comment'></div>武之受谤。不当其刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376081_comment'></div>况其死乎。如非武心者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376081_comment'></div>纵免死。其心不能无愤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376081_comment'></div>况<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1376081", 1376081, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>感分</span>用命哉。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376081_comment'></div>古之士事上<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1376081", 1376081, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>遇谤</span>。当职<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1376081", 1376081, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>遭辱</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376081_comment'></div>苟其君免之。必以愤报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376081_comment'></div>破家亡国者。可胜道哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376081_comment'></div>春秋弑其君三十六。其中未必不由是而致者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376081_comment'></div>武一卒也。独有是心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376081_comment'></div>呜呼。今之士事上当职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376081_comment'></div>苟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1376081", 1376081, "Clauses/78/Comments/0")'>遇谤</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1376081", 1376081, "Clauses/78/Comments/1")'>遭辱</span>无是心者。吾又不知武一卒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376081_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1376081_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='7bf35b1c8d1148bab463d072082d1384_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7bf35b1c8d1148bab463d072082d1384");'><span id='7bf35b1c8d1148bab463d072082d1384_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=866&endYear=866')">866年</a>，33岁</div><div id='7bf35b1c8d1148bab463d072082d1384' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>科举不第后归寿州，寓州东别墅，是年淮右蝗旱，颍水流域百姓流离失所，皮日休作《三羞诗》之“天子丙戍年”以吊民之痛。作品：三羞诗（吾闻古君子）三羞诗（天子丙戌岁）<div id='poem_15587' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15587' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15587?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三羞诗三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（866年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15587")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15587_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_15587'>丙戌岁，日休射策不上，东退于肥陵，出都门，见朝列中论犯当权者，得罪南窜。卯诏辰发，持法吏不容一息留私室。视其色，若将厌禄位、悔名望者。皮子窥之，惄然泣，衄然羞，故作是诗以赆之。</div><div id='poem_preface_15587_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_15587'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2805, "poem_allusion_15587")'>方寸</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_15587_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15587'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15587'>吾闻古君子，介介励其节。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15587'>入门疑储宫，抚己思鈇钺。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15587'>志<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作忠）</span>者若不退，佞者何由达。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15587'>君臣一殽膳，家国共残杀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15587'>此道见于今，永思心若裂。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15587'>王臣方謇謇，佐我无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_15587", 15587, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>玷缺</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15587'>如何以谋计，中道生<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_15587", 15587, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>芽蘖</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15587'>宪司遵故典，分道播南越。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15587'>苍惶出<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_15587", 15587, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>班行</span>，家室不容别。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15587'>玄鬓行为霜，清泪立成血。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15587'>乘遽剧飞鸟，就传过风发。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15587'>嗟吾何为者，叨在造士列。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15587'>献文不上第，归于淮之汭。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15587'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_15587", 15587, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>蹇蹄</span>可再奔，退羽可后歇。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15587'>利则侣轩裳，塞则友松月。<div id='poem_sentence_14_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15587'>而于<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2805, "poem_sentence_15_15587")'>方寸</span>内，未有是<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_15587", 15587, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>愁结</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_15_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_15587'>未为禄食仕，俯不愧梁粝。<div id='poem_sentence_16_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_15587'>未为冠冕人，死不惭忠烈。<div id='poem_sentence_17_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_15587'>如何有是心，不能叩丹阙。<div id='poem_sentence_18_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_15587'>赫赫负君归，南山采芝蕨。<div id='poem_sentence_19_15587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_15587'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_15587_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15588' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15588' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15588?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（866年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15588_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15588'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15588'>南荒不择吏，致我交阯覆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15588'>绵联三四年，流为中夏辱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15588'>懦者斗即退，武者兵则黩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15588'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_15588", 15588, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>军庸</span>满天下，战将多金玉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15588'>刮则齐民痈，分为猛士禄。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15588'>雄健许昌师，忠武冠其族。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15588'>去为万骑风，住作一川肉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15588'>昨朝残卒回，千门万户哭。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15588'>哀声动闾里，怨气成山谷。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15588'>谁能听昼鼙，不忍看金镞。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15588'>吾有制胜术，不奈贱碌碌。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15588'>贮之胸臆间，惭见许师属。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15588'>自嗟胡为者，得蹑前修躅。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15588'>家不出军租，身不识部曲。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15588'>亦衣许师衣，亦食许师粟。<div id='poem_sentence_14_15588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15588'>方知古人道，荫我已为足。<div id='poem_sentence_15_15588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_15588'>念此向谁羞，悠悠颍川绿。<div id='poem_sentence_16_15588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_15588'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_15588_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15589' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15589' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15589?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（866年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15589_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15589'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15589'>天子丙戌年，淮右民多饥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15589'>就中颍之汭，转徙何累累。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15589'>夫妇相顾亡，弃却抱中儿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15589'>兄弟各自散，出门如大痴。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15589'>一金易芦卜，一缣换凫茈。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15589'>荒村墓鸟树，空屋野花篱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15589'>儿童齧草根，倚桑空羸羸。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15589'>斑白死路傍，枕土皆离离。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15589'>方知圣人教，于民良在斯。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15589'>厉能去人爱，荒能夺人慈。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15589'>如何司牧者，有术皆在兹。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15589'>粤吾何为人，数亩清溪湄。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15589'>一写落第文，一家欢复嬉。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15589'>朝食有麦饘，晨起有布衣。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15589'>一身既饱暖，一家无怨咨。<div id='poem_sentence_14_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15589'>家虽有畎亩，手不秉镃基。<div id='poem_sentence_15_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_15589'>岁虽有札瘥，庖不废晨炊。<div id='poem_sentence_16_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_15589'>何道以致是，我有明公知。<div id='poem_sentence_17_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_15589'>食之以侯食，衣之以侯衣。<div id='poem_sentence_18_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_15589'>归时恤金帛，使我奉庭闱。<div id='poem_sentence_19_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_15589'>抚己愧颍民，奚不进德为。<div id='poem_sentence_20_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_15589'>因兹感知己，尽日空涕洟。<div id='poem_sentence_21_15589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_15589'></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_15589_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>仿中唐文人元结编辑《文编》之例，编辑其以往诗文，成省卷《皮子文薮》十卷。作品：文薮序。<div id='poem_1375939' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375939' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375939?labeling=true' target='_blank'>文薮序</a><span class='authorDate'>（866年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375939")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375939_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375939'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375939'>咸通丙戌中。日休射策不上第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375939_comment'></div>退归州来别墅。编次其文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375939_comment'></div>复将贡于有司。登箧丛萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375939_comment'></div>繁如薮泽。因名其书曰文薮焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375939_comment'></div>比见元次山纳文编于有司。侍郎杨公浚见文编叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375939_comment'></div>上第污元子耳。斯文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375939_comment'></div>不敢希杨公之叹。希当时作者一知耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375939_comment'></div>赋者古诗之流也。伤前王太佚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375939_comment'></div>作忧赋。虑民道难济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375939_comment'></div>作河桥赋。念下情不达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375939_comment'></div>作霍山赋。悯寒士道壅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375939_comment'></div>作桃花赋。离骚者文之菁英者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375939_comment'></div>伤于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1375939", 1375939, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>宏奥</span>。今也不显离骚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375939_comment'></div>作九讽。文贵穷理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375939_comment'></div>理贵原情。作十原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375939_comment'></div>大乐既亡。至音不嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375939_comment'></div>作补周礼九夏歌。两汉庸儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375939_comment'></div>贱我左氏。作春秋决疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375939_comment'></div>其馀碑铭赞颂。论议书序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375939_comment'></div>皆上剥远非。下补近失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375939_comment'></div>非空言也。较其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375939_comment'></div>可在古人之后矣。古风诗编之文末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375939_comment'></div>俾视之粗俊于口也。亦由食鱼遇鲭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375939_comment'></div>持肉偶。皮子世录著之于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375939_comment'></div>亦太史公自序之意也。凡二百篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375939_comment'></div>为十卷。览者无诮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375939_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1375939_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
石台（石埭）
-----detail
