ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=864&endYear=864')">864年</a>　移书元征君某。<div id='poem_1375932' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375932' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375932?labeling=true' target='_blank'>移元徵君书</a><span class='authorDate'>（864年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375932")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375932_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375932'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375932'>徵君足下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375932_comment'></div>行奇操峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375932_comment'></div>舍明天子贤宰相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375932_comment'></div>退隐于陵阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375932_comment'></div>踞见青山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375932_comment'></div>傲视白云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375932_comment'></div>得丧不可摇其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375932_comment'></div>荣辱不能动其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375932_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1375932", 1375932, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>桎拲</span>冠冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375932_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1375932", 1375932, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>泥滓</span>禄位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375932_comment'></div>甚善甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375932_comment'></div>苟与足下同道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375932_comment'></div>必汲汲自退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375932_comment'></div>名惟恐闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375932_comment'></div>行惟恐显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375932_comment'></div>老死为山谷人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375932_comment'></div>或名欲遗千载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375932_comment'></div>利欲及当今者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375932_comment'></div>闻足下之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375932_comment'></div>可以不进其说耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375932_comment'></div>日休闻古之圣贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375932_comment'></div>无不欲有意于民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375932_comment'></div>苟或退者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375932_comment'></div>是时弊不可正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375932_comment'></div>主惛不可晓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375932_comment'></div>进则祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375932_comment'></div>退则安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375932_comment'></div>斯或隐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375932_comment'></div>有是者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375932_comment'></div>世不可知其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375932_comment'></div>俗不能得其教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375932_comment'></div>尚惧来世圣人责乎无意于民故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375932_comment'></div>此谓之道隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375932_comment'></div>其次者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375932_comment'></div>行不端于巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375932_comment'></div>名不闻于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375932_comment'></div>欲乎仕则惧祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1375932_comment'></div>欲乎退则思进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1375932_comment'></div>必为怪行以动俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1375932_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1375932", 1375932, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>诙言</span>以矫物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1375932_comment'></div>上则邀天子再三之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1375932_comment'></div>下则取诸侯殷勤之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1375932_comment'></div>甚有百世之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1375932_comment'></div>次有当时之誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1375932_comment'></div>此之谓名隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1375932_comment'></div>其次者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1375932_comment'></div>行有过僻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1375932_comment'></div>志有深傲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1375932_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1375932", 1375932, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>饰身</span>不由乎礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1375932_comment'></div>行巳不在乎是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1375932_comment'></div>入其室者惟清风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1375932_comment'></div>升其牖者惟明月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1375932_comment'></div>木石然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1375932_comment'></div>糜鹿然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1375932_comment'></div>期夫道家之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1375932_comment'></div>以全彼生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1375932_comment'></div>此之谓性隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1375932_comment'></div>然而道隐者贤人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1375932_comment'></div>名隐者小人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1375932_comment'></div>性隐者野人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1375932_comment'></div>有夫尧舜救世汤禹拯乱之心者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1375932_comment'></div>视道隐之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1375932_comment'></div>由夫樵苏之民耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1375932_comment'></div>况名与性哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1375932_comment'></div>今天下虽无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1375932_comment'></div>河湟有黠虏之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1375932_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1375932", 1375932, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>岭徼</span>有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1375932", 1375932, "Clauses/66/Comments/1")'>逋蛮</span>之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1375932_comment'></div>主上焦心灼思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1375932_comment'></div>晏询夜谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1375932_comment'></div>宰相战慄于岩廊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1375932_comment'></div>百执事奔走于朝右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1375932_comment'></div>然尚未复贞观开元之大治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1375932_comment'></div>有致君于唐虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1375932_comment'></div>跻民于仁寿者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1375932_comment'></div>其人则鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1375932_comment'></div>其求则勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1375932_comment'></div>元纁之聘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1375932_comment'></div>屡降于山林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1375932_comment'></div>少微之星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1375932_comment'></div>但明于霄汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1375932_comment'></div>此真足下之所高视也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1375932_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1375932_comment'></div>斯时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1375932_comment'></div>山林之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1375932_comment'></div>宜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_84_1375932", 1375932, "Clauses/84/Comments/0")'>倒衣</span>以接礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1375932_comment'></div>重趼以应命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1375932_comment'></div>赴明天子千年之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1375932_comment'></div>成大丈夫万世之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1375932_comment'></div>勋铭于钟鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1375932_comment'></div>德著于竹帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1375932_comment'></div>可不盛哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1375932_comment'></div>夫主上知足下之道久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1375932_comment'></div>加以郡守荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1375932_comment'></div>宰相誉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1375932_comment'></div>虽锡命屡颁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1375932_comment'></div>而高风转固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1375932_comment'></div>接物日简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1375932_comment'></div>入山益深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1375932_comment'></div>且足下将为道隐乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1375932_comment'></div>则道隐者世不可知其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1375932_comment'></div>俗不能得其尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1375932_comment'></div>足下之名尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1375932_comment'></div>丹青于世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1375932_comment'></div>岂谓道隐哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1375932_comment'></div>将为名隐乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1375932_comment'></div>则名隐者以怪行动俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1375932_comment'></div>以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_106_1375932", 1375932, "Clauses/106/Comments/0")'>诙言</span>矫物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1375932_comment'></div>足下之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1375932_comment'></div>伸之而伊夔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1375932_comment'></div>屈之而夷齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1375932_comment'></div>岂谓名隐哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1375932_comment'></div>将为性隐乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1375932_comment'></div>则性隐者<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_112_1375932", 1375932, "Clauses/112/Comments/0")'>饰身</span>不由乎礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1375932_comment'></div>行巳不在乎是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1375932_comment'></div>足下顷荐名于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1375932_comment'></div>客位于侯伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1375932_comment'></div>岂所谓性隐乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1375932_comment'></div>然三隐者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1375932_comment'></div>足下皆出其表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1375932_comment'></div>复何为而高卧哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1375932_comment'></div>如终卧陵阳而不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1375932_comment'></div>是废乎古人之道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1375932_comment'></div>仲尼曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1375932_comment'></div>素隐行怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1375932_comment'></div>后世有述焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1375932_comment'></div>吾弗为之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1375932_comment'></div>君子<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_126_1375932", 1375932, "Clauses/126/Comments/0")'>遵道</span>而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1375932_comment'></div>半途而废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1375932_comment'></div>吾弗能巳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1375932_comment'></div>君子依乎中庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1375932_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_130_1375932", 1375932, "Clauses/130/Comments/0")'>遁世</span>不见知而不悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1375932_comment'></div>夫前二者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1375932_comment'></div>圣人之所不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1375932_comment'></div>足下之学杨墨乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1375932_comment'></div>申韩乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1375932_comment'></div>何其悖于道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1375932_comment'></div>如<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_136_1375932", 1375932, "Clauses/136/Comments/0")'>遁世</span>不见知而不悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1375932_comment'></div>则舜不为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_137_1375932", 1375932, "Clauses/137/Comments/0")'>高蹈</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1375932_comment'></div>舜不为真隐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1375932_comment'></div>足下其亦有意乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1375932_comment'></div>如纳仆之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1375932_comment'></div>翻然而起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1375932_comment'></div>醒然而用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1375932_comment'></div>朝庭必处足下于大谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1375932_comment'></div>次用足下于宰辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1375932_comment'></div>其在大谏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1375932_comment'></div>以直气吹日月之翳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1375932_comment'></div>以正道立天地之根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1375932_comment'></div>先黜陟于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1375932_comment'></div>次按察于侯国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1375932_comment'></div>其在宰辅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1375932_comment'></div>外以道宁四夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1375932_comment'></div>内以法提百揆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1375932_comment'></div>俾天地反妖为瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1375932_comment'></div>使阴阳易愆为穰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1375932_comment'></div>然后以元菟乐浪为持节之州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1375932_comment'></div>昆崙崦嵫作驻跸之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1375932_comment'></div>又不知房杜姚宋何人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1375932_comment'></div>果行是道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1375932_comment'></div>罄南山之竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1375932_comment'></div>不足以书足下之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1375932_comment'></div>穷百谷之波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1375932_comment'></div>不足以注足下之善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1375932_comment'></div>以足下之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1375932_comment'></div>可以知仆之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1375932_comment'></div>以仆之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1375932_comment'></div>可以发足下之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1375932_comment'></div>故不远千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1375932_comment'></div>授书于御者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1375932_comment'></div>用以吐仆臆中之奇贮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1375932_comment'></div>仆之取舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1375932_comment'></div>自有方寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1375932_comment'></div>异时无望于足下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1375932_comment'></div>发函之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1375932_comment'></div>但起无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1375932_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1375932_comment'></div>日休再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_176_1375932_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
枞阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='79c155d93f4f4eb7ac033f9194bb4059_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("79c155d93f4f4eb7ac033f9194bb4059");'><span id='79c155d93f4f4eb7ac033f9194bb4059_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=864&endYear=864')">864年</a>，31岁</div><div id='79c155d93f4f4eb7ac033f9194bb4059' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>刊《咎繇碑》于县壁，又作《补大戴礼祭法文》作品：咎繇碑。补大戴礼祭法文。<div id='poem_1376075' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376075' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376075?labeling=true' target='_blank'>咎繇碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（864年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1376075")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376075_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376075'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376075'>噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376075_comment'></div>谆谆之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376075_comment'></div>必归于德盛者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376075_comment'></div>出不徒然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376075_comment'></div>上应运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376075_comment'></div>次命代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376075_comment'></div>苟非相者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376075_comment'></div>数十祀翼出于一时者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376075_comment'></div>其运与命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376075_comment'></div>彼失此得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376075_comment'></div>彼得此失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376075_comment'></div>咸在乎谆谆之命焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376075_comment'></div>奚在归乎德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376075_comment'></div>夫帝挚之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376075_comment'></div>不盛于尧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376075_comment'></div>尧而得焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376075_comment'></div>十六族之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376075_comment'></div>不盛于舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376075_comment'></div>舜而得焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376075_comment'></div>至于咎繇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376075_comment'></div>德齐于舜禹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376075_comment'></div>道超乎稷启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376075_comment'></div>禹荐于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376075_comment'></div>不命而殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376075_comment'></div>则谆谆之命奚归乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376075_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376075_comment'></div>天何为哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376075_comment'></div>不付咎繇之命者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376075_comment'></div>将欲空授天下哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376075_comment'></div>未必独死咎繇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376075_comment'></div>设咎繇得天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376075_comment'></div>其暮必荐益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376075_comment'></div>益得天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376075_comment'></div>其暮之荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376075_comment'></div>必有其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376075_comment'></div>自咎繇之降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376075_comment'></div>空授之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376075_comment'></div>其暴民黩天者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376075_comment'></div>可忍言也哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376075_comment'></div>太史公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376075_comment'></div>禹封咎繇之后于英六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376075_comment'></div>五年春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376075_comment'></div>日休自淝陵之江左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376075_comment'></div>道出英六城下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376075_comment'></div>因求遗实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376075_comment'></div>厥祀存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376075_comment'></div>乃絓马于古木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376075_comment'></div>再拜于庙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376075_comment'></div>退而碑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376075_comment'></div>请枞阳小尹刊于壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376075_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376075_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1376075'>惟天降圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376075_comment'></div>不锡厥命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376075_comment'></div>一篇帝谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376075_comment'></div>百王之镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376075_comment'></div>禹有奚遏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376075_comment'></div>荐之不定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376075_comment'></div>启有令德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376075_comment'></div>受之而正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376075_comment'></div>已矣何伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376075_comment'></div>明德逾盛。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1376075_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1375967' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375967' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375967?labeling=true' target='_blank'>补大戴礼祭法文</a><span class='authorDate'>（864年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375967")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375967_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375967'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375967'>祭法曰。法施于人则祀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375967_comment'></div>咎繇作帝谟。为士师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375967_comment'></div>其道参乎舜禹。不曰法施于人乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375967_comment'></div>何祀典之阙哉。祭法曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375967_comment'></div>能御大灾则祀之。尧舜之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375967_comment'></div>山林蕃。鸟兽暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375967_comment'></div>益作虞也。山林疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375967_comment'></div>鸟兽鲜。人民安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375967_comment'></div>不曰能御大灾乎。何祀典之阙哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375967_comment'></div>祭法曰。以劳定国则祀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375967_comment'></div>昔者周公辅武以宁殷乱。佐成而立周业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375967_comment'></div>制礼乐。立明堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375967_comment'></div>不曰以劳定国乎。何祀典之阙哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375967_comment'></div>如以咎繇伯益之功小于舜禹。不在祀典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375967_comment'></div>则契为司徒而民成。咎繇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375967_comment'></div>冥勤其官而水死。伯益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375967_comment'></div>如以圣人制礼。自有七庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375967_comment'></div>不合列在祀典。则文王以文治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375967_comment'></div>武王以武功。周公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375967_comment'></div>如皆以功烈列于民者。则吾之先师仲尼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375967_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1375967", 1375967, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>迈德</span>于百王。垂化于万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375967_comment'></div>孰不若契为司徒冥勤其官也哉。日休惧圣人之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375967_comment'></div>将乱而坠。敢参补而附之文曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375967_comment'></div>咎繇能平其法以位终。益能立其功以让禹政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375967_comment'></div>周公以文化。仲尼以德成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375967_comment'></div>非此族也。不在祀典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375967_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1375967_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
霍山
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='52f7496e5fb046d3aca74278f36413b7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("52f7496e5fb046d3aca74278f36413b7");'><span id='52f7496e5fb046d3aca74278f36413b7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=865&endYear=865')">865年</a>，32岁</div><div id='52f7496e5fb046d3aca74278f36413b7' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>皮日休至淝陵，途经霍山，为获幸令狐绹氏作《霍山赋》作品：霍山赋。春申君碑。<div id='poem_1375926' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375926' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375926?labeling=true' target='_blank'>霍山赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（865年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375926")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375926_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1375926'>臣日休以文为命士。所至州县山川。未尝不求其风谣。以颂以文。幸上发輶轩使。得采以闻。六年。至寿之骈邑曰霍山。山故岳也。邑赘于阯。至之二日。离邑一舍。望乎岳。将颂之文也。及见之。则目乎戆。手乎亸。心乎耸。神乎瞀。始欲狂其文。写其状。如丹青之不差也。颂其风。文其谣。如金石之永播也。既而其精怯然搏敌。躁然械囚。纷然棼丝。恍然堕空。浩然涉溟。幽然久疹。则知才智之劣。如髦而加疾。将杖而奔者。于戏。霍山之灵哉。霍山之灵哉。将阏于神而愚之邪。抑有所达而托之邪。其辰既浃。其精忽渝。怯然而胜。躁然而适。纷然而静。恍然而安。浩然而济。幽然而愈。如壮而能决。将阵而敌者。于是狂其文。写其状。其词曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1375926_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375926'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375926'>太始之气。有清有浊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375926_comment'></div>结浊为山。峻清为岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375926_comment'></div>其山厥臣。其岳惟君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375926_comment'></div>惟南之镇。曰霍为尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375926_comment'></div>岳之大。与地角壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375926_comment'></div>与天勍势。荆豫华嵩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375926_comment'></div>青沂兖岱。如垤而秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375926_comment'></div>如块而锐。岳之高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375926_comment'></div>千仞万仞。苍苍茫茫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375926_comment'></div>日月相避其光。望之数百里外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375926_comment'></div>为天栋梁。岳之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375926_comment'></div>端然<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1375926", 1375926, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>御极</span>。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1375926", 1375926, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>耸然</span>正位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375926_comment'></div>静然而听。凝然而视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375926_comment'></div>其体当中。如君之毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375926_comment'></div>其属者如骈其拇。如枝其指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375926_comment'></div>若卑其仪。若肃其位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375926_comment'></div>岳之气。其秀如春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375926_comment'></div>其清若秋。其翠如云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375926_comment'></div>云不能丽。其色如烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375926_comment'></div>烟不能鲜。若雨收气爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375926_comment'></div>丹青满天。岳之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375926_comment'></div>其神不眹。其报如响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375926_comment'></div>若雨用淫。岳能霁之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375926_comment'></div>若岁用旱。岳能泽之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375926_comment'></div>岳之德。生之育之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375926_comment'></div>煦之和之。开蘤染卉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375926_comment'></div>萋萋迷迷。藻绘数百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375926_comment'></div>岳之形。有云<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1375926", 1375926, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>骛骛</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375926_comment'></div>其勃如怒。有泉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1375926", 1375926, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>烈烈</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375926_comment'></div>其来如决。叱<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1375926", 1375926, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>丰隆</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375926_comment'></div>奔列缺。轰然霹雳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375926_comment'></div>天地俱裂。岳之异状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375926_comment'></div>其势如危。或不可支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375926_comment'></div>若不可维。或仰而呀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375926_comment'></div>有如吮空。或俯而拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375926_comment'></div>有如攫地。其晓而东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375926_comment'></div>有如冠日。其暮而西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1375926_comment'></div>有如孕月。有水而脉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1375926_comment'></div>有石而骨。有洞而腹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1375926_comment'></div>有堮而节。或锐而励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1375926_comment'></div>或断而截。或回而驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1375926_comment'></div>或低而折。其经之怪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1375926_comment'></div>祥之诡之。千种万类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1375926_comment'></div>繄不可得而详记。因神狂不能自主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1375926_comment'></div>殆而寐。梦一人绛衣朱冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1375926_comment'></div>怪貌魁形。曰余祝融之相也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1375926_comment'></div>夫霍山。余君之故治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1375926_comment'></div>尔赋之。诚形矣胜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1375926_comment'></div>怪矣典矣。然义有不备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1375926_comment'></div>帝俾余莅。夫古有五岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1375926_comment'></div>霍居其一。所以五岳相迩者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1375926_comment'></div>唐虞之帝。五载一巡狩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1375926_comment'></div>一载而遍。上以觐侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1375926_comment'></div>下以存民。侯有治者陟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1375926_comment'></div>不治者黜。民有冤者平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1375926_comment'></div>穷者济。洎唐虞以降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1375926_comment'></div>皆燔柴于霍。我帝用飨其礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1375926_comment'></div>至周旦策而命我。与诸岳星列中国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1375926_comment'></div>自汉之后。乃易我号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1375926_comment'></div>而归于衡。故祝融迁都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1375926_comment'></div>命余守霍。今圣天子越唐迈虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1375926_comment'></div>而废巡罢狩。余之封内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1375926_comment'></div>有可陟可黜可平可济者。是圣天子无由知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1375926_comment'></div>尔能以文请于执事之达者。易衡之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1375926_comment'></div>以归于我。请天子复唐虞陟黜之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1375926_comment'></div>故尔之将赋。余闭遏尔怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1375926_comment'></div>而不尔文。帝曰有衡既远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1375926_comment'></div>有狩必劳。惟霍之迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1375926_comment'></div>斯号可复。赋者能言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1375926_comment'></div>胡不俾传。帝俾命尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1375926_comment'></div>锡尔文。尔无忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1375926_comment'></div>臣曰。惟请神贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1375926_comment'></div>既觉而书。呜呼异哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1375926_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_73_1375926_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1376077' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376077' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376077?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春申君碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（865年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1376077")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376077_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376077'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376077'>士以知巳委用于人。报其用者术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376077_comment'></div>苟不王。要在强其国尊其君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376077_comment'></div>上可以霸略。次可以忠烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376077_comment'></div>无王术而有霸略者。可以胜人国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376077_comment'></div>无霸略而有忠烈者。亦足以胜人国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376077_comment'></div>春申君之道复何如哉。忧荆不胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376077_comment'></div>以身市奇计。不曰忠乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376077_comment'></div>荆太子既去。歇孤在秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376077_comment'></div>其俟刑待祸。若自屠以当馁虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376077_comment'></div>不曰烈乎。然徙都于寿春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376077_comment'></div>失邓塞之固。去方城之险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376077_comment'></div>舍江汉之利。其为谋已下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376077_comment'></div>犹死以吴为宫室。以鲁为封疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376077_comment'></div>春申之力哉。当斯时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376077_comment'></div>苟任荀卿之儒术。广圣深道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376077_comment'></div>用之期月。荆可王矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376077_comment'></div>然卒以猜去士。以谤免贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376077_comment'></div>于戏。儒术之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376077_comment'></div>其奥藏天地。其明烛鬼神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376077_comment'></div>春申且不悟。况李园之阴谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376077_comment'></div>岂易悟哉。岂易悟哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376077_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1376077_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
商州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b2449dd9b6da410e838034e0a36da605_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b2449dd9b6da410e838034e0a36da605");'><span id='b2449dd9b6da410e838034e0a36da605_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=865&endYear=865')">865年</a>，32岁</div><div id='b2449dd9b6da410e838034e0a36da605' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=865&endYear=865')">865年</a>　入冬后自寿州经樊、邓、商颜、蓝关入京。作品：蓝田关铭。<div id='poem_1375964' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375964' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375964?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蓝田关铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（865年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375964")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1375964_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1375964'>六年。皮子副诸侯贡士之荐入京。程至蓝田关。睹山形关势。回抱于天。秀欲染眸。危将惊魄。噫。将造物者心是而加力耶。不然者。何壮观若斯之盛也。易曰。王公设险以守其国。信矣哉。若为天下之枢机。万世之阃阈者。非兹关而莫守也。因陈其规。是为蓝田关铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1375964_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375964'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375964'>天辅唐业，地造唐关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1375964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1375964'>千岩作锁，万嶂为拴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1375964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1375964'>难图其形，莫壮其秀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1375964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1375964'>双扉未开，天地如斗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1375964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1375964'>轧然画启，人流如济。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1375964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1375964'>似画秦图，铺于马底。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1375964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1375964'>崄不可侵，惟王之心。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1375964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1375964'>矧夫兹关，独可<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1375964", 1375964, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>规临</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1375964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1375964'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1375964_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

蓝田

-----title
扬州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d9995a171e734db1a0ffca897fe45724_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d9995a171e734db1a0ffca897fe45724");'><span id='d9995a171e734db1a0ffca897fe45724_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=866&endYear=866')">866年</a>，33岁</div><div id='d9995a171e734db1a0ffca897fe45724' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=866&endYear=866')">866年</a>　携《文薮》游淮南扬州干谒令狐绹，并于令狐滈有酬唱。作品：汴河铭。<div id='poem_1375966' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375966' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375966?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汴河铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（866年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375966")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375966_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375966'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375966'>夫垂后以德者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375966_comment'></div>当时逸而后时美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375966_comment'></div>垂后以功者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375966_comment'></div>当时劳而后时利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375966_comment'></div>若然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375966_comment'></div>守道之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375966_comment'></div>惟恐德不美后时逸于己民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375966_comment'></div>夸力之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375966_comment'></div>惟恐功不及当时劳于己民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375966_comment'></div>故天下事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375966_comment'></div>不逸不足守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375966_comment'></div>不劳不可去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375966_comment'></div>致其利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375966_comment'></div>生于贤愚之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375966_comment'></div>自古然耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375966_comment'></div>则隋之疏淇汴凿太行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375966_comment'></div>在隋之民不胜其害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375966_comment'></div>在唐之民不胜其利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375966_comment'></div>今自九河外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375966_comment'></div>复有淇汴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375966_comment'></div>北通涿郡之渔商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375966_comment'></div>南运江都之转输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375966_comment'></div>其为利也博哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375966_comment'></div>不劳一夫之荷畚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375966_comment'></div>一卒之凿险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375966_comment'></div>而先功巍巍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375966_comment'></div>得非天假暴隋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375966_comment'></div>成我大利哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375966_comment'></div>尚恐国家有淇汴太行之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375966_comment'></div>因献纤诫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375966_comment'></div>是为汴河铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375966_comment'></div>汴河沵沵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375966_comment'></div>循禹之轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375966_comment'></div>厥有暴隋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375966_comment'></div>凿通淮泗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375966_comment'></div>昼泣疲民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375966_comment'></div>夜哭溺鬼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1375966_comment'></div>似赭流川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1375966_comment'></div>如松贯地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1375966_comment'></div>龙舟未故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1375966_comment'></div>江都已弑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1375966_comment'></div>陈迹空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1375966_comment'></div>逝波不止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1375966_comment'></div>在隋则害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1375966_comment'></div>在唐则利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1375966_comment'></div>呜乎圣王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1375966_comment'></div>守旧而已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1375966_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ab4481e6849649b0b577c3ce618c746d_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=871&endYear=871')">871年3月</a>　崔璞罢郡，有文会，皮日休、陆龟蒙等作诗相送。作品：谏议罢郡将归，以六韵赐示，因伫酬献。<div id='poem_15576' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15576' class='poemTitle ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=871&endYear=871')">871年</a>　崔幕解散，皮日休欲谋求新路而致书各方故知，有诗劄寄裴坦者。作品：吴中书事，寄汉南裴尚书。<div id='poem_15432' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15432' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_4_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15570'>才非师赵壹，直欲效陈咸。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15570'>壅泉教咽咽，垒石放巉巉。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15570'>掣钓随心动，抽书任意杴。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15570'>茶教弩父摘，酒遣僰童监。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15570'>药苞陈雨匼，诗草蠹云函。<div id='poem_sentence_15_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_15570'>遣客呼林狖，辞人寄海𧍧。<div id='poem_sentence_16_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_15570'>室唯搜古器，钱只买秋杉。<div id='poem_sentence_17_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_15570'>寡合无深契，相期有至諴。<div id='poem_sentence_18_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_15570'>他年如访问，烟茑暗髟髟。<div id='poem_sentence_19_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_15570'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_15570_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=871&endYear=871')">871年</a>　皮陆唱和，皮日休有《寄题罗浮轩辕先生所居》，陆龟蒙和之。本年夏秋，皮日休临别吴中之际，陆龟蒙将两年左右唱和诗集集合成编，为《松陵集》十卷，以为纪念。皮日休为作《松陵集序》，阐述其诗歌见解，叙其与陆龟蒙之唱和大致经历，序中有论当代诗人李商隐、温庭筠者，颇有说。集中多次韵长篇，又有离合、叠韵、回文、双声及县名、药名等类诗作，陆龟蒙将其归入杂体诗卷，皮日休撰《杂体诗序》，记述诸类诗之缘起。作品：鲁望以花翁之什见招，因次韵酬之。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第282页。）</span>寄题罗浮轩辕先生所居。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第282页。）</span>松陵集序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年文见第283页。）</span>座右铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年文见第283页。）</span>杂体诗序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年文见第283页。）</span>襄州孔子庙学记唐社稷坛记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年文见第283页。）</span>江南书情二十韵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第282页。）</span>屐步访鲁望不遇。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第282页。）</span>馆娃宫怀古。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第282页。）</span>春夕陪崔谏议樱桃园序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第282页。）</span>春夕酒醒。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第282页。）</span>松江早春。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第282页。）</span>奉和1。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第282页。）</span>奉和2。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第282页。）</span><div id='poem_15546' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15546' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15546?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鲁望以花翁之什见招因次韵詶之</a><span class='authorDate'>（871年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>九十</span>携锄伛偻翁，小园幽事尽能通。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15546'>斸烟栽药为身计，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_15546", 15546, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>负水</span>浇花是世功。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15546'>婚嫁定期杉叶紫，盖藏应待桂枝红。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15546'>不知家道能多少，只在句芒一夜风。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15546'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15546_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15535' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15535' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15535?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄题罗浮轩辕先生所居</a><span class='authorDate'>（871年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15535")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_15535_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15535'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15535'>乱峰四百三十二<span class='inlineComment2'>（罗浮山峰数）</span>，欲问徵君何处寻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15535'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_15535", 15535, "Clauses/2/Comments/2")'>红翠</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（山鸟名）</span>数声<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_15535", 15535, "Clauses/2/Comments/3")'>瑶室</span>响<span class='inlineComment2'>（山有璇房瑶室七十有二）</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_15535", 15535, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>真檀</span>一炷石楼深。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15535'>山都遣负沽来酒，樵客容看化后金。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15535'>从此谒师知不远，求官先有葛洪心。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15535'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15535_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1375937' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375937' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375937?labeling=true' target='_blank'>松陵集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（871年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375937")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375937_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375937'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375937'>诗有六艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375937_comment'></div>其一曰比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375937_comment'></div>比者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375937_comment'></div>定物之情状也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375937_comment'></div>则必谓之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375937_comment'></div>才之备者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375937_comment'></div>于圣为六艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375937_comment'></div>于贤为声诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375937_comment'></div>噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375937_comment'></div>春秋之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375937_comment'></div>颂声亡寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375937_comment'></div>降及汉氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375937_comment'></div>诗道荐作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375937_comment'></div>然二雅之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375937_comment'></div>委而不兴矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375937_comment'></div>在诗有三言四言五言六言七言之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1375937_comment'></div>三言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1375937_comment'></div>曰振振鹭鹭于飞是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1375937_comment'></div>五言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1375937_comment'></div>曰谁谓雀无角何以穿我屋是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1375937_comment'></div>六言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1375937_comment'></div>我姑酌彼金罍是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1375937_comment'></div>七言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1375937_comment'></div>交交黄鸟止于桑是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1375937_comment'></div>九言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1375937_comment'></div>曰泂酌彼行潦挹彼注兹是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1375937_comment'></div>盖古诗率以四言为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1375937_comment'></div>而汉氏方以五言七言为之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1375937_comment'></div>其句亦出于周诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1375937_comment'></div>五言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1375937_comment'></div>李陵曰携手上河梁是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1375937_comment'></div>七言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1375937_comment'></div>汉武曰日月星辰和四时是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1375937_comment'></div>尔后盛于建安以降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1375937_comment'></div>江左君臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1375937_comment'></div>得其浮艳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1375937_comment'></div>然诗之六艺微矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1375937_comment'></div>逮及吾唐开元之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1375937_comment'></div>易其体为律焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1375937_comment'></div>始切于俪偶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1375937_comment'></div>拘于声势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1375937_comment'></div>诗云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1375937_comment'></div>觏闵既多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1375937_comment'></div>受侮不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1375937_comment'></div>其对也工矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1375937_comment'></div>尧典曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1375937_comment'></div>声依永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1375937_comment'></div>律和声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1375937_comment'></div>其为律也甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1375937_comment'></div>由汉及唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1375937_comment'></div>诗之道尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1375937_comment'></div>吾又不知千祀之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1375937_comment'></div>诗之道止于斯而巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1375937_comment'></div>即后有变而作者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1375937_comment'></div>不得以知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1375937_comment'></div>夫才之备者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1375937_comment'></div>犹天地之气乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1375937_comment'></div>气者止乎一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1375937_comment'></div>分而为四时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1375937_comment'></div>其为春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1375937_comment'></div>则煦枯发蘖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1375937_comment'></div>如弃如濩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1375937_comment'></div>百物融洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1375937_comment'></div>酣人肌骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1375937_comment'></div>其为夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1375937_comment'></div>则赫曦朝升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1375937_comment'></div>天地如窑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1375937_comment'></div>草焦木暍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1375937_comment'></div>若燎毛发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1375937_comment'></div>其为秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1375937_comment'></div>则凉飔高瞥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1375937_comment'></div>若露天骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1375937_comment'></div>景爽夕清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1375937_comment'></div>神不蔽形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1375937_comment'></div>其为冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1375937_comment'></div>则霜阵一凄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1375937_comment'></div>万物皆瘁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1375937_comment'></div>云沮日惨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1375937_comment'></div>若惮天责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1375937_comment'></div>夫如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1375937_comment'></div>岂拘于一哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1375937_comment'></div>亦变之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1375937_comment'></div>人之有才者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1375937_comment'></div>不变则已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1375937_comment'></div>苟变之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1375937_comment'></div>岂异于是乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1375937_comment'></div>故才之用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1375937_comment'></div>广之为沧溟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1375937_comment'></div>细之为沟窦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1375937_comment'></div>高之为山岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1375937_comment'></div>碎之为瓦砾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1375937_comment'></div>美之为西子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1375937_comment'></div>恶之为敦洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1375937_comment'></div>壮之为武贲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1375937_comment'></div>弱之为处女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1375937_comment'></div>大则八荒之外不可穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1375937_comment'></div>小则一毫之末不可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1375937_comment'></div>苟其才如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1375937_comment'></div>复能善用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1375937_comment'></div>则庖丁之牛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1375937_comment'></div>扁之轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1375937_comment'></div>郢之斤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1375937_comment'></div>不足谓神解也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1375937_comment'></div>噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1375937_comment'></div>古之士穷达必形于歌咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1375937_comment'></div>苟欲见乎志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1375937_comment'></div>非文不能宣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1375937_comment'></div>于是为其词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1375937_comment'></div>词之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1375937_comment'></div>固不能独善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1375937_comment'></div>必须人以成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1375937_comment'></div>昔周公为诗以遗成王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1375937_comment'></div>吉甫作诵以赠申伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1375937_comment'></div>诗之酬赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1375937_comment'></div>其来尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1375937_comment'></div>后每为诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1375937_comment'></div>必多□□为□咸通七年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1375937_comment'></div>今兵部令狐员外在淮南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1375937_comment'></div>今中书舍人□□公守毗陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1375937_comment'></div>日休皆以词获幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1375937_comment'></div>悉蒙以所制命之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1375937_comment'></div>各□□轴亦有名其守者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1375937_comment'></div>十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1375937_comment'></div>大司谏清河公出牧于吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1375937_comment'></div>日休为郡奁事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1375937_comment'></div>居一月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1375937_comment'></div>有进士陆龟蒙字鲁望者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1375937_comment'></div>以其业见造凡数编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1375937_comment'></div>其才之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1375937_comment'></div>真天地之气也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1375937_comment'></div>近代称温飞卿李义山为之最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1375937_comment'></div>俾生参之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1375937_comment'></div>未知其孰为之后先也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_132_1375937_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15570' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15570' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15570?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江南书情二十韵寄秘阁韦校书贻之商洛宋先辈垂文二同年</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_15570", 15570, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>凤尾诏</span>，我住虎头岩。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15570'>季氏唯谋逐，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(10410, "poem_sentence_2_15570")'>臧仓</span>只拟谗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15570'>时讹轻<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(8944, "poem_sentence_3_15570")'>五羖</span>，俗浅重<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1880, "poem_sentence_3_15570")'>三缄</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15570'>瘦去形如鹤，忧来态似獑。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15570'>才非师赵壹，直欲效陈咸。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15570'>孤竹宁收笛，黄琮未作瑊。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15570'>作羊宁免狠，为兔即须毚。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15570'>枕户槐从亚，侵阶草懒芟。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
常州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='dd4e588a8cf74906b53cf5501a88b728_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dd4e588a8cf74906b53cf5501a88b728");'><span id='dd4e588a8cf74906b53cf5501a88b728_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=866&endYear=866')">866年</a>，33岁</div><div id='dd4e588a8cf74906b53cf5501a88b728' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=866&endYear=866')">866年</a>　下江南毗陵，干谒杨知至，并与其酬唱。作品：七爱诗（白太傅）<div id='poem_15584' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15584' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15584?labeling=true' target='_blank'>七爱诗<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>房杜二相国<span class='inlineComment2'>（玄龄、如晦）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（866年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15584")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15584_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_15584'>皮子之志，常以真纯自许。每谓立大化者，必有真相，以房杜为真相焉；定大乱者，必有真将，以李太尉为真将焉。傲大君者，必有真隐，以卢徵君为真隐焉；镇浇俗者，必有真吏，以元鲁山为真吏焉；负逸气者，必有真放，以李翰林为真放焉；为名臣者，必有真才，以白太傅为真才焉。呜呼！吾之道时耶，行其事也，在乎爱忠矣。不时耶，行其事也，亦在乎爱忠矣。苟有心歌咏者，岂徒然哉！</div><div id='poem_preface_15584_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_15584'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4236, "poem_allusion_15584")'>黄阁</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(8264, "poem_allusion_15584")'>陶铸</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(10639, "poem_allusion_15584")'>执鞭</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_15584_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15584'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15584'>吾爱房与杜，贫贱共联步。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15584'>脱身抛乱世，策杖归真主。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15584'>纵横握中算，左右天下务。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15584'>肮脏无敌才，磊落不世遇。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15584'>美矣名公卿，魁然真宰辅。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15584'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4236, "poem_sentence_5_15584")'>黄阁</span>三十年，清风一万古。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15584'>巨业照国史，大勋镇王府。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15584'>遂使后世民，至今受<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(8264, "poem_sentence_7_15584")'>陶铸</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15584'>粤吾少有志，敢蹑前贤路。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15584'>苟得同其时，愿为<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(10639, id='poem_sentence_10_15584_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15582' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15582' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15582?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_1_15582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15582'>一战取王畿，一叱散妖氛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15582'>乘舆既反正，凶竖争亡魂。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15582'>巍巍柱天功，荡荡盖世勋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15582'>仁于曹孟德，勇过<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4379, id='poem_sentence_6_15582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15582'>所谓大丈夫，动合惊乾坤。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15582'>百世必一乱，千年方一人。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15580' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15580?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>卢徵君<span id='poem_content_15580'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15580'>吾爱卢徵君，高卧嵩山里。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15580'>百辟未一顾，三徵方暂起。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15580'>坦腹对宰相，岸帻揖天子。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15580'>建礼门前吟，金銮殿里醉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15580'>天下皆餔糟，徵君独洁己。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15580'>天下皆乐闻，徵君独洗耳。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15580'>再看缑山云，重酌嵩阳水。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15580'>吾谓巢与许，不若徵君义。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15580'>高名无阶级，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_15580", 15580, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>逸迹</span>绝涯涘。<div id='poem_sentence_14_15580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15580'>万世唐书中，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_15580", 15580, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>逸名</span>不可比。<div id='poem_sentence_15_15580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_15580'>粤吾慕真隐，强以骨肉累。<div -----title
华阴（华州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='320f9085c1c84732a7731ba62cf81043_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("320f9085c1c84732a7731ba62cf81043");'><span id='320f9085c1c84732a7731ba62cf81043_link' -----title
苏州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b9dc1ae27c924152a49b14bdbd4d3961_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b9dc1ae27c924152a49b14bdbd4d3961");'><span id='b9dc1ae27c924152a49b14bdbd4d3961_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=869&endYear=870')">869-870年</a>，36-37岁</div><div id='b9dc1ae27c924152a49b14bdbd4d3961' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=869&endYear=869')">869年</a>　皮日休入苏州，为郡从事，主军事院判官；不久，陆龟蒙以郡中进士身份怀行卷谒皮日休。自此，两人相交酬唱甚密。作品：鲁望读，见赠五百言，过褒庸才，靡有称事。然襄阳曩事，历历在目，夫所未载者，汉阳王则宗社元动，孟浩然则文长大匠。子次而赞之，因而寄答，亦诗人无言不酬之议也。次韵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第208页。）</span>鲁望昨以五百言见贶，过有褒美，内揣庸陋，弥增愧悚。因成一千言，上述吾唐文物之盛，次叙相得之欢，亦迭和之微旨也。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第208页。）</span>公齐四咏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第208页。）</span>新秋言怀寄鲁望三十韵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第208页。）</span>初冬偶作，寄南阳润卿。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第209页。）</span>冬晓章上人院。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第209页。）</span>醉中即席赠润卿博士。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第209页。）</span>褚家林亭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第210页。）</span>润卿、鲁望寒夜见访，各惜其志，遂成一绝。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第210页。）</span>奉酬次韵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第208页。）</span>奉和次韵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第209页。）</span>奉和。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第210页。）</span><div id='poem_15728' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15728' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15728?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鲁望读襄阳耆旧传见赠五百言过褒庸材靡有称是然襄阳曩事历历在目夫耆旧传所未载者汉阳王则宗社元勋孟浩然则文章大匠予次而赞之因而寄荅亦诗人无言不詶之义也次韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（869年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15728")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15728_comment'></div><div id='poem_allusion_15728_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15728'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15728'>汉水碧于天，南荆廓然秀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15728'>庐罗遵古俗，鄢郢迷昔囿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15728'>幽奇无得状，巉绝不能究。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15728'>兴替忽矣新，山川<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_4_15728'>斑斑生造士，一一应<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_15728", 15728, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>玄宿</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15728'>是非既自分，泾渭不相就。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15728'>粤自灵均来，清才若天漱。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15728'>始将麋鹿狎，遂与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_15728", 15728, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>麒麟斗</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15728'>万乘不可谒，千钟固非茂。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15728'>檀溪试戈船，岘岭屯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_15728", 15728, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>贝胄</span>。<div
