id='poem_sentence_8_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15727'>太浮如潋滟，太细如蚳蝝。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15727'>太乱如靡靡，太轻如芊芊。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15727'>流之为酗醟，变之为游畋。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15727'>百足虽云众，不救杀马蚿。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15727'>君臣作降虏，北走如㺦猭。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15727'>所以文字妖，致其国朝迁。<div id='poem_sentence_14_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15727'>吾唐革其弊，取士将科县。<div id='poem_sentence_15_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_15727'>文星下为人，洪秀密于缏。<div id='poem_sentence_16_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_15727'>大开紫宸扉，来者皆详延。<div id='poem_sentence_17_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_15727'>日晏朝不罢，龙姿欢𨌈<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>𨌈。<div id='poem_sentence_18_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_15727'>于焉周道反，由是秦法悛。<div id='poem_sentence_19_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_15727'>射洪陈子昂，其声亦喧阗。<div id='poem_sentence_20_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_15727'>惜哉不得时，将奋犹拘挛。<div id='poem_sentence_21_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_15727'>玉垒李太白，铜堤孟浩然。<div id='poem_sentence_22_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_15727'>李宽包堪舆，孟澹拟<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作凝）</span>漪涟。<div id='poem_sentence_23_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_15727'>埋骨采石圹，留神鹿门埏。<div id='poem_sentence_24_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_15727'>俾其羁旅死，实觉天地孱。<div id='poem_sentence_25_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_15727'>猗与子美思，不尽如转辁。<div id='poem_sentence_26_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_15727'>纵为三十车，一字不可捐。<div id='poem_sentence_27_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_15727'>既作风雅主，遂司歌咏权。<div id='poem_sentence_28_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_15727'>谁知耒阳土，埋却真神仙。<div id='poem_sentence_29_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_15727'>当于李杜际，名辈或溯沿。<div id='poem_sentence_30_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_15727'>良御非异马，由弓非他弦。<div id='poem_sentence_31_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_15727'>其物无同异，其人有媸妍。<div id='poem_sentence_32_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_15727'>自开元至今，宗社纷如烟。<div id='poem_sentence_33_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_15727'>爽若沆瀣英，高如昆崙巅。<div id='poem_sentence_34_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_15727'>百家嚣浮说，诸子率寓篇。<div id='poem_sentence_35_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_15727'>筑之为京观，解之为牲牷。<div id='poem_sentence_36_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_15727'>各持天地维，率意东西牵。<div id='poem_sentence_37_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_15727'>竞抵元化首，争扼真宰咽。<div id='poem_sentence_38_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_15727'>或作制诰薮，或为宫体渊。<div id='poem_sentence_39_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_15727'>或堪被金石，或可投花钿。<div id='poem_sentence_40_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_15727'>或为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_15727", 15727, "Clauses/82/Comments/0")'>舆隶</span>唱，或被儿童怜。<div id='poem_sentence_41_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_15727'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_15727", 15727, "Clauses/84/Comments/0")'>乌垒</span>虏亦写，鸡林夷争传。<div id='poem_sentence_42_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_15727'>披揭<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作猖）</span>覆载枢，捭阖神异键。<div id='poem_sentence_43_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_15727'>力抛<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(8700, "poem_sentence_44_15727")'>尾闾</span>立，思<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作鬼）</span>轧大块旋。<div id='poem_sentence_44_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_15727'>降气或若虹，耀影或如■<span class='inlineComment2'>（{艹/冖/残}）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_45_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_15727'>万象疮复痏，百灵瘠且𤼙。<div id='poem_sentence_46_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_15727'>谓乎数十公，笔若明堂椽。<div id='poem_sentence_47_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_15727'>其中有拟者，不绝当如綖。<div id='poem_sentence_48_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_15727'>齐驱不让策，并驾或争骈。<div id='poem_sentence_49_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_15727'>所以吾唐风，直将三代甄。<div id='poem_sentence_50_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_15727'>被此文物盛，由乎声诗宣。<div id='poem_sentence_51_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_15727'>采彼风人谣，輶轩轻似鹯。<div id='poem_sentence_52_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_15727'>丽者固不舍，鄙者亦为铨。<div id='poem_sentence_53_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_15727'>其中有銮戒，一一堪雕镌。<div id='poem_sentence_54_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_15727'>乙夜以观之，吾君无释焉。<div id='poem_sentence_55_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_15727'>遂命大司乐，度之如星躔。<div id='poem_sentence_56_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_15727'>播于乐府中，俾为万代蠲。<div id='poem_sentence_57_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_15727'>吹彼圆丘竹，诵兹清庙弦。<div id='poem_sentence_58_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_15727'>不惟娱列祖，兼可格<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(7597, "poem_sentence_59_15727")'>上玄</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_59_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_15727'>粤予何为者，生自江海壖。<div id='poem_sentence_60_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_61_15727'>騃騃自<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(11014, "poem_sentence_61_15727")'>总角</span>，不甘耕一廛。<div id='poem_sentence_61_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_62_15727'>诸昆指仓库，谓我死道边。<div id='poem_sentence_62_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_15727'>何为不力农，稽古真可嘕。<div id='poem_sentence_63_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_64_15727'>遂与袯襫著，兼之籉笠全。<div id='poem_sentence_64_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_15727'>风吹蔓草花，飒飒盈荒田。<div id='poem_sentence_65_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_66_15727'>老牛瞪不行，力弱谁能鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_66_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_67_15727'>乃将耒与耜，并换椠与铅。<div id='poem_sentence_67_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_15727'>阅彼图籍肆，致之千百编。<div id='poem_sentence_68_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_15727'>携将入苏岭<span class='inlineComment2'>（鹿门别名）</span>，不就无出缘。<div id='poem_sentence_69_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_70_15727'>堆书塞低屋，添砚涸小泉。<div id='poem_sentence_70_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_71_15727'>对灯任髻爇，冯案从肘研。<div id='poem_sentence_71_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_15727'>苟无切玉刀，难除指上胼。<div id='poem_sentence_72_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_73_15727'>尔来五寒暑，试艺称精专。<div id='poem_sentence_73_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_74_15727'>昌黎道未著，文教如欲骞。<div id='poem_sentence_74_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_15727'>其中有声病，于我如𦧝<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>𦧴。<div id='poem_sentence_75_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_76_15727'>是敢驱颓波，归之于大川。<div id='poem_sentence_76_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_77_15727'>其文如可用，不敢佞与便。<div id='poem_sentence_77_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_78_15727'>明水在稿秸，太羹临豆笾。<div id='poem_sentence_78_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_79_15727'>将来示时人，䝟貐垂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_79_15727", 15727, "Clauses/159/Comments/0")'>馋涎</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_79_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_80_15727'>亦或尚华缛，亦曾为便嬛。<div id='poem_sentence_80_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_15727'>亦能制灏灏，亦解攻翩翩。<div id='poem_sentence_81_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_82_15727'>唯思逢阵敌，与彼争后先。<div id='poem_sentence_82_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_83_15727'>避兵入句吴，穷悴祗自跧。<div id='poem_sentence_83_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_84_15727'>平原陆夫子，投刺来翩跹。<div id='poem_sentence_84_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_85_15727'>开卷读数行，为之加<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_85_15727", 15727, "Clauses/171/Comments/0")'>敬虔</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_85_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_86_15727'>忽穷一两首，反顾唯曲拳。<div id='poem_sentence_86_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_15727'>始来<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9904, "poem_sentence_87_15727")'>遗巾帼</span>，乃敢排戈鋋。<div id='poem_sentence_87_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_88_15727'>或为<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(215, "poem_sentence_88_15727")'>拔帜</span>走，或遭劘垒还。<div id='poem_sentence_88_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_89_15727'>不能收乱辙，岂暇重为篿。<div id='poem_sentence_89_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_90_15727'>虽然未<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_90_15727", 15727, "Clauses/180/Comments/0")'>三北</span>，亦可输千鐉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_90_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_91_15727'>向来说文字，尔汝名可联。<div id='poem_sentence_91_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_15727'>圣人病殁世，不患穷而蹎。<div id='poem_sentence_92_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_93_15727'>我未九品位，君无一囊钱。<div id='poem_sentence_93_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_94_15727'>相逢得何事，两笼酬戏笺。<div id='poem_sentence_94_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_95_15727'>无颜解媮合，底事居冗员。<div id='poem_sentence_95_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_96_15727'>方知<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(8561, "poem_sentence_96_15727")'>万钟禄</span>，不博五湖船。<div id='poem_sentence_96_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_97_15727'>夷险但明月，死生应白莲。<div id='poem_sentence_97_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_98_15727'>吟馀凭几饮，钓罢偎蓑眠。<div id='poem_sentence_98_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_99_15727'>终抛岘山业，相共此留连。<div id='poem_sentence_99_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_100_15727'></div><div id='poem_sentence_100_15727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_15727'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_18_15727_0'>⑴ 音田，《吕氏春秋》云：“天子𨌈𨌈。”</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_75_15727_0'>⑵ 音天蝉，语不正貌</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_90_15727_0'>⑶ 丑专切，《尚书》云：“赎罪千鐉。”</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_15727_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_15591' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15591' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15591?labeling=true' target='_blank'>公斋四咏<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>小松</a><span class='authorDate'>（869年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15591")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15591_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15591'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15591'>婆娑只三尺，移来白云径。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15591'>亭亭向空意，已解凌辽夐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15591'>叶健似虬须，枝脆如<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_15591", 15591, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>鹤胫</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15591'>清音犹未成，绀彩空不定。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15591'>阴圆小芝盖，鳞涩修荷柄。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15591'>先愁被鴳抢，预恐遭蜗病。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15591'>结根幸得地，且免离离映。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15591'>磥砢不难遇，在保晚成性。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15591'>一日造明堂，为君当毕命。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15591'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_15591_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15592' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15592' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15592?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>小桂</a><span class='authorDate'>（869年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15592_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15592'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15592'>一子落天上，生此青璧枝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15592'>歘从山之幽，斸断云根移。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15592'>劲挺隐圭质，盘珊缇油姿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15592'>叶彩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_15592", 15592, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>碧髓</span>融，花状<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_15592", 15592, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>白毫</span>蕤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15592'>棱层立<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_15592", 15592, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>翠节</span>，偃蹇樛<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_15592", 15592, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>青螭</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15592'>影澹雪霁后，香汎风和时。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15592'>吾祖在月竁，孤贞能见怡。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15592'>愿老君子地，不敢辞喧卑。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15592'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_15592_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15593' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15593' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15593?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_6_15689'>谁能变羊质，竞不获<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(512, "poem_sentence_6_15689")'>骊珠</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15689'>粤有造化手，曾开天地炉。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15689'>文章邺下秀，气貌淹中儒。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15689'>展我此志业，期君持中枢。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15689'>苍生眼穿望，勿作磻溪谟。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15689'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_15689_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=869&endYear=869')">869年</a>　进士崔璐谒皮日休，皮日休以其《文薮》十卷示之，崔璞有诗赞仰，皮有酬答，陆龟蒙亦和之。作品：奉酬崔璐进士见寄次韵。<div id='poem_15689' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15689' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_11_15689_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=869&endYear=869')">869年</a>　又与吴中名士徐修矩、任晦等交游，赏其藏书之富、园林之胜。作品：二游诗。任诗。<div id='poem_15586' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15586' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15586?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二游诗<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>徐诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（869年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15586")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15586_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_15586'>吴之士有恩王府参军徐修矩者，守世书万卷，优游自适。余假其书数千卷，未一年，悉偿夙志，酣饫经史，或日晏忘饮食。次有前泾县尉任晦者，其居有深林曲沼，危亭幽砌，余并次以见之，或退公之暇，必造以息焉。林泉隐事，恣用研咏。大凡游于二君宅，无浃旬之间，因作诗以留赠，名之曰二游（目之曰二游），兼寄陆鲁望。</div><div id='poem_preface_15586_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_15586'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2946, "poem_allusion_15586")'>坟籍</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_15586_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15586'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15586'>东莞为著姓，奕代皆隽哲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15586'>强学取科第，名声尽孤揭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15586'>自为方州来，清操称凛冽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15586'>唯写<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2946, "poem_sentence_3_15586")'>坟籍</span>多，必云清俸绝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15586'>宣毫利若风，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_15586", 15586, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>剡纸</span>光于月。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15586'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_15586", 15586, id='poem_sentence_6_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15586'>转徙入吴都，纵横碍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_15586", 15586, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>门闑</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15586'>缥囊轻似雾，缃帙殷于血。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15586'>以此为基构，将斯用贻厥。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15586'>重于通侯印，贵却全师节。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15586'>我爱参卿道，承家能介洁。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15586'>潮田五万步，草屋十馀<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作数）</span>楶。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15586'>微宦不能去，归来坐如刖。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_15586'>引之看秘宝，任得穷披阅。<div id='poem_sentence_16_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_15586'>帙解带芸香，卷开和桂屑。<div id='poem_sentence_18_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_15586'>枕兼石锋刃，榻共松<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_15586", 15586, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>疮疖</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_19_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_15586'>一卧寂无諠，数编看尽彻。<div id='poem_sentence_20_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_15586'>如斯未星纪，悉得分毫末。<div id='poem_sentence_23_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_15586'>苟昧古与今，何殊瘖共𦘍<span class='inlineComment2'>（五骨切）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_27_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_15586'>昔之慕经史，有以佣笔札。<div id='poem_sentence_28_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_15586'>其道苟可光，斯文那自伐。<div id='poem_sentence_31_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15585' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15585?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>任诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（869年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15585_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_15585'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3604, "poem_allusion_15585")'>圭窦</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_15585_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15585'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15585'>任君恣高放，斯道能寡合。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15585'>歘尔解其绶，遗之如<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_15585", 15585, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>弃靸</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15585'>归来乡党内，却与亲朋洽。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15585'>开溪未让丁，列第方称甲。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15585'>入门约百步，古木声霎霎。<div id='poem_sentence_23_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_15585'>欲者解挤排，诟者能詀讘。<div id='poem_sentence_24_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_15585'></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_15585_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=869&endYear=869')">869年</a>　皮陆二人与张贲等交游唱和。作品：南阳广文欲于荆襄卜居，因而有赠。<div id='poem_15488' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15488' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15488?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南阳广文欲于荆襄卜居因而有赠</a><span class='authorDate'>（869年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15488")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_15488_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15488'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15488'>地脉从来是福乡，广文高致更无双。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15488_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15488'>青精饭熟云侵灶，白■<span class='inlineComment2'>（{衤劫}）</span>裘成雪溅窗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15488_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15488'>度日竹书千万字，经冬朮煎两三缸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15488_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15488'>鲈鱼自是君家味，莫背松江忆汉江。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=869&endYear=869')">869年</a>　秋深送别张贲还雷平。作品：南阳润卿将归雷平，因而有赠。<div id='poem_15489' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15489' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15489?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南阳润卿将归雷平因而有赠</a><span class='authorDate'>（869年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_15489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15489'>绛树实多分紫鹿，丹沙泉浅种红鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15489_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=869&endYear=869')">869年</a>　陆龟蒙旧友吴兴进士严子重访皮陆。作品：伤进士严子重诗。<div id='poem_15415' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15415' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15415?labeling=true' target='_blank'>伤进士严子重诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（869年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15415")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_15415_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_15415'>余为童在乡校时，简上抄杜舍人牧之集，见有与进士严恽诗。后至吴，一日，有客曰严某，余志其名久矣，遽怀文见造，于是乐得礼而观之。其所为工于七字，往往有清便柔媚，时可轶骇于常轨。其佳者曰：「春光冉冉归何处，更向花前把一杯。尽日问花花不语，为谁零落为谁开。」余美之，讽而未尝怠，生举进士，亦十馀计偕。余方冤之，谓乎竟有得于时也。未几，归吴兴，后两月（案：咸通十一年也。），霅人至云：「生以疾亡于所居矣。」噫！生徒以词闻于士大夫，竟不名而逝，岂止此而湮没耶？江湖间多美材，士君子苟乐退而有文者死，无不为时惜，可胜言耶？于是哭而为诗。鲁望，生之友也，当为我同作。</div><div id='poem_preface_15415_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15415'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15415'>十哭都门榜上尘，盖棺终是五湖人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15415'>生前有敌唯丹桂，没后无家秖白蘋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15415'>箬下斩新醒处月，江南依旧咏来春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15415'>知君精爽应无尽，必在酆都颂帝晨<span class='inlineComment2'>（梁成酆都官颂，纣绝标帝晨）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15415'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15415_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=870')">870年2月</a>　皮日休、陆龟蒙等人作诗伤严子重进士；并迎其妻室山阴滕式入苏州。作品：伤进士严子重诗并序。<div class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第254页。）</span>又寄次前韵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第255页。）</span>四明山诗并序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第255页。）</span>病中有人惠海蟹转寄鲁望。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第256页。）</span>病中美景颇阻追游因寄鲁望。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第256页。）</span>病中庭际海石榴花盛发，感而有寄。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第256页。）</span>早春以橘子寄鲁望。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第257页。）</span>病中书情寄上崔谏议，时眼疾未平。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第257页。）</span>病孔雀。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第257页。）</span>奉酬惜春见寄。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第257页。）</span>闻鲁望游颜家园林，病中有寄。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第257页。）</span>鲁望春日多寻野景，皮日休抱疾杜门，因有是寄。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第257页。）</span>奉和次韵（野客正闲移竹远）<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第258页。）</span>鲁望以躬掇野荒，兼示雅什，用以酬谢。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>卧疾感春寄鲁望。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>奉酬见答鱼笺之什。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>病后春思。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>偶成小酌，招鲁望不至，以诗为解。因次韵酬之。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>以纱巾寄鲁望，因而有作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第253页。）</span>以紫石砚见鲁望，兼酬见赠。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第254页。）</span>奉和次韵1。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第255页。）</span>奉和次韵2。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>奉和次韵9。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第260页。）</span>奉和次韵10。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第261页。）</span>奉和次韵11。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第265页。）</span>奉和6。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第265页。）</span>夏首病愈，因招鲁望。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>登初阳楼，寄怀北平郎中。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>夏初访鲁望，偶题小斋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>所居首夏水木尤清，适然有作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>重玄寺元达年逾八十，好种名药，凡所植者多至自天台、四明、包山、句曲，业萃纷糅，各可指名。余奇而访之，因题二章。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>夏景无事，因怀章、来二上人。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>鲁望以轮钩相示，缅怀高致，因作三篇。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第260页。）</span><div id='poem_15421' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15421' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_4_15549'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15549_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=870')">870年</a>　皮日休病愈，并作诗招羊振文等小饮，羊振文赴，陆龟蒙以病不赴，然皆有和诗。作品：偶留羊振文先辈及一二文友小饮，日休以眼病初平，不敢饮酒，遣侍密欢，因成四韵。<div id='poem_15527' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15527' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15527?labeling=true' target='_blank'>偶留羊振文先辈及一二文友小饮日休以眼病初平不敢饮酒遣侍密欢因成四韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15527")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div id='poem_sentence_3_15527_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15527'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15527_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=870')">870年</a>　吴中淫雨不息。皮日休有诗写连日大雨时情况，陆龟蒙和之。至此，皮陆唱和已达半年之久。作品：吴中苦雨，因书一百韵寄鲁望。<div id='poem_15654' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15654' id='poem_sentence_16_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_15654'>狂发铿訇音，不得懈怠僇。<div id='poem_sentence_17_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_15654'>顷刻势稍止，尚自倾蔌蔌。<div id='poem_sentence_18_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_15654'>不敢履洿处，恐蹋烂地轴。<div id='poem_sentence_19_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_15654'>自尔凡十日，茫然晦林麓。<div id='poem_sentence_20_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_15654'>只是遇滂沱，少曾逢霢霂。<div id='poem_sentence_21_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_15654'>伊余之廨宇，古制拙卜筑。<div id='poem_sentence_22_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_15654'>颓檐倒菌黄，破砌顽莎绿。<div id='poem_sentence_23_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_15654'>只有方丈居，其中蹐且跼。<div id='poem_sentence_24_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_15654'>朽处或似醉，漏时又如沃。<div id='poem_sentence_25_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_15654'>阶前平汎滥，墙下起<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_15654", 15654, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>趢趚</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_26_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_15654'>唯堪著籉笠，复可乘𦨧<span class='inlineComment2'>（𦨙）</span>宿<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作䑿）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_27_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_15654'>鸡犬并淋漓，儿童但咿喔。<div id='poem_sentence_28_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_15654'>勃勃生湿气，人人牢于锔。<div id='poem_sentence_29_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_15654'>须眉渍将断，肝膈蒸欲熟。<div id='poem_sentence_30_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_15654'>当庭死兰芷，四垣盛薋菉。<div id='poem_sentence_31_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_15654'>解帙展断书，拂床安坏椟<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作牍）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_32_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_15654'>跳梁老蛙黾，直向床前浴。<div id='poem_sentence_33_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_15654'>蹲前但相聒，似把白丁辱。<div id='poem_sentence_34_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_15654'>空厨方欲炊，渍米未离䉛。<div id='poem_sentence_35_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_15654'>薪蒸湿不著，白昼须然烛。<div id='poem_sentence_36_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_15654'>污莱既已泞，买鱼不获鮛。<div id='poem_sentence_37_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_15654'>竟未成<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_15654", 15654, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>麦饘</span>，安能得粱肉。<div id='poem_sentence_38_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_15654'>更有陆先生，荒林抱穷蹙。<div id='poem_sentence_39_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_15654'>坏宅四五舍，病筱三两束。<div id='poem_sentence_40_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_15654'>盖檐低碍首，藓地滑澾足。<div id='poem_sentence_41_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_15654'>注欲透承尘，湿难庇厨簏。<div id='poem_sentence_42_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_15654'>低摧在圭窦，索漠抛偏裻。<div id='poem_sentence_43_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_15654'>手指既已胼，肌肤亦将瘯。<div id='poem_sentence_44_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_15654'>一苞势<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作庖）</span>欲陊，将撑乏寸木。<div id='poem_sentence_45_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_15654'>尽日欠束薪，经时无寸粟。<div id='poem_sentence_46_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_15654'>螔蝓将入甑，蟛蜞已临鍑<span class='inlineComment2'>（音复，说文云，如釜而口大）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_47_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_15654'>娇儿未十岁，枵然自啼哭。<div id='poem_sentence_48_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_15654'>一钱买粔籹，数里走病仆。<div id='poem_sentence_49_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_15654'>破碎旧鹤笼，狼籍晚蚕蔟。<div id='poem_sentence_50_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_15654'>千卷素书外，此外无馀蓄。<div id='poem_sentence_51_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_15654'>著处纻衣裂，戴次纱帽醭。<div id='poem_sentence_52_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_15654'>恶阴潜过午，未及烹葵菽。<div id='poem_sentence_53_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_15654'>吴中铜臭户，七万沸如臛。<div id='poem_sentence_54_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_15654'>啬止甘蟹䱬，侈唯僭车服。<div id='poem_sentence_55_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_15654'>皆希尉吏旨，尽怕里胥录。<div id='poem_sentence_56_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_15654'>低眉事庸奴，开颜纳金玉。<div id='poem_sentence_57_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_15654'>唯到陆先生，不能分一斛。<div id='poem_sentence_58_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_15654'>先生之志气，薄汉如鸿鹄。<div id='poem_sentence_59_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_15654'>遇善必擎跽，见才辄驰逐。<div id='poem_sentence_60_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_61_15654'>廉不受<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_15654", 15654, "Clauses/122/Comments/0")'>一芥</span>，其馀安可黩。<div id='poem_sentence_61_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_62_15654'>如何乡里辈，见之乃<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_15654", 15654, "Clauses/125/Comments/0")'>猬缩</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_62_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_15654'>粤予苦心者，师仰但踖踧。<div id='poem_sentence_63_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_64_15654'>受易既可注，请玄又堪卜。<div id='poem_sentence_64_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_15654'>百家皆搜荡，六艺尽翻覆。<div id='poem_sentence_65_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_66_15654'>似馁见太牢，如迷遇华烛。<div id='poem_sentence_66_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_67_15654'>半年得酬唱，一日屡往复。<div id='poem_sentence_67_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_15654'>三秀间稂莠，九成杂巴濮。<div id='poem_sentence_68_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_15654'>奔命既不暇，乞降但相续。<div id='poem_sentence_69_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_70_15654'>吟诗口吻噅，把笔指节瘃。<div id='poem_sentence_70_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_71_15654'>君才既不穷，吾道由是笃。<div id='poem_sentence_71_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_15654'>所益谅弘多，厥交过亲族。<div id='poem_sentence_72_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_73_15654'>相逢似丹漆，相望如朓肭。<div id='poem_sentence_73_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_74_15654'>论业敢并驱，量分合继躅。<div id='poem_sentence_74_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_15654'>相违始两日，忡忡想华缛。<div id='poem_sentence_75_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_76_15654'>出门泥漫漶，恨无直辕辇。<div id='poem_sentence_76_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_77_15654'>十钱赁一轮，逢上<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作篷）</span>鸣斛觫。<div id='poem_sentence_77_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_78_15654'>赤脚枕书帙，访予穿诘曲。<div id='poem_sentence_78_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_79_15654'>入门且抵掌，大噱时碌碌。<div id='poem_sentence_79_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_80_15654'>兹淋<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作滋）</span>既浃旬，无乃害九谷。<div id='poem_sentence_80_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_15654'>予惟饿不死，得非道之福。<div id='poem_sentence_81_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_82_15654'>手中捉诗卷，语快还共读。<div id='poem_sentence_82_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_83_15654'>解带似归来，脱巾若沐浴。<div id='poem_sentence_83_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_84_15654'>疏如松间篁，野甚麋对鹿。<div id='poem_sentence_84_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_85_15654'>行谭弄书签，卧话枕棋局。<div id='poem_sentence_85_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_86_15654'>呼童具盘餐，擪衣换鸡鹜。<div id='poem_sentence_86_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_15654'>或蒸一升麻，或煠两把菊。<div id='poem_sentence_87_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_88_15654'>用以阅幽奇，岂能资口腹。<div id='poem_sentence_88_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_89_15654'>十分煎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_89_15654", 15654, "Clauses/178/Comments/0")'>皋卢</span>，半榼挽醽醁。<div id='poem_sentence_89_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_90_15654'>高谈繄无尽，昼漏何太促。<div id='poem_sentence_90_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_91_15654'>我公大司谏，一切从民欲。<div id='poem_sentence_91_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_15654'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_15654", 15654, "Clauses/184/Comments/0")'>梅润</span>侵<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_15654", 15654, "Clauses/184/Comments/1")'>束杖</span>，和气生空狱。<div id='poem_sentence_92_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_93_15654'>而民当斯时，不觉有烦溽。<div id='poem_sentence_93_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_94_15654'>念涝为之灾，拜神再三告。<div id='poem_sentence_94_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_95_15654'>太阴霍然收，天地一澄肃。<div id='poem_sentence_95_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_96_15654'>燔炙既芬芬，威仪乃毣毣。<div id='poem_sentence_96_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_97_15654'>须权元化柄，用拯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_97_15654", 15654, "Clauses/195/Comments/0")'>中夏</span>酷。<div id='poem_sentence_97_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_98_15654'>我愿荐先生，左右辅司牧。<div id='poem_sentence_98_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_99_15654'>兹雨何足云，唯思举颜歜。<div id='poem_sentence_99_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_100_15654'></div><div id='poem_sentence_100_15654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_15654'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(15654)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=870')">870年</a>　皮日休与陆龟蒙唱和，并欲推荐陆龟蒙入崔璞幕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=870')">870年</a>　皮日休等奉崔璞命，祷于太湖。作品：初入太湖。<div id='poem_15603' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15603' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15603?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太湖诗<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>初入太湖<span class='inlineComment2'>（自胥口入，去州五十里。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15603")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15603_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_15603'>余顷在江汉，尝耨鹿门，渔泂湖，然而未能放形者，抑志于道也。尔后以文事造请，于是南浮至二别，涉洞庭，回观敷浅源，登庐阜，济九江，由天柱抵霍岳，又自箕颍转樊邓，陟商颜，入蓝关，凡自江汉至于京，干者十数侯，绕者二万里。道之不行者，有困辱危殆。志之可适者，有山水游玩，则休戚不孤矣。咸通九年，自京东游，复得宿太华，乐荆山，赏女几，度轘辕，穷嵩高，入京索，浮汴渠至扬州。又航天堑，从北固至姑苏。噫！江山幽绝，见贵于地志者，余之所到，不翅于半，则烟霞鱼鸟，林壑云月，可为属厌之具矣。尚枵然于志者，抑古圣人所谓独行之性乎？逸民之流乎？余真得而为也。尔后闻震泽包山，其中有灵异，学黄老徒乐之，多不返，益欲一观，豁平生之郁郁焉。十一年夏六月，会大司谏清河公忧霖雨之为患，乃择日休，将公命，祷于震泽。祀事既毕，神应如响，于是太湖之中，所谓洞庭山者，得以恣讨。凡所历皆图籍称为灵异者，遂为诗二十章，以志其事，兼寄天随子。</div><div id='poem_preface_15603_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15603'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15603'>闻有太湖名，十年未曾识。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15603'>今朝得游汎，大笑称平昔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15603'>一舍行胥塘，尽日到震泽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15603'>三万六千顷，千顷颇黎色。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15603'>连空澹无颣，照野平绝隙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15603'>好放<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_15603", 15603, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>青翰舟</span>，堪弄白玉笛。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15603'>疏岑七十二，𡾼𡾼露矛戟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15603'>悠然啸傲去，天上摇画艗。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15603'>西风乍猎猎，惊波罨涵碧。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15603'>倏忽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_15603", 15603, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>雷阵</span>吼，须臾玉崖<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作岸）</span>坼。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15603'>树动为蜃尾，山浮似鳌脊。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15603'>落照射鸿溶，清辉荡抛𢶉<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作掷）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15603'>云轻似可染，霞烂如堪摘。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15603'>渐暝无处泊，挽帆从所适。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15603'>枕下闻澎湃<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作汃）</span>，肌上生瘆𤶬。<div id='poem_sentence_14_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15603'>讨异足邅回，寻幽多阻隔。<div id='poem_sentence_15_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_15603'>愿风与良便，吹入神仙宅。<div id='poem_sentence_16_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_15603'>甘将一蕴书，永事嵩山伯。<div id='poem_sentence_17_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_15603'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_15603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_15603'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(15603)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=870')">870年</a>　皮日休等奉崔璞命，祷于太湖；祀事既毕，又游洞庭山之神景宫、林屋洞、包山精舍、毛公坛、飘渺峰、桃花坞、明月湾、练渎、投龙潭、孤园寺、上真观、销夏湾、包山祠、圣姑庙、崦裹、石板等，有诗记之，合二十首。作品：石板。晓次景神宫。崦裹。入林屋洞。雨中游包山精舍。游毛公坛。三宿神景宫。以毛公泉一瓶献上谏议因寄。缥缈峰。桃花坞。明月湾。练渎。投龙湾。孤园寺。上真观。销夏湾。包山祠。圣姑庙。太湖石。题包山。石板忆洞庭观十步韵。宿木兰后池三咏。<div id='poem_15602' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15602' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15602?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太湖诗<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二十 </span>石板<span class='inlineComment2'>（在石公山前）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15602")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15602_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15602'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15602'>翠石数百步，如板漂不流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15602'>空疑水妃意，浮出青玉洲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15602'>中若莹龙剑，外唯叠蛇矛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15602'>狂波忽然死，浩气清且浮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15602'>似将<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_15602", 15602, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>翠黛</span>色，抹破太湖秋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15602'>安得三五夕，携酒棹扁舟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15602'>召取月夫人，啸歌于上头。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15602'>又恐霄景阔，虚皇拜仙侯。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15602'>欲建九锡碑，当立十二楼。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15602'>琼文忽然下，石板谁能留。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15602'>此事少知者，唯应波上鸥。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15602'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_15602_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15609' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15609' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15609?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>晓次神景宫</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15609_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15609'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15609'>夜半幽梦中，扁舟似凫跃。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15609'>晓来到何许，俄倚包山脚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15609'>三百六十丈，攒空利如削。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15609'>遐瞻但徙倚，欲上先矍铄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15609'>浓露湿莎裳，浅泉渐草屩。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15609'>行行未一里，节境转寂寞。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15609'>静径侵泬寥，仙扉傍岩崿。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15609'>松声正清绝，海日方照灼。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15609'>歘临幽虚天，万想皆摆落。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15609'>坛灵有芝菌，殿圣无鸟雀。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15609'>琼帏自回旋，锦旌空粲错。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15609'>鼎气为龙虎，香烟混丹雘。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15609'>凝看出次云，默听语时鹤。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15609'>绿书不可注，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_15609", 15609, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>云笈</span>应无钥。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15609'>晴来鸟思喜，崦里花光弱。<div id='poem_sentence_14_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15609'>天籁如<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_15609", 15609, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>击琴</span>，泉声似摐铎。<div id='poem_sentence_15_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_15609'>清斋洞前院，敢负<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_15609", 15609, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>玄科</span>约。<div id='poem_sentence_16_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_15609'>空中悉羽章，地上皆灵药。<div id='poem_sentence_17_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_15609'>金醴可酣畅，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_15609", 15609, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>玉豉</span>堪咀嚼。<div id='poem_sentence_18_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_15609'>存心服燕胎，叩齿读龙蹻。<div id='poem_sentence_19_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_15609'>福地七十二，兹焉永堪<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作堪永）</span>托。<div id='poem_sentence_20_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_15609'>在兽乏虎䝙，于虫不毒蠚。<div id='poem_sentence_21_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_15609'>尝闻择骨录，仙志非可作。<div id='poem_sentence_22_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_15609'>绿肠既朱髓，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_15609", 15609, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>青肝</span>复紫络。<div id='poem_sentence_23_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_15609'>伊余乏此相，天与形貌恶。<div id='poem_sentence_24_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_15609'>每嗟原宪尰，常苦齐侯疟。<div id='poem_sentence_25_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_15609'>终然合委顿，刚亦慕寥廓。<div id='poem_sentence_26_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_15609'>三茅亦常<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作尝）</span>住，竟与圭组薄。<div id='poem_sentence_27_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_15609'>欲问包山神，来赊少岩壑。<div id='poem_sentence_28_15609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_15609'></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_15609_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15595' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15595' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15595?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>入林屋洞</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15595_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15595'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15595'>斋心已三日，筋骨如烟轻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15595'>腰下佩金兽，手中持<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_15595", 15595, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>火铃</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15595'>幽塘四百里，中有日月精。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15595'>连亘三十六，各各为玉京。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15595'>自非心至诚，必被神物烹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15595'>顾余慕大道，不能惜微生。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15595'>遂招放旷侣，同作幽忧行。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15595'>其门才函丈，初若盘薄硎。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15595'>洞气黑昳𥄴，苔发红鬇鬡。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15595'>试足值坎窞，低头避峥嵘。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15595'>攀缘不知倦，怪异焉敢惊。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15595'>匍匐一百步，稍稍策可横。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15595'>忽然白蝙蝠，来扑<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_15595", 15595, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>松炬</span>明。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15595'>人语散澒洞，石响高<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_15595", 15595, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>玲玎</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15595'>脚底龙蛇气，头上波涛声。<div id='poem_sentence_14_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15595'>有时若服匿，偪仄如见绷。<div id='poem_sentence_15_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_15595'>俄尔造平澹，豁然逢光晶。<div id='poem_sentence_16_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_15595'>金堂似镌出，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_15595", 15595, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>玉座</span>如琢成。<div id='poem_sentence_17_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_15595'>前有方丈沼，凝碧融人睛。<div id='poem_sentence_18_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_15595'>云浆湛不动，璚露涵而馨。<div id='poem_sentence_19_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_15595'>漱之恐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_15595", 15595, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>减算</span>，酌之必延龄。<div id='poem_sentence_20_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_15595'>愁为三官责，不敢携一罂。<div id='poem_sentence_21_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_15595'>昔云夏后氏，于此藏真经。<div id='poem_sentence_22_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_15595'>刻之以紫琳，秘之以丹琼。<div id='poem_sentence_23_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_15595'>期之以万祀，守之以百灵。<div id='poem_sentence_24_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_15595'>焉得彼丈人，窃之不加刑。<div id='poem_sentence_25_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_15595'>石匮一以出，左神俄不扃。<div id='poem_sentence_26_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_15595'>禹书既云得，吴国由是倾。<div id='poem_sentence_27_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_15595'>藓缝才半尺，中有怪物腥。<div id='poem_sentence_28_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_15595'>欲去既嚄唶，将回又伶俜。<div id='poem_sentence_29_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_15595'>却遵旧时道，半日出杳冥。<div id='poem_sentence_30_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_15595'>屦泥<span class='inlineComment2'>（去声）</span>惹石髓，衣湿沾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_15595", 15595, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>云英</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_31_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_15595'>玄箓乏仙骨，青文无绛名。<div id='poem_sentence_32_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_15595'>虽然入<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_15595", 15595, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>阴宫</span>，不得朝上清。<div id='poem_sentence_33_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_15595'>对彼神仙窟，自厌浊俗形。<div id='poem_sentence_34_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_15595'>却憎造物者，遣我骑文星。<div id='poem_sentence_35_15595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_15595'></div><div class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><div id='poem_15608' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15608' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15608?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>雨中游包山精舍</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15608_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15608'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15608'>松门亘五里，彩碧高下绚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15608'>幽人共跻攀，胜事颇清便。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15608'>翣翣林上雨，隐隐湖中电。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15608'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_15608", 15608, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>薜带</span>轻束腰，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_15608", 15608, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>荷笠</span>低遮面。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15608'>湿屦黏烟雾<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作露）</span>，穿衣落霜霰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15608'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_15608", 15608, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>笑次</span>度岩壑，困中遇台殿。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15608'>老僧三四人，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_15608", 15608, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>梵字</span>十数卷。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15608'>施稀无夏屋，境僻乏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_15608", 15608, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>朝膳</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15608'>散发抵泉流，支颐数云片。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15608'>坐石忽忘起，扪萝不知倦。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15608'>异蝶时似锦，幽禽或如钿。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15608'>篥簩还戛刃，栟榈自摇扇。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15608'>俗态既斗薮，野情空眷恋。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15608'>道人摘芝菌，为予备<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_15608", 15608, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>午馔</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15608'>渴兴<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作与）</span>石榴羹，饥惬胡麻饭。<div id='poem_sentence_14_15608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15608'>如何事于役，兹游急于传。<div id='poem_sentence_15_15608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_15608'>却将尘土衣，一任瀑丝溅。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15612'>摆履跨乱云，侧中蹲怪树。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15612'>三休且半日，始到毛公坞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15612'>两水合一涧，潨崖却为浦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15612'>相敌百千戟，共擂十万鼓。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15612'>喷散日月精，射破神仙府。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15612'>唯愁绝地脉，又恐折天柱。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15612'>一窥耳目眩，耳听云发竖。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15612'>次到鍊丹井，井干翳宿莽。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15612'>下有蕊刚丹，勺之百疾愈。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15612'>凝于白獭髓，湛似桐马乳。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15612'>黄露醒齿牙，碧黏甘肺腑。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15612'>桧异松复怪，枯疏互撑拄。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15612'>乾蛟一百丈，髐然半天舞。<div id='poem_sentence_14_15612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15612'>下有毛公坛，坛方不盈亩。<div id='poem_sentence_15_15612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_15612'>当时云龙篆，一片苔藓古<span id='poem_sentence_21_15612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_15612'>将山待夸娥，以肉投䝟貐。<div id='poem_sentence_22_15612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15598'>我来讨灵胜，到此期终焉。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15614'>带露嗅药蔓，和云寻鹿踪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15614'>时惊𪕍𪕌鼠，飞上千丈松。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15614'>翠壁内有室，叩之虚䃔<span id='poem_sentence_5_15614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15614'>遇歇有佳思，缘危无倦容。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15614'>须臾到绝顶，似鸟穿樊笼。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15614'>恐足蹈海日，疑身凌天风。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15614'>众岫点巨浸，四方接圆穹。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15614'>暴光隔云闪，髣髴亘天龙。<div id='poem_sentence_15_15614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_15614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_15614'>移时却𢷈下，细碎衡与嵩。<div id='poem_sentence_18_15614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15610' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15610?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span>桃花坞</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15610_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15610'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15610'>穷深到兹坞，逸兴转<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_15610", 15610, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>超忽</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15610'>坞名虽然在，不见桃花发。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15610'>恐是武陵溪，自闭仙日月。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15610'>闲禽啼叫窱，险狖眠硉矹。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15610'>微风吹重岚，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_15610", 15610, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>碧埃</span>轻勃勃。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15610'>清阴减鹤睡，秀色治人渴。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15610'>敲竹斗<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_15610", 15610, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>铮摐</span>，弄泉争咽嗢。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15610'>空斋蒸柏叶，野饭调石发。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15610'>空羡坞中人，终身无履袜。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15610'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_15610_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15606?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15606'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15606'>晓景澹无际，孤舟恣回环。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15606'>试问最幽处，号为明月湾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15606'>半岩翡翠巢，望见不可攀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15606'>柳弱下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_15606", 15606, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>丝网</span>，藤深垂花鬘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15606'>松瘿忽似狖，石文或如虥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15606'>钓坛两三处，苔老腥斑斑。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15606'>沙雨几处霁，水禽相向闲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15606'>野人波涛上，白屋幽深间。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15606'>晓培橘栽去，暮作鱼梁还。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15606'>清泉出<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_15606", 15606, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>石砌</span>，好树临柴关。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15606'>对此老且死，不知忧与患。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15606'>好境无处住，好处无境删。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15606'>赧然不自适，脉脉当湖山。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15606'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_15606_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15607' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15607' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15607?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span>练渎<span class='inlineComment2'>（吴王所开）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15607_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15607'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15607'>吴王厌得国，所玩终不足。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15607'>一上姑苏台，犹自嫌局促。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15607'>艅艎六宫闹，艨冲<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_3_15607'>一阵水麝风，空中荡平渌。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15607'>鸟困避锦帆，龙跧防铁轴。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15607'>流苏惹烟浪，羽葆飘岩谷。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15607'>灵境太蹂践，因兹塞林屋。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15607'>空阔嫌太湖，崎岖开练渎。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15607'>三寻齾石齿，数里穿山腹。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15607'>底静似金膏，砾碎如<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_15607", 15607, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>丹粟</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15607'>波殿郑妲醉，蟾阁西施宿。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15607'>几转含烟舟，一唱来云曲。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15607'>不知阑楯上，夜有越人镞。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15607'>君王掩面死，嫔御不敢哭。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15607'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_15607", 15607, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>艳魄</span>逐波涛，荒宫养麋鹿。<div id='poem_sentence_14_15607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15607'>国破沟亦浅，代变草空绿。<div id='poem_sentence_15_15607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_15607_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15605' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15605?labeling=true' id='poem_title_15605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15605'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15605'>艇子小且兀，缘湖荡白芷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15605'>萦纡泊一埼，宛到孤园寺。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15605'>萝岛凝清阴，松门湛虚翠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15605'>寒泉飞碧螭，古木斗苍兕。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15605'>钟梵在水魄，楼台入<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_15605", 15605, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>云肆</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15605'>岩边足鸣𧔢，树杪多飞鸓。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15605'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_15605", 15605, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>香莎</span>满院落，风汎金靃靡。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15605'>静鹤啄柏蠹，闲猱弄榅䗁。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15605'>小殿熏陆香，古经贝多纸。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15605'>老僧方瞑坐，见客还强起。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15605'>指兹正险绝，何以来到此。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15605'>先言洞壑数，次话真如理。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15605'>磬韵醒闲心，茶香凝皓齿。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15605'>巾之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_15605", 15605, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>劫贝</span>布，馔以栴檀饵。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15605'>数刻得清净，终身欲依止。<div id='poem_sentence_14_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15605'>可怜陶侍读，身列丹台位。<div id='poem_sentence_15_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_15605'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_15605", 15605, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>雅号</span>曰胜力，亦闻师佛氏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_16_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_15605'>今日到孤园，何妨称弟子。<div id='poem_sentence_17_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_15605'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_15605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_15605'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_16_15605_0'>⑴ 陶隐居尝梦见神像谓己曰：“尔当七地大王，号曰胜力也。”</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_15605_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_15597' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15597' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15597?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span id='poem_allusion_15597'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2313, "poem_allusion_15597")'>天钧</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_15597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15597'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15597'>径盘在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_15597", 15597,
