id='poem_sentence_1_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15597'>半日到上真，洞宫知造难。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15597'>双户启真景，斋心方可观。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15597'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2313, "poem_sentence_4_15597")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_15597", 15597, "Clauses/8/Comments/1")'>天钧</span></span>鸣响亮，天禄行<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_15597", 15597, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>蹒跚</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15597'>琪树夹一径，万条<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_15597", 15597, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>青琅玕</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15597'>两松峙庭际，怪状吁可叹。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15597'>大螾腾共结，修蛇飞相盘。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15597'>皮肤坼甲胄，枝节擒䝙犴。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15597'>罅处似天裂，朽中如<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_15597", 15597, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>井眢</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15597'>襹褷风声癣，跁跒地力痑<span class='inlineComment2'>（音滩）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15597'>根上露钳釱，空中狂波澜。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15597'>合时若莽苍，辟处如轘辕。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15597'>俨对<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_15597", 15597, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>无霸</span>阵，静问严陵滩。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15597'>灵飞一以护，山都焉敢干。<div id='poem_sentence_14_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15597'>两廊洁寂历，中殿高巑岏。<div id='poem_sentence_15_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_15597'>静架九色节，闲悬十绝幡。<div id='poem_sentence_16_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_15597'>微风时一吹，百宝清阑珊。<div id='poem_sentence_17_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_15597'>昔有叶道士，位当升灵官。<div id='poem_sentence_18_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_15597'>欲笺紫微志，唯食虹影丹。<div id='poem_sentence_19_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_15597'>既逐隐龙去，道风由此残。<div id='poem_sentence_20_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_15597'>犹闻绛目草，往往生空坛。<div id='poem_sentence_21_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_15597'>羽客两三人，石上谭泥丸。<div id='poem_sentence_22_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_15597'>谓我或龙胄，粲然与之欢。<div id='poem_sentence_23_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_15597'>衣巾紫华冷，食次白芝寒。<div id='poem_sentence_24_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_15597'>自觉有真气，恐随风力抟。<div id='poem_sentence_25_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_15597'>明朝若更往，必拟隳儒冠。<div id='poem_sentence_26_15597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_15597'></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_15597_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15613' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15613' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15613?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十五 </span>销夏湾</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15613_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15613'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15613'>太湖有曲处，其门为两崖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15613'>当中数十顷，别如一天池。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15613'>号为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_15613", 15613, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>销夏湾</span>，此名无所私。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15613'>赤日莫斜照，清风多遥吹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15613'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_15613", 15613, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>沙屿</span>埽粉墨，松竹调埙篪。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15613'>山果红靺鞨，水苔青髬髵。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15613'>木阴厚若瓦，严磴滑如饴。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15613'>我来此游息，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_15613", 15613, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>夏景</span>方赫曦。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15613'>一坐盘石上，肃肃寒生肌。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15613'>小艖<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>或可汎，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_15613", 15613, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>短策</span>或可支。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15613'>行惊翠羽起，坐见白莲披。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15613'>敛袖弄轻浪，解巾敌凉飔。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15613'>但有水云见，更馀沙禽知。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15613'>京洛往来客，暍死缘奔驰。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15613'>此中便可老，焉用名利为。<div id='poem_sentence_14_15613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15613'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_15613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_15613'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_15613_0'>⑴ 《方言》云：“小舸谓之艖。”</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_15613_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_15600' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15600' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15600?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十六 </span>包山祠</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15600_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15600'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15600'>白云最深处，像设盈<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_15600", 15600, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>岩堂</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15600'>村祭足茗粣，水奠多桃浆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15600'>箘䉦突古砌，薜荔绷颓墙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15600'>炉灰寂不然，风送杉桂香。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15600'>积雨晦州里，流波漂稻粱。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15600'>恭惟大司谏，悯此如发狂。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15600'>命予传明祷，祇事实不遑。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15600'>一奠若肸蚃，再祝如激扬。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15600'>出庙未半日，隔云逢澹光。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15600'>𡾼𡾼雨点少，渐收羽林枪。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15600'>忽然山家犬，起吠白日傍。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15600'>公心与神志，相向如玄黄。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15600'>我愿作一疏，奏之于穹苍。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15600'>留神千万祀，永福吴封疆。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15600'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_15600_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15601' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15601' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15601?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十七 </span>圣姑庙<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15601_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_15601_0'>① 在大姑山，晋王彪二女，相次而殁，有灵，因而庙焉。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15601'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15601'>洛神有灵逸，古庙临空渚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15601'>暴雨驳丹青，荒萝绕梁梠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15601'>野风旋芝盖，饥乌衔椒糈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15601'>寂寂落枫花，时时斗鼯鼠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15601'>常云三五夕，尽会妍神侣。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15601'>月下留紫姑，霜中召青女。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15601'>俄然响环佩，倏尔鸣机杼。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15601'>乐至有闻时，香来无定处。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15601'>目瞪如有待，魂断空无语。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15601'>云雨竟不生，留情在何处。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15601'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_15601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_15601'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(15601)'>评注</a><span id='poem_sentence_2_15599'>乃是天诡怪，信非人功夫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15599'>白丁一云取，难甚网珊瑚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15599'>厥状复若何，鬼工不可图。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15599'>或拳若虺蜴，或蹲如虎䝙。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15599'>连络若钩锁，重叠如萼跗。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15599'>或若巨人骼，或如太帝符。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15599'>膀肛<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_15599", 15599, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>筼筜笋</span>，格磔琅玕株。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15599'>断处露海眼，移来和沙须。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15599'>求之烦耄倪，载之劳舳舻。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15599'>通侯一以眄，贵却骊龙珠。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15599'>厚赐以琛赆，远去穷京都。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15599'>五侯土山下，要尔添岩龉。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15599'>赏玩若称意，爵禄行斯须。<div id='poem_15383' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15383' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15383?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宿木兰院</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span id='poem_sentence_0_15383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15383'>今夜宿来还似尔，到明无计梦云泉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15383'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_15383_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2605e165614044aebbf62ac26cb2c5e4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2605e165614044aebbf62ac26cb2c5e4");'><span id='2605e165614044aebbf62ac26cb2c5e4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=870')">870年</a>，37岁</div><div id='2605e165614044aebbf62ac26cb2c5e4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=870')">870年</a>　是年，皮陆唱和规模不断扩大。唱和友中除羊昭业、张贲等之外，尚有李縠、颜萱、司马都、郑璧、穰嵩起等，刺州史崔璞亦参与唱和，推波助澜。作品：鲁望悯臣之吉之孤，为诗序，邀予属和，欲用予道振其孤而利之。噫！承吉之困身后乎鲁望视予困与承吉生前孰若哉未有已困而能振人者。抑为之辞，用塞良友之意。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第263页。）</span>夏景冲澹偶然作二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第260页。）</span>宿报恩寺水阁。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第260页。）</span>奉和鲁望徐方平后闻赦次韵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第258页。）</span>苦雨中又作四声诗寄鲁望。新秋即事三首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第261页。）</span>临顿为吴中偏胜之地，陆鲁望居之，不出郛郭，旷若郊墅。余每访之，欸然惜去，因成五言十首，奉题屋壁。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第255页。）</span>和鲁望风人诗三首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第页。）</span>五贶诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第255页。）</span>寄昆陵魏处士璞。奉和杂题五首。<div id='poem_15512' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15512' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15512?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夏景冲澹偶然作二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><div id='poem_15402' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15402' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15402?labeling=true' target='_blank'>五贶诗<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>五泻舟</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15402")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_15402_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_15402'>毗陵处士魏君不琢，气真而志放，居毗陵凡二纪，闭门穷学。是乎，里民不得以师之；非乎，里民不得以訾之。用之不难进，利之被人也；舍之不难退，辱非及己也。噫！古君子处乎进退而全者，由此道乎。抑夷之隘，惠之不恭，不能造于是也。江南秋风时，鲈肥而难钓，菰脆而易挽，不过乘短舟符（案：《方言》曰：「船短而深者谓之舟符。」），载一甔酒，加以隐具，由五泻泾入震泽，穿松陵，抵杭越耳。日休尝闻道于不琢，敢不求雅物，成雅思乎。于是买钓船一，修二丈，阔三尺，施篷以庇烟雨，谓之五泻舟。天台杖一，色黯而力遒，谓之华顶杖，有龟头山叠石砚一，高不二寸，其仞数百，谓之太湖砚。有桐庐养和一，怪形拳跼，坐若变去，谓之乌龙养和。有南海鲎鱼壳樽一，涩锋齾角，内玄外黄，谓之诃陵樽。皆寄于不琢，行以资云水之兴，止以益琴籍之玩，真古人之雅贶也。因思乘韦之义，不过于词，遂为五篇，目之曰五贶，兼请鲁望同作。</div><div id='poem_preface_15402_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15402'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15402'>何事有青钱，因人买钓船。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15402'>阔容兼饵坐，深许共蓑眠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15402'>短好随朱鹭，轻堪倚白莲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15402'>自知无用处，却寄五湖仙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15402'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15402_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15404' "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>白芝</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15404_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15404'>量泉将濯足，阑鹤把支颐。<div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15560'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15560'>轻裁鸭绿任金刀，不怕西风断野蒿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15560'>詶赠既无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_15560", 15560, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>青玉案</span>，纤华犹欠赤霜袍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15560'>烟披怪石难同逸，竹映仙禽未胜高。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15560'>成后料君无别事，只应酣饮咏离骚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15560'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15560_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=870')">870年</a>　皮日修所蓄华亭鹤卒，诗以悼之，陆龟蒙、张贲、李縠、魏璞等诗友和诗同悼。作品：华亭鹤闻之旧矣。及来吴中，以钱半斤得一只养之，殆经岁，不幸为饮啄所误，经夕而卒。悼之不已，遂继已诗。南阳润卿博士、浙东德诗侍御、昆陵魏不琢处士、东吴陆鲁望秀才及厚于予者，悉寄之，请垂见和。<div id='poem_15417' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15417' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15417?labeling=true' target='_blank'>华亭鹤闻之旧矣及来吴中以钱半千得一只养之殆经岁不幸为饮啄所误经夕而卒悼之不已遂继以诗南阳润卿博士浙东德师侍御毗陵魏不琢处士东吴陆鲁望秀才及厚于予者悉寄之请垂见和</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15417")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_15417_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15417'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15417'>池上低摧病不行，谁教仙魄反层城。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15417_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15417'>阴苔尚有前朝迹，皎月新无昨夜声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15417_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15417'>菰米正残三日料，筠笼休碍九霄程。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15417_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15417'>不知此恨何时尽，遇著云泉即怆情。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15417_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15417'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15417_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=870')">870年</a>　皮日休致书各方故知，如有寄同年进士韦承贻、宋垂文等。作品：寄同年韦校书。江南书情二十韵，寄秘阁韦校书贻之、商洛宋先辈垂文二同年。<div id='poem_15384' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15384' id='poem_sentence_20_15570_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=870')">870年10月9日</a>　皮陆唱和，军事院霜菊盛开，皮日休有诗赠崔璞，崔璞和之，陆龟蒙共和。作品：军事院霜菊盛开，因书一绝，寄上谏议。<div id='poem_15336' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15336' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15336?labeling=true' target='_blank'>军事院霜菊盛开因书一绝寄上谏议<span class='inlineComment2'>（一本无寄字）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（870年10月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15336")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_15336_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15336'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15336'>金华千点晓霜凝，独对壶觞又不能。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15336_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15336'>已过重阳三十日，至今犹自待王弘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15336_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15336'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_15336_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=870')">870年</a>　自春徂冬，皮陆常游苏州各寺观，与僧道相往还，并有文会，皮陆与开元寺章、怀二上人相友，在寺中有联句之作；又游楞伽精舍，有诗；又与苏州北禅院寂上人、苏州重玄寺达上人等交游；又与支山南峰僧某交；与开元观顾道士交。作品：二游诗并序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第254页。）</span>追和虎丘寺清远道士诗并序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第254页。）</span>追和幽独君诗次韵二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第254页。）</span>秋晚留题鲁望郊居二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第255页。）</span>初冬章上人院。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第255页。）</span>武丘殿前有古杉一本，形状丑怪，图之不尽。况百卉竞媚，若妒若媢。唯此杉死抱奇节，髐然闯然，不知雨露之可生也，风霜之可瘁也，乃造化者方外之才乎遂赋三百言以见志。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第255页。）</span>奉和读阴符经见寄。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第255页。）</span>临顿宅将有归之日，鲁望以诗见贶，因抒怀詶之。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第256页。）</span>江南道中怀茅山广文南阳博士三首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第256页。）</span>吴中言情寄鲁望。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第256页。）</span>行次野梅。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第256页。）</span>扬州看辛夷花。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第256页。）</span>暇日独处寄鲁望。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第256页。）</span>开元寺客省早景即是。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第256页。）</span>闻开元寺开笋，因寄章上人。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>女坟湖。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>泰伯庙。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>宿木兰院。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>重题蔷薇。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>开元寺佛钵诗并序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>登初阳楼，寄怀北平郎中。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>怀华阳润卿博士三首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>鲁望以竹夹膝见寄，因次韵酬谢。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第259页。）</span>宿报恩寺水阁。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第260页。）</span>重提后池。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第260页。）</span>馆娃宫怀古五绝。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第260页。）</span>虎丘寺西小溪闲泛三绝。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第260页。）</span>寄怀南阳润卿。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第260页。）</span>友人以人参见惠，因以诗谢之。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第261页。）</span>访寂上人不遇。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第261页。）</span>秋夕文宴得遥字。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第261页。）</span>南阳广文欲于荆襄卜居，因而有赠。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第261页。）</span>寄题玉霄峰叶涵象尊师所居。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第262页。）</span>寒日书斋即事三首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第262页。）</span>题支山南峰僧。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第262页。）</span>送董少卿游茅山。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第262页。）</span>钓侣二章。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第262页。）</span>初冬偶作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第262页。）</span>醉中寄鲁望一壶并一绝。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第262页。）</span>更次来韵寄鲁望。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第262页。）</span>皋桥。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第262页。）</span>重玄寺双矮桧。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第262页。）</span>鲁望示广文先生吴门二章，情格高散，可醒俗态。因追想山中风度，次韵属和，存诗于编，鲁望之命也。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第262页。）</span>寄润卿博士。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第262页。）</span>走笔奉酬次韵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第263页。）</span>同前。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第264页。）</span>寒夜文宴，润卿有期不至。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第264页。）</span>润卿遗青饣迅饭，兼之一绝，聊用答谢。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第264页。）</span>酒病偶作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第264页。）</span>友人许惠酒，以诗征之。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第264页。）</span>杂体诗序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第264页。）</span>苦雨杂言寄鲁望。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第264页。）</span>奉和六韵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第264页。）</span>奉和晓起回文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第264页。）</span>奉和夏日四声四首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第265页。）</span>苦雨中又作四声诗寄鲁望。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第265页。）</span>奉和叠韵双声二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第265页。）</span>奉和叠韵吴宫词二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第265页。）</span>奉和杂题五首以题十五字离合。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第265页。）</span>怀锡山药名离合二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第265页。）</span>怀鹿门县名离合二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第265页。）</span>胥口即是六言二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第265页。）</span>寄题天台国清寺齐梁体。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第265页。）</span>初夏游楞伽精舍。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第266页。）</span><div id='poem_15586' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15586' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15586?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二游诗<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>徐诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（869年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15586")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15586_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_15586'>吴之士有恩王府参军徐修矩者，守世书万卷，优游自适。余假其书数千卷，未一年，悉偿夙志，酣饫经史，或日晏忘饮食。次有前泾县尉任晦者，其居有深林曲沼，危亭幽砌，余并次以见之，或退公之暇，必造以息焉。林泉隐事，恣用研咏。大凡游于二君宅，无浃旬之间，因作诗以留赠，名之曰二游（目之曰二游），兼寄陆鲁望。</div><div id='poem_preface_15586_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_15586'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2946, "poem_allusion_15586")'>坟籍</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_15586_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15586'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15586'>东莞为著姓，奕代皆隽哲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15586'>强学取科第，名声尽孤揭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15586'>自为方州来，清操称凛冽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15586'>唯写<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2946, "poem_sentence_3_15586")'>坟籍</span>多，必云清俸绝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15586'>宣毫利若风，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_15586", 15586, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>剡纸</span>光于月。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15586'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_15586", 15586, id='poem_sentence_6_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15586'>转徙入吴都，纵横碍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_15586", 15586, id='poem_sentence_8_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15586'>以此为基构，将斯用贻厥。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15586'>重于通侯印，贵却全师节。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15586'>我爱参卿道，承家能介洁。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15586'>潮田五万步，草屋十馀<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作数）</span>楶。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15586'>微宦不能去，归来坐如刖。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15586'>保兹万卷书，守慎如羁绁。<div id='poem_sentence_14_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15586'>念我曾苦心，相逢无间别。<div id='poem_sentence_15_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_15586'>引之看秘宝，任得穷披阅。<div id='poem_sentence_16_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_15586'>帙解带芸香，卷开和桂屑。<div id='poem_sentence_18_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_15586'>枕兼石锋刃，榻共松<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_15586", 15586, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>疮疖</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_19_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_15586'>一卧寂无諠，数编看尽彻。<div id='poem_sentence_20_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_15586'>或携归廨宇，或把穿林樾。<div id='poem_sentence_21_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_15586'>挈过太湖风，抱宿支硎雪。<div id='poem_sentence_22_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_15586'>如斯未星纪，悉得分毫末。<div id='poem_sentence_23_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_15586'>剪除幽僻薮，涤荡玄微窟。<div id='poem_sentence_24_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_15586'>学海正狂波，予头向中■<span class='inlineComment2'>（{殳页}）。（乌没切）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_25_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_15586'>圣人患不学，垂诫尤为切。<div id='poem_sentence_26_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_15586'>苟昧古与今，何殊瘖共𦘍<span class='inlineComment2'>（五骨切）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_27_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_15586'>昔之慕经史，有以佣笔札。<div id='poem_sentence_28_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_15586'>何况遇斯文，借之不曾辍。<div id='poem_sentence_29_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_15586'>吾衣任縠纑，吾食甘糠覈。<div id='poem_sentence_30_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_15586'>其道苟可光，斯文那自伐。<div id='poem_sentence_31_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_15586'>何竹青堪杀，何蒲重好截。<div id='poem_sentence_32_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_15586'>如能盈兼两，便足酬饥渴。<div id='poem_sentence_33_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_15586'>有此竞苟荣，闻之兼可哕。<div id='poem_sentence_34_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_15586'>东皋耨烟雨，南岭提薇蕨。<div id='poem_sentence_35_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_15586'>何以谢徐君，公车不闻设。<div id='poem_sentence_36_15586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_15586'></div><div id='poem_sentence_37_15586_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15585' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15585' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15585?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>任诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（869年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15585_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_15585'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3604, "poem_allusion_15585")'>圭窦</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_15585_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15585'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15585'>任君恣高放，斯道能寡合。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15585'>一宅闲林泉，终身远嚣杂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15585'>尝闻佐浩穰，散性多儑<span class='inlineComment2'>（五盍切）</span>𠉤<span class='inlineComment2'>（音沓，不任事貌）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15585'>歘尔解其绶，遗之如<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_15585", 15585, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>弃靸</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15585'>归来乡党内，却与亲朋洽。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15585'>开溪未让丁，列第方称甲。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15585'>入门约百步，古木声霎霎。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15585'>广槛小山欹，斜廊怪石夹。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15585'>白莲倚阑楯，翠鸟缘帘押。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15585'>地势似五泻，岩形若三峡。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15585'>猿眠但<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_15585", 15585, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>腽肭</span>，凫食时啑唼。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15585'>拨荇下文竿，结藤萦桂楫。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15585'>门留医树客，壁倚栽花锸。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_15585'>度岁止褐衣，经旬唯白帢。<div id='poem_sentence_13_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_15585'>多君方闭户，顾我能倒屧。<div id='poem_sentence_14_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_15585'>请题在茅栋，留坐于石榻。<div id='poem_sentence_15_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_15585'>魂从清景遛，衣任烟霞裛。<div id='poem_sentence_16_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_15585'>阶墀龟任上，枕席鸥方狎。<div id='poem_sentence_17_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_15585'>沼似颇黎镜，当中见鱼眨。<div id='poem_sentence_18_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_15585'>杯杓悉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_15585", 15585, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>杉瘤</span>，盘筵尽荷叶。<div id='poem_sentence_19_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_15585'>闲斟不置罚，闲弈无争劫。<div id='poem_sentence_20_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_15585'>闲日不整冠，闲风无用箑。<div id='poem_sentence_21_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_15585'>以斯为思虑，吾道宁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_15585", 15585, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>疲薾</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_22_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_15585'>衮衣竞璀璨，鼓吹争<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_15585", 15585, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>鞺鞳</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_23_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_15585'>欲者解挤排，诟者能詀讘。<div id='poem_sentence_24_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_15585'>权豪暂翻覆，刑祸相填压。<div id='poem_sentence_25_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_15585'>此时一<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3604, "poem_sentence_26_15585")'>圭窦</span>，不肯饶阊阖。<div id='poem_sentence_26_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_15585'>有第可栖息，有书可渔猎。<div id='poem_sentence_27_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_15585'>吾欲与任君，终身以斯惬。<div id='poem_sentence_28_15585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_15585'></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_15585_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15702' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15702' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15702?labeling=true' target='_blank'>追和虎丘寺清远道士诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15702")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15702_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_15702'>圣人为《春秋》，凡诸侯有告则书，无告则不书，盖所以惩其伪而敦其实也。夫怪之与神，虽曰不言，在传则书之者，亦摭其实而为之也。若然者，神之与怪果邪（神之与果有邪）？噫！圣贤有不得其志者，则必垂之于言也。大则为经诰，小则为歌咏，盖不信于当时，则取愬于后世。抑鬼神有生不得其志者，死亦然邪？若凭而宣之，则石言乎晋，物叫于宋是也；若梦而辩之，则良夫有昆吾之歌，声伯有琼瑰之谣是也。自兹已后，人伦不修，神藻益炽。在君人者，悟之则为瑞，逆之则为妖。其冥讽昧刺，时出于世者，则与骚人狎客，往往敌于忽微焉。虎丘山有清远道士诗一首，其所称自殷周而历秦汉，迄于近代，抑二千年，末以鬼神自谓，亦神怪之甚者。格之以清健，饰之以俊丽，一句一字，若奋若搏，彼建安词人傥在，不得居其右矣。颜太师鲁公爱之不暇，遂刻于岩际，并有继作。李太尉卫公，钦清远之高致，慕鲁公之素尚，又次而和之。颜之叙事也典，李之属思也丽，并一时之寡和。又幽独君诗二首，亦甚奇怆。予嗜古者，观而乐之，因继而为和答。幽独君一篇，不知孰氏之作，其词古而悲，亦存于篇末。《太玄》曰：「大无方，易无时，然后为鬼神也。」噫！清远道士果鬼神乎？抑道家者流乎？抑隐君子乎？词则已矣，人则吾不知也。</div><div id='poem_preface_15702_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15702'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15702'>成道自衰周，避世穷炎汉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15702'>荆杞虽云梗，烟霞尚容窜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15702'>兹岑信灵异，吾怀惬流玩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15702'>石涩古铁鉎，岚重轻埃漫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15702'>松膏腻幽径，蘋沫著孤岸。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15702'>诸萝幄幕暗，众鸟陶匏乱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15702'>岩罅地中心，海光天一半。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15702'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_15702", 15702, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>玄猿</span>行列归，白云次第散。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15702'>蟾蜍生夕景，沆瀣馀清旦。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15702'>风日采幽什，墨客学灵翰。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15702'>嗟予慕斯文，一咏复三叹。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15702'>显晦虽不同，兹吟粗堪赞。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15702'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_15702_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15703' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15703' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15703?labeling=true' target='_blank'>追和幽独君诗次韵<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15703")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15703_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15703'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15703'>念尔风雅魄，幽咽犹能文。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15703'>空令伤魂鸟，啼破山边坟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15703'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_15703_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15704' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15704' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15704?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15704_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15704'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15704'>恨剧但埋土，声幽难放哀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15704'>坟古春自晚，愁绪空崔嵬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15704'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_15704", 15704, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>白杨</span>老无花，枯根侵夜台。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15704'>天高有时裂，川去何时回？<div id='poem_sentence_3_15704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15704'>双睫不能濡，六藏无可摧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15704'>不闻搴蓬事，何必深悲哉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15704'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_15704_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15495' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15665'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15665'>三百八十言，出自伊祁氏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15665'>禹本刑人后，以功继其嗣。<div id='poem_sentence_12_15665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15378_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15378'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_15378_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15409' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15409' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15409?labeling=true' target='_blank'>开元寺佛钵诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15409")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_15409_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_15409'>按《释法显传》云：佛钵本在毗舍离，今在乾陀卫。竟若干百年，当复至四月支国。若干百年，至于阗国。若干百年，当至屈茨国。若干百年，当复来汉地。晋建兴二年，二圣像浮海而至沪渎，侩尼辈取之以归，今存于开元寺。后建兴八年，渔者于沪渎沙汭上获之，以为臼类，乃荤而用焉。俄有佛像见于外，渔者始为异，意沪渎二圣之遗祥也，乃以钵供之，迄今尚存。余遂观而为之咏，因寄天随子。</div><div id='poem_preface_15409_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15409'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15409'>帝青石作绿冰姿<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，曾得金人手自持。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15409'>拘律树边斋散后，提罗花下洗来时。<div "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>麦麨</span>香消大劫知。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15409'>从此共君亲顶戴，斜风应不等闲吹。<div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_15515_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15515'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15515'>传得三元䭀饭名，大宛闻说有仙卿<sup class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15382' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15382?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酒病偶作</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15382")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_15382_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15382'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15382'>郁林步障昼遮明，一炷浓香养病酲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15382_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15382'>何事晚来还欲饮，隔墙闻卖<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_15382", 15382, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>蛤蜊</span>声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15382_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15382'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_15382_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15325' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15325' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15325?labeling=true' target='_blank'>友人许惠酒以诗徵之</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15325")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_15325_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_15325'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(10947, "poem_allusion_15325")'>子山</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_15325_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15325'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15325'>野客萧然访我家，霜威白菊两三花。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15325_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15325'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(10947, "poem_sentence_1_15325")'>子山</span>病起无馀事，只望蒲台酒一车<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15325_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15325'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_15325_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_15325'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_15325_0'>⑴ 《庾信集》云：“蒲州刺史中山公许酒一车未送。”</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_15325_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_15650' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15650' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15650?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杂体诗<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>苦雨杂言寄鲁望</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15650")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15650_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_15650'>案，《舜典》：「帝曰：『夔，命汝典乐，教胄子。』」诗言志、歌永言在焉。《周礼》，太师之职，掌教六诗，讽赋既兴，风雅互作，杂体遂生焉。后系之于乐府，盖典乐之职也。在汉代李延年为协律，造新声，雅道虽缺，乐府乃盛。铙歌鼓吹，拂舞予俞，因斯而兴。词之体不得因时而易也。古乐书论之甚详，今不能备载。载其他见者，案《汉武集》：「元封三年，作柏梁台，诏群臣二千石，有能为七言诗者乃得上坐。帝曰：『日月星辰和四时。』梁王曰：『骖驾驷马从梁来。』」由是联句兴焉。孔融诗曰：「渔父屈节水，潜匿方作郡。」姓名字离合也，由是离合兴焉。晋傅咸有回文反覆诗二首云，反覆其文者，以示忧心展转也。「悠悠远迈独茕茕是也。」由是反覆兴焉。晋温峤有回文虚言诗云：「宁神静泊，损有崇亡。」由是回文兴焉。梁武帝云：「后牖有朽柳。」沈约云：「偏眠船舷边。」由是叠韵兴焉。《诗》云：「螮蝀在东。」又曰：「鸳鸯在梁。」由是双声兴焉。《诗》云：「维南有箕，不可以簸扬；维北有斗，不可以挹酒浆。」近乎戏也。古诗或为之，盖风俗之言也。古有采诗官，命之曰风人。「围棋烧败袄，看子故依然。」由是风人之作兴焉。《梁书》云：「昭明善赋短韵，吴均善压强韵。」今亦效而为之，存于编中。陆生与余，各有是为，凡八十六首。至如四声诗，三字离合，全篇双声叠韵之作，悉陆生所为，又足见其多能也。案齐竟陵王〈郡县诗〉曰：「追芳承荔浦，揖道信云丘。」县名由是兴焉。案梁元〈药名诗〉曰：「戍客恒山下，当思衣锦归。」药名由是兴焉。陆与予亦有是作。至如鲍昭之建除，沈炯之六甲、十二属，梁简文之卦名，陆惠晓之百姓，梁元帝之鸟名、龟兆，蔡黄门之口字，古〈两头纤纤〉、〈蒿砧〉、〈五杂组〉已降，非不能也，皆鄙而不为。噫，由古至律，由律至杂，诗之道尽乎此也。近代作杂体，唯刘宾客集中有回文、离合、双声、叠韵。如联句则莫若孟东野与韩文公之多。他集罕见，足知为之之难也。陆与予窃慕其为人，遂合已作，为杂体一卷，属予序杂体之始云。</div><div id='poem_preface_15650_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_15650'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(258, "poem_allusion_15650")'>太玄</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_15650_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15650'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15650'>吴中十日涔涔雨，歊蒸庳下豪家苦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15650'>可怜临顿陆先生，独自翛然守环堵。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15650'>儿饥仆病漏空厨，无人肯典破衣裾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15650'>螺蠃时时上几案，蛙黾往往跳琴书。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15650'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_15650", 15650, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>桃花米</span>斗半百钱，枯荒湿坏炊不然。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15650'>两床苮席一素几，仰卧高声吟<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(258, "poem_sentence_5_15650")'>太玄</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_15650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_15650'>知君志气如铁石，瓯冶虽神销不得。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15650'>乃知苦雨不复侵，枉费毕星无限力。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15650'>鹿门人作州从事，周章似鼠唯知醉。<div id='poem_sentence_8_15650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_15650'>府金廪粟虚请来，忆著先生便知愧。<div id='poem_sentence_9_15650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_15650'>愧多馈少真徒然，相见唯知携酒钱。<div id='poem_sentence_10_15650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_15650'>豪华满眼语不信，不如直上天公笺。<div id='poem_sentence_11_15650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_15650'>天公笺，方修次，且榜鸣篷来一醉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_15650_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15422' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15422' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15422?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>奉和鲁望晓起回文</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_15422_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15422'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15422'>孤烟晓起初原曲，碎树微分半浪中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15422'>湖后钓筒移夜雨，竹傍眠几侧晨风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15422'>图梅带润轻沾墨，画藓经蒸半失红。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15422'>无事有杯持永日，共君惟好隐墙东。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15422'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15422_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15645' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15645' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15645?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杂体诗 奉詶鲁望夏日四声四首 平声</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15645")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15645_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15645'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15645'>塘平芙蓉低，庭闲梧桐高。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15645'>清烟埋阳乌，蓝空含秋毫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_15652'>梅风脱纶帽，乳水透芒屩。<div id='poem_sentence_18_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_15652'>岚姿与波彩，不动浑相著。<div id='poem_sentence_19_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_15652'>既不暇供应，将何以酬酢。<div id='poem_sentence_20_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_15652'>却来穿竹径，似入青油幕。<div id='poem_sentence_21_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_15652'>穴恐水君开，龛如鬼工凿。<div id='poem_sentence_22_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_15652'>穷幽入兹院，前楯临巨壑。<div id='poem_sentence_23_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_15652'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_15652", 15652, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>遗画</span>龙奴狞，残香虫篆薄。<div id='poem_sentence_24_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_15652'>褫魂窥玉镜，澄虑闻金铎。<div id='poem_sentence_25_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_15652'>云态共萦留，鸟言相许诺。<div id='poem_sentence_26_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_15652'>古木势如虺，近之恐相蠚。<div id='poem_sentence_27_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_15652'>怒泉声似激，闻之意争博。<div id='poem_sentence_28_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_15652'>时禽倏已嘿，众籁萧然作。<div id='poem_sentence_29_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_15652'>遂令不羁性，恋此如缠缚。<div id='poem_sentence_30_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_15652'>念彼上人者，将生付寂寞。<div id='poem_sentence_31_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_15652'>曾无肤挠事，肯把心源度。<div id='poem_sentence_32_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_15652'>胡为儒家流，没齿勤且恪。<div id='poem_sentence_33_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_15652'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(6460, id='poem_sentence_35_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_15652'>愿力傥不遗，请作华林鹤。<div id='poem_sentence_36_15652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_15652'></div><div id='poem_sentence_37_15652_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=870')">870年</a>　皮陆唱和，隐士谢遗尘经玉泉生介绍，来访陆龟蒙，陆龟蒙有《四明山诗》九题，皮日休和之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=870')">870年</a>　皮日休又有诗寄周景复。作品：寄题镜严周禅师所居并序。<div id='poem_15536' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15536' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15536?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄题镜岩周尊师所居</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15536")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_15536_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_15536'>并句：处州仙都山，山之半有洞口，下望之如鉴，目之曰镜岩。下去地二百尺，上者以竹梯为级，中如方丈，内有乳水，滴沥嵌罅，黄老徒周君景复居焉。迨八十年，不食乎粟，日唯焚降真香一炷，读灵宝度人经而已。东牟段公柯昔为州日，闻其名，梯其室以造之，且曰：「君居此久矣，乳水之滴，昼夜可知量乎？」周君曰：「某常揣之，尽昼与夜，一斛加半焉。」公异而礼之。后柯别十二年，日休至吴，处人过，说周君尚存。吟想其道，无由以睹，因寄题是诗云。</div><div id='poem_preface_15536_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15536'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15536'>八十馀年住镜岩，鹿皮巾下雪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_15536", 15536, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>髟髟</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15536'>床寒不奈云萦枕，经润何妨雨滴函。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15536'>饮涧猿回窥绝洞，缘梯人歇倚危杉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15536'>如何计吏穷于鸟，欲望仙都举一帆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15536'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15536_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=870')">870年11月</a>　十一月底，皮日休有诗《送润卿博士还华阳》，陆龟蒙和之。<div id='poem_15502' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15502' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_2_15673'>惊羽决凝碧，伤鳞浮殷红。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15673'>堪将指杯术，授与太湖公。<div id='poem_sentence_4_15675_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1375938' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1375938' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1375938?labeling=true' target='_blank'>添渔具诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_1375938")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1375938_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1375938'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1375938'>天随子为渔具诗十五首以遗余。凡有䱷以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1375938_comment'></div>术之与器。莫不尽于是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1375938_comment'></div>噫。古之人或有溺于渔者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1375938_comment'></div>行其术而不能言。用其器而不能状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1375938_comment'></div>此与泽沮之䱷者又何异哉。如吟鲁望之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1375938_comment'></div>想其致。则江风海雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1375938_comment'></div>槭槭生齿牙间。真世外渔者之才也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1375938_comment'></div>余昔之渔所。在浻上则为庵以守之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1375938_comment'></div>居岘下则占矶以待之。江汉间时候率多雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1375938_comment'></div>唯以籉笠自庇。每伺鱼必多俯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1375938_comment'></div>籉笠不能庇其上。由是织蓬以障之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1375938_comment'></div>上抱而下仰。字之曰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1375938", 1375938, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>背蓬</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1375938_comment'></div>今观鲁望之十五篇。未有是作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1375938_comment'></div>因次而咏之。用以补其遗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1375938_comment'></div>渔家生具。获足于吾属之文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1375938_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1375938_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>陆龟蒙有《樵人十咏》，皮日休和之。作品：奉和樵人十咏并序。<div id='poem_15686' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15686' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15686?labeling=true' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_15680", 15680, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>束薪</span>白云湿，负担春日暮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15682'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15682'>蒙茏中一径，绕在千峰里。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15682'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_15682", 15682, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>歇处</span>遇松根，危中值石齿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15682'>花穿枲衣落，云拂芒鞋起。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15682'>自古行此途，不闻颠与坠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15682'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15682_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15684' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15684' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15684?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15684'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15684'>腰间插大柯，直入深溪里。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15684'>不知仗钺者，除害谁如此。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15684'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15684_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15683' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15683' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_3_15683_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15683'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15683_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15687' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15687' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15687?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span>樵歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15687_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15687'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15687'>此曲太古音，由来无管奏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15687'>多云<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_15687", 15687, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>采樵</span>乐，或说林泉候。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15687'>一唱凝闲云，再谣悲顾兽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15687'>若遇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_15687", 15687, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>采诗</span>人，诬辞收鄙陋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15687'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15687_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>陆龟蒙有《添酒中六咏》，皮日休和之。作品：酒中十咏并序。奉和酒中六咏。<div id='poem_15712' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15712' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15712?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酒中十咏<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>酒星</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15712")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15712_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_15712'>鹿门子性介而行独，于道无所全，于才无所全，于进无所全，于退无所全，岂天民之惷者邪？然进之与退，天行未觉于余也，则有穷有厄，有病有殆，果安而受邪，未若全于酒也。夫圣人之诫酒祸也大矣，在书为沈湎，在诗为童羖，在礼为豢豕，在史为狂药。余饮至酣，徒以为融肌柔神，消沮迷丧，颓然无思，以天地大顺为堤封，傲然不持，以洪荒至化为爵赏，抑无怀氏之民乎，葛天氏之民乎？苟沈而乱，狂而身，祸而族，真蚩蚩之为也。若余者，于物无所斥，于性有所适，真全于酒者也。噫！天之不全余也多矣，独以曲蘖全之，抑天犹幸于遗民焉。《太玄》曰：「君子在玄则正，在福则冲，在祸则反；小人在玄则邪，在福则骄，在祸则穷。」余之于酒得其乐，人之于酒得其祸，亦若是而已矣。于是徵其具，悉为之咏，用继东皋子酒谱之后。夫酒之始名，天有星，地有泉，人有乡，今总而咏之者，亦古人初终必全之义也。天随子深于酒道，寄而请之和。</div><div id='poem_preface_15712_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15712'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15712'>谁遣酒旗耀，天文列其位。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15712'>彩微尝似酣，芒弱偏如醉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15712'>唯忧犯帝座，只恐骑天驷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15712'>若遇卷舌星，谗君应堕地。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15712'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15712_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15713' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15713' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15713?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>酒泉</a><span id='poem_sentence_0_15659'>坚净不苦窳，陶于醉封疆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15659'>临溪刷旧痕，隔屋闻新香。<div "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>曲室</span>，倒处临糟床。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15659'>所嗟无比邻，余亦能偷尝。<div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15657'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15657'>八齐竞奔注，不知深几丈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15657'>以此献吾君，愿铭于几杖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href='/Writing/15656?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>酒龙</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15656_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15656'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15656'>铜为蚴蟉鳞，铸作鱙■<span class='inlineComment2'>（{鱼翏}）</span>角。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15656'>吐处百里雷，泻时千丈壑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15660'>尝行曲封内，稍系糟丘泊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15660_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15661' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15661' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15661?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15661'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15661'>象鼎格仍高，其中不烹饪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15661'>唯将煮浊醪，用以资酣饮。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15661'>偏宜旋樵火，稍近馀酲枕。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15661'>若得伴琴书，吾将著闲品。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15661'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15661_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>皮日修有《茶中杂咏》十首，陆龟蒙和之。作品：茶中杂咏并序。<div id='poem_15694' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15694' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15694?labeling=true' target='_blank'>茶中杂咏<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span>茶灶</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15694")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_15694_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_15694'>案《周礼》，酒正之职，辨四饮之物，其三曰浆。又浆人之职，共王之六饮，水、浆、醴、凉、医、酏，入于酒府。郑司农云：「以水和酒也，盖当时人率以酒醴为饮，谓乎六浆。酒之醨者也，何得姬公制？」《尔雅》云：「槚，苦茶，即不撷而饮之。」岂圣人纯于用乎？抑草木之济人，取舍有时也。自周已降，及于国朝茶事，竟陵子陆季疵言之详矣。然季疵以前，称茗饮者必浑以烹之，与夫瀹蔬而啜者无异也。季疵之始为经三卷，由是分其源，制其具，教其造，设其器，命其煮，俾饮之者除痟而去疠，虽疾医之不若也。其为利也，于人岂小哉！余始得季疵书，以为备矣，后又获其〈顾渚山记〉二篇，其中多茶事。后又太原温从云、武威段磶之，各补茶事十数节，并存于方册。茶之事，由周至于今，竟无纤遗矣。昔晋杜育有《荈赋》，季疵有《茶歌》，余缺然于怀者，谓有其具而不形于诗，亦季疵之馀恨也，遂为十咏，寄天随子。</div><div id='poem_preface_15694_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15694'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15694'>南山茶事动，灶起岩根傍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15694'>水煮石发气，薪然杉脂香。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15694'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_15694", 15694, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>青琼</span>蒸后凝，绿髓炊来光。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15694'>如何重辛苦，一一输膏粱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15699'>草堂暮云阴，松窗残雪明。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15699'>此时勺复茗，<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_2_15692'>庭从𣟤<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>子遮，果任獳师虏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15692'>日晚相笑归，腰间佩轻蒌。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15692'></div><div id='poem_preface_15697_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15697'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15697'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_15697", 15697, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>褎然</span>三五寸，生必依岩洞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15697'>寒恐结红铅，暖疑销紫汞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15697'>圆如玉轴光，脆似琼英冻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15697'>每为遇之疏，南山挂幽梦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15697'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15697_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15700' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15700' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15700?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>茶籯</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15700_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_15700'>案《周礼》，酒正之职，辨四饮之物，其三曰浆。又浆人之职，共王之六饮，水、浆、醴、凉、医、酏，入于酒府。郑司农云：「以水和酒也，盖当时人率以酒醴为饮，谓乎六浆。酒之醨者也，何得姬公制？」《尔雅》云：「槚，苦茶，即不撷而饮之。」岂圣人纯于用乎？抑草木之济人，取舍有时也。自周已降，及于国朝茶事，竟陵子陆季疵言之详矣。然季疵以前，称茗饮者必浑以烹之，与夫瀹蔬而啜者无异也。季疵之始为经三卷，由是分其源，制其具，教其造，设其器，命其煮，俾饮之者除痟而去疠，虽疾医之不若也。其为利也，于人岂小哉！余始得季疵书，以为备矣，后又获其〈顾渚山记〉二篇，其中多茶事。后又太原温从云、武威段磶之，各补茶事十数节，并存于方册。茶之事，由周至于今，竟无纤遗矣。昔晋杜育有《荈赋》，季疵有《茶歌》，余缺然于怀者，谓有其具而不形于诗，亦季疵之馀恨也，遂为十咏，寄天随子。</div><div id='poem_preface_15700_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15700'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15700'>筤篣晓携去，蓦个山桑坞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15700'>开时送紫茗，负处沾清露。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15700'>歇把傍云泉，归将挂烟树。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15700'>满此是生涯，黄金何足数。<div id='poem_preface_15701_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15701'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15701'>香泉一合乳，煎作连珠沸。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15701'>时看蟹目溅，乍见鱼鳞起。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15701'>声疑松带<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作带松）</span>雨，饽恐生烟翠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15701'>尚<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作倘）</span>把沥中山，必无千日醉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_15701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_15701'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_15701_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>冬夜，皮日休又与陆龟蒙、张贲等人宴集分韵赋诗，有联句之咏。作品：报恩寺南池联句。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第266页。）</span>开元寺楼看雨联句。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第265页。）</span>独在开元寺避暑，颇怀鲁望，因飞笔联句。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第266页。）</span>北禅院避暑联句。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第265页。）</span>寂上人院联句。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第265页。）</span>药名联句。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第266页。）</span>寒夜文宴联句。<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第266页。）</span>寒夜问答十首（皮日休问鲁望、陆龟蒙问袭美、皮日休问润卿、贲问袭美、陆龟蒙问润卿）<span class='inlineComment2'>（编年诗见第266页。）</span><div id='poem_15573' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15573' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15573?labeling=true' target='_blank'>独在开元寺避暑颇怀鲁望因飞笔联句</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15573")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_15573_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15573'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15573'>烦暑虽难避，僧家自有期。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15573'>泉甘于马乳，苔滑似龙漦<span class='inlineComment2'>（日休）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_15573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_15573'>任诞襟全散，临幽榻旋移。<div id='poem_sentence_2_15573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_15573'>松行将雅拜，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_15573", 15573, id='poem_sentence_4_15573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_15573'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_15573", 15573, onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_15573", 15573, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>筠簟</span>临杉穗，纱巾透<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_15573", 15573, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>雨丝</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_15573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_15573'>静谭蝉噪少，凉步鹤随迟<span class='inlineComment2'>（日休）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_15573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_15573'>烟重回<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_15573", 15573, id='poem_sentence_12_15573_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_15615' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_15615' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/15615?labeling=true' target='_blank'>北禅院避暑联句<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18853, "唐", "皮日休", "poem_title_15615")'>皮日休</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_15615_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_15615_0'>① 院昔为戴颙宅，后司勋陆郎中居之。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_15615'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_15615'>歊蒸何处避，来入戴颙宅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_15615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_15615'>逍遥脱<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_15615", 15615, 杭州

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=878&endYear=878')">878年8月</a>　八月，黄巢攻占杭州，皮日休当在杭州，此时被劫从军。皮日休被劫后，其妻室当南下会稽，依山阴滕氏。<br /><a href="javascript: -----title
武汉（江夏）

-----title
绍兴（会稽）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a276541317c648a38814113d1e88a988_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a276541317c648a38814113d1e88a988");'><span id='a276541317c648a38814113d1e88a988_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=878&endYear=878')">878年</a>，45岁</div><div id='a276541317c648a38814113d1e88a988' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=878&endYear=878')">878年5月</a>　夏五月左右，皮日休往会稽避乱，时其子光业约两岁。<br /></div>
-----end
